DL Power Control
Related definitions:
\* Pmax: Maximum output power per TRX in dBm.
\* Generally, one PA per TRX, therefore Pmax = PA power per TRX
\* Practically, NIDD setting of pMax is important, it makes sure that the applied power will NOT exceed the maximum output power allowed by the RU
\* According to HW RU module specification, the setting of pMax shall always give the value lower than maximum output power according to the number of TRXs per RU, meaning that:
\* NIDD: pMax (dBm) <= Max output power – 10log10(Num. of TRXs per RU)
\* powerBudgetPerBeam = Pmax + 10log10(Num. of TRXs per polar); //Total power per polarization or total power per TRX array or it is the power budget of all streams per polar
\* NOTE: It is defined in 5G\_UP\_698\_replaced([11352190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub1JQ_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where it can be undertood that the "Beam" denotes the "Polar Beam" for TDD case.
\* NOTE: For 5GC000920 w/o BF or mmW application, powerBudgetPerBeam = Pmax
\* powerBudgetPerStream= Pmax + 10log10(Num. of TRXs per polar) – 10log10(Num. of streams per polar); //Power per stream per polarization
An example is given in below:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a table comparing two RU modules: AEQA AirScale MAA 64T64R 128AE n78 200W and AEQN AirScale MAA 32T32R 96AE n78 80W. The table has rows for "RU Module", "Num. of TRX per RU", "Num. of Polar", "Num. of TRX per Polar", "Output power", "Pmax/Tx.Carrier.Pa.Power", "powerBudgetPerBeam", and "powerBudgetPerStream".

| RU Module | AEQA AirScale MAA 64T64R 128AE n78 200W | AEQN AirScale MAA 32T32R 96AE n78 80W |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Num. of TRX per RU | 64, two arrays (+45, -45) | 32, two arrays (+45, -45) |
| Num. of Polar | 2 | 2 |
| Num. of TRX per Polar | 32 | 16 |
| Output power | 200w (53dBm) | 80w (49dBm) |
| Pmax/Tx.Carrier.Pa.Power | 53 - 10log10(64) ~= 35 | 49 - 10log10(32) ~= 34 |
| powerBudgetPerBeam | 35 + 10log10(32) = 50 | 34 + 10log10(16) = 46 |
| powerBudgetPerStream | If there is 1 stream per polar | If there is 1 stream per polar |
|  | 35 + 10log10(32) - 10log10(1) = 50 | 34 + 10log10(16) - 10log10(1) = 46 |
|  | Elseif there is 2 streams per polar | Elseif there is 2 streams per polar |
|  | 35 + 10log10(32) - 10log10(2) = 47 | 34 + 10log10(16) - 10log10(2) = 43 |
|  | Elseif there is 8 streams per polar | Elseif there is 8 streams per polar |
|  | 35 + 10log10(32) - 10log10(8) = 41 | 34 + 10log10(16) - 10log10(8) = 37 |
|  |  |  |
| In the case of **No beamforming mode, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2183\_replaced([11112736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_907\_replaced([11353384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub-6UvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** and dlMimoMode is 4x4/4x2, a total offset of 6dB shall be applied to **powerBudgetPerBeam (see 5G\_UP\_698\_replaced([11352190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub1JQ_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**\*\*\*\* |  |  |
|  |  |  |
| In the case of the cell that not in the **energySavingState= reducedEnergySaving state (5G\_CP\_OTH\_9124\_replaced([11609773](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y472ifwOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the maximum transmitted power per component carrier is derived as legacy.** |  |  |
| In the case of the cell that is in the **energySavingState= reducedEnergySaving state, half of TX paths switched off for 4T4R or 8T8R radios, then the maximum transmitted power per component carrier shall be reduced with 3dB comparing with 'full running' antenna configuration. And maximum transmitted power per component carrier shall impact EIRP control algorithm and AvgTxPower(Average TX Power estimated for the Cell from 5GC000956) as well.** |  |  |
| If the rank before and after TX paths switched off is not changed for 4T4R or 8T8R radios, |  |  |
| Then ACTUAL\_TX\_POWER, EIRP\_SEGMENT, MAX\_EIRP\_SEGMENT, MAX\_EIRP\_SLIDING\_SEGMENT, MIN\_EIRP\_SLIDING\_SEGMENT, EIRP\_SLIDING\_SEGMENT, MAX\_CELL\_TX\_POWER\_SLIDING, MIN\_CELL\_TX\_POWER\_SLIDING, CELL\_TX\_POWER\_SLIDING shall be reduced to half in linear domain accordingly. |  |  |
| If the rank is different before and after TX paths switched off **for 4T4R or 8T8R radios, above counters may increased due to more PRB used for less rank.** |  |  |
|  |  |  |
| In the case of the cell that is in the **energySavingState= reducedEnergySaving state and NRBTS.actSSBBoostInmMIMOMuting = False, half of TX paths switched off for 64T64R radios or 32T32R radios, then the maximum transmitted power per component carrier to report ACTUAL\_TX\_POWER shall be reduced by 3dB. If NRBTS.actSSBBoostInmMIMOMuting is True, no TX paths shall be switched off and ACTUAL\_TX\_POWER shall not be reduced for the symbols with SSB when the cell is in the**energySavingState= reducedEnergySaving state.\*\*\*\* |  |  |
| **[CB015174-B]** |  |  |
| In the case of the cell that is in the MIMO muting with hopping due to RF thermal management, the maximum transmitted power per component carrier shall be reduced by 3dB comparing with 'full running' antenna configuration. |  |  |
| **[End CB015174-B]** |  |  |
| Note: |  |  |
| 1. powerBudgetPerBeam is calculated by OAM and sent to CPlane. |  |  |
| 2. For O-RAN radios connected via NetConf interface, pMax is not configured and NRCELL.dlGain is configured |  |  |
| - for BF case, powerBudgetPerBeam = dlGain + 10log10(Num. of TRXs per polar). |  |  |
| - for non-BF or mmW application, powerBudgetPerBeam = dlGain. (Only non-BF case valid for CB013571 feature scope) |  |  |

### 3.6.1.0-5 DL Power Control Power of PDCCH (ID: 11118347)

**3.6.1.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `12809172`)

DL Power Control
5G-L2-PS shall indicate the relative dBFS value of PDCCH Power to 5G-L1-DL via the parameter pdcchDciTransmitPower.

Based on the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2579\_replaced([11118670](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqEZe_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the relative dBFS value of PDCCH power shall be calculated directly as:

 pdcchDciTransmitPower = -10 \* log(N\_RB\_SC \* NRB) + pdcchPowerOffset + **pdcchPowerOffsetAdd** + staticPdcchPowerOffset\*\*\*\*

Where:

 NRB: the total number of PRBs over the carrier bandwidth. It equals to MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/dlBandwidth

 N\_RB\_SC =12: resource block size in the frequency domain (expressed as the number of subcarriers).

 pdcchPowerOffset: the extra power offset that applies to the transmit power of PDCCH under some conditions. Its default value is 0 if below conditions cannot be met：

o If (dlMimoMode = 4x4 or 4x2 Open Loop \ Closed Loop) and (actBeamforming = TRUE) and (pdcchPrecodingOption4X4 = 0 or 1), pdcchPowerOffset = -3 dB

o Note: the meaning of pdcchPrecodingOption4x4 is defined in 5G\_L2\_3723\_replaced([11182089](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Y_Q_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

o **IMPORTANT NOTE: pdcchTbTransmitPower in message DlData\_PdcchSendReq has unit in dBFs and step is 0.1dB, to remove 3dB, -30 has to be applied.**

o [Before CB007372-M] Case1 referred in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29314\_replaced([11171254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29324\_replaced([11171308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6kPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If cellBW is equal to 10MHz, 15MHz, 20MHz, On an FDD carrier shared with LTE and the PRB blanking function is also enabled (NRBTS/NRCELL/actPRBBlanking set to true), the pdcchDciTransmitPower shall be added 3db after it calculated with the “pdcchDciTransmitPower” formula above if the aggregation level  used (refactor to sync with implementation, tag will be removed after review) **for the relative PDCCH transmission is equal to 2, ie dciDedicatedAggregationLevel, dciRaMsg2AggregationLevel or dciRaCompletionAggregationLevel.**

o Case2 referred in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29314\_replaced([11171254](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuCThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29324\_replaced([11171308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6kPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **For 10 MHz and 15 MHz and 20 Mhz FDD carrier shared with LTE, when the used aggregation level of the PDCCH is configured as 2: For PDCCH in SSB slot, the pdcchDciTransmitPower shall be added 3db after it calculated with the “pdcchDciTransmitPower” formula above. Note that the aggregation level of the PDCCH shall be dciDedicatedAggregationLevel when the Al selection mode is set to static, or PDCCH used one from aggregationLevelList when the Al selection mode is set to dynamic.**

o [CB007372-M] [13415103: Conditions for PDCCH power control in symmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_QRCaYBNOEfG3gf_qmG8Vww?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End CB007372-M]

 If rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_16401\_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60, pdcchPowerOffset = 0 **dB**

 pdcchPowerOffsetAdd: the power offset from PDCCH power boosting. If PDCCH power boosting flag is marked as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29346\_replaced([11171327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuC6lPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_UP\_ALG\_29348\_replaced([11171360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuDhmPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and not Case1 and not Case2, it is 3dB, otherwise it is 0dB. Its unit is same as pdcchPowerOffset.

 staticPdcchPowerOffset: Static power offset added on the PDCCH transmit power specified by the rdStaticPdcchPowerOffset (see 5G\_L2\_3121\_replaced([11184168](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27pd8PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

### 3.6.1.1 Power of PDSCH

#### 3.6.1.1.0-1 Power of PDSCH Overview of power setting for PDSCH (ID: 11118372)

**3.6.1.1.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `13244503`)

Power of PDSCH
gNB-DU (5G-L2-PS) shall indicate the relative dBFS value of PDSCH Power to gNB-DU (5G-L1-DL) via the parameter pdschTbTransmitPower.

gNB-DU (5G-L2-PS) shall indicate the best beam power offset index to gNB-DU (5G-L1-DL) via the parameter bestBeamPowerOffset in message DlData\_PdschSendReq ([11118538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Based on the requirement ([11118670](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqEZe_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the relative dBFS value of PDSCH power shall be calculated directly as

pdschTbTransmitPower

= - 10log(N(RB,SC) \* N(RB)) – rrmQamPowerBackoff(t)

+ pdschPowerOffset + deltaPdschPower

+ pdschPowOffForVonrSrbReTxn

**- pdschRIMDLPowerReduction**

**[CB014923-C]  + pdschPwrOffsetByPwrPool**[End CB014923-C]\*\*\*\*

where,

**N(RB) is the total number of PRBs over the whole bandwidth which is defined by the maximum number of PRBs from requirement [11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ);**

**N(RB,SC) is resource block size in the frequency domain (expressed as the number of subcarriers);**

rrmQamPowerBackoff(t) is the power backoff for high modulation order, it is given by:

If 256QAM MCS table is used on PDSCH, then rrmQamPowerBackoff(t) is set to rrmQam256PowerBackoff(t) as per [11118403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11118462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ);

else If 1024QAM MCS table is used on PDSCH, then

- If modulation order is 10 (MCS=23-26, 31)  rrmQamPowerBackoff(t) is set to NRCELL/dlQam1024PowerBackoff;

- else if modulation order is 8 (MC=15-22, 30) rrmQamPowerBackoff(t) is set to NRCELL/dlQam256PowerBackoff;

- else (other MCS), rrmQamPowerBackoff(t) is set to 0;

else rrmQamPowerBackoff(t) is set to 0;

**pdschPowerOffset is the extra power offset that applies to the transmit power of PDSCH under some conditions, for example 4x4 MIMO or MU-MIMO, etc.  The** pdschPowerOffset is computed as per :\*\*\*\*

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13149\_replaced([11118478](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for 1x1 Single antenna transmission
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2565\_replaced([11118485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for 2x2 OL/CL SU MIMO
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2565\_replaced([11118485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **for 4x4 OL/CL SU MIMO**
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2567\_replaced([11118493](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLW_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for 8x4 closed loop SU MIMO
* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14413\_replaced([11118501](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for PDSCH transmission with subband BWVs ~~from MMSE method~~ to be used no matter what dlMimoMode is.

**- If {actDlSrsBm = True and dlMimoMode = 8x4 Closed Loop}** or if {actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf = True and dlMimoMode = 8x4 Closed Loop}, UEs with 8 port cell specific CSI-RS shall follow power setting **pdschPowerOffset in [11118493](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLW_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), UEs with 4 port UE specific CSI-RS shall follow power setting in [11118485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).**\*\*\*\*

* 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2570\_replaced([11118507](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLX_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for MU-MIMO where pdschPowerOffset is updated on top of SU-MIMO (references above)
* pdschPowerOffset is updated with extra power reduction. The **PowerReduction is computed as per [11118517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).**
* deltaPdschPower is the increased power for PDSCH for power balance between 2 beams. The calculation is as per [11118538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

**- pdschRIMDLPowerReduction is a reduction of the DL power due to remote interference mitigation as provided by [11118533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).**

**[CB014923-C]  - pdschPwrOffsetByPwrPool is an offset of the DL power limited by power pooling, as provided by [13244501: Calculation of PDSCH power offset caused by power pooling allocation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_fX-p4cL1EfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)**[End CB014923-C]\*\*\*\*

**pdschPowOffForVonrSrbReTxn is the extra power offset that applies to the transmit power of eligible PDSCH retransmissions. The calculation is as per [11118526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)**

**IMPORTANT NOTE: pdschTbTransmitPower has unit in dBFs and step is 0.1dB, to add/remove 3dB, +/-30 has to be applied.**

Power of PDSCH
12746916:
Power of PDSCH
12746916:
Power of PDSCH
This requirement applies to [11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

**rrmQam256PowerBackoff[t] is the power back-off, which shall be applied for the UEs in scheduling set during slot t.**

If the NIDD parameter NRBTS/NRCELL/actDynamicPowerBackoff **is set to 0 (Off), the power back-off defined by the parameter dlQam256PowerBackoff (refer to****[Before CB008475-A] MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlQam256PowerBackoffAbove6 in FR2 or MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlQam256PowerBackoffSub6 in FR1** [CB008475-A] MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlQam256PowerBackoff for FR1 or FR2 **[End CB008475-A]) shall be applied to all UEs in the cell.**\*\*\*\*

A slot specific configuration of the power back-off shall be applied to the UEs in scheduling set if the NIDD parameter NRBTS/NRCELL/actDynamicPowerBackoff **is set to 1 (On, precoding independent). For this purpose, the power back-off shall be evaluated as follows:**

1. In a first step the power back-off rrm256QamMaxPowerBackoff[t] related to **each UE in scheduling set with corresponding MCS and full allocation shall be evaluated . The MCS individual power back-off is defined by a linearly increasing function. The value of the step-up for the gradual power back-off is provided by the range between the two parameters, NRBTS/NRCELL/lowerMcsPowerBackoff and NRBTS/NRCELL/upperMcsPowerBackoff and it’s equal to dlQam256PowerBackoff / (NRBTS/NRCELL/upperMcsPowerBackoff - NRBTS/NRCELL/lowerMcsPowerBackoff + 1). The starting MCS NRBTS/NRCELL/lowerMcsPowerBackoff shall be smaller or equal than the ending MCS NRBTS/NRCELL/upperMcsPowerBackoff** and the starting MCS is the smallest MCS with a power back-off > 0. The maximum power back-off is defined by the NIDD parameter[Before CB008475-A] MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlQam256PowerBackoffAbove6 in FR2 or MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlQam256PowerBackoffSub6 in FR1 **[CB008475-A] MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlQam256PowerBackoff for FR1 or FR2** [End CB008475-A]). If NRBTS/NRCELL/upperMcsPowerBackoff **is smaller than MCS27 the maximum power back-off value shall be used for the MCSes from NRBTS/NRCELL/upperMcsPowerBackoff and up to MCS27.**   
The UE individual power back-off of 256QAM non-capable UEs is always 0 and doesn’t need to be evaluated.***\****\*

2. Next, if not disabled by rdDisable256QamPowerBackoffRescaling [11120224](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqOxiPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), the power back-off shall be scaled to the number of allocated PRBs in DL, **which are allocated to each UE considered individually in the scheduling set during slot t . The scaling of the power back-off shall be calculated by the following rule.  
  [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula defines a variable `rrmQam256PowerBackoff[t]` as the maximum of two values. The first value is `rrm256QamMaxPowerBackoff[t]`. The second value is `-10 log10` of a fraction, where the numerator is `dlChBw[PRB]` and the denominator is `allocatedPrb[t]`. This fraction is enclosed in parentheses, and the entire expression is followed by a semicolon and the number `0`. The formula is presented on a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6001.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]  
with:  
t: Time (DL slot) for that the power back-off is calculated  
dlChBw[PRB]: Number of PRB available for the channel bandwidth  
allocatedPrb[t]: Sum of allocated PRB in DL slot t**

3.   An additional step shall be performed for computation of power back-off in order to apply an offset

dependent on the correspondent rank used for UE scheduling; This scalling of power back-off

per rank shall **not be done if dlMimoMode =** 1x1 Single antenna transmission, **2x2 Open Loop or 2x2 Closed Loop.**\*\*\*\*

rrmQam256PowerBackoff[t]= rankOffset \* rrmQam256powerBackoff[t]

**IF actDlMuMimoEnh = TRUE and UE is PAIRED:**

If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = False,

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula defines "rrmEffectiveRank" as the rounded result of a fraction. The numerator of the fraction is a summation over "all paired UEs" of the product of "rankMuUe\_j" and "allocatedRbgUe\_j". The denominator is a summation over "all paired UEs" of "allocatedRbgUe\_i".
The formula is:
rrmEffectiveRank = ROUND [ Σ\_{j∈(all paired UEs)} (rankMuUe\_j \* allocatedRbgUe\_j) / Σ\_{i∈(all paired UEs)} allocatedRbgUe\_i ][/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6001.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

- [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "allocatedRbgUe,". The text is in a sans-serif font and appears to be in a dark blue or black color. The background is a light, off-white color. The text is slightly blurred, but it is still legible.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6001.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]: the number of allocated RBG for UE(j).

Else,

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula defines "rrmEffectiveRank" as the rounded result of a fraction. The numerator of the fraction is the sum of the product of "rankMuUe\_i" and "allocatedPrbUe\_i" for all paired UEs. The denominator is the sum of "allocatedPrbUe\_j" for all paired UEs.
The formula is:
rrmEffectiveRank = ROUND( Σ\_{i∈{all paired UEs}} (rankMuUe\_i \* allocatedPrbUe\_i) / Σ\_{j∈{all paired UEs}} allocatedPrbUe\_j )[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6001.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

-       [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "allocatedPrbUe,". The text is in a dark color against a light background. The font appears to be sans-serif. The text is slightly blurry.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6001.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]: the number of allocated PRBs for UE(j).

- [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "rankMuUe,". The text is blurry and appears to be in a sans-serif font. The letters are dark blue and are set against a white background. The text is positioned in the center of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6001.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]: the PDSCH rank of MU UE(j). See [11142677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5ldPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

where rankOffset is equal to:

rdMuRank4OffsetPowerBackoff (default 1.0), in rrmEffectiveRank = 4.

rdMuRank3OffsetPowerBackoff (default 0.8), in rrmEffectiveRank = 3.

rdMuRank2OffsetPowerBackoff (default 0.7), in rrmEffectiveRank = 2.

rdMuRank1OffsetPowerBackoff (default 0.2), in rrmEffectiveRank = 1.

**ELSE**

where rankOffset is equal to:

1, in case of rank 4.

rdRank3OffsetPowerBackoff, in case of rank 3.

rdRank1andRank2OffsetPowerBackoff, in case of rank 1 or rank 2.

**ENDIF**

A slot specific configuration of the power back-off shall be applied to the UEs in scheduling set when the R&D parameter NRBTS/NRCELL/actDynamicPowerBackoff is set to 2 (On, precoding dependent).

if (dlMimoMode="4x4 or 4x2 open loop spatial multiplexing" **and NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme="Dynamic**and (**'No beamforming mode'** or subsectorization mode) **and UE is rank3 or rank4), see [11112736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11353384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub-6UvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).*****\****\*

please refer to [11118462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

else

behavior is unchanged compared to NRBTS/NRCELL/actDynamicPowerBackoff **is set to 1(On, precoding independent)**

**IMPORTANT NOTE1: Only per UE backoff computation is availlable before** FGCR-9054 (cf. **PR556454 in 5G20A). Therefore same shall be applied for the FGCR-9054 until further study shows benefit of common backoff computation in case of FDM.**\*\*\*\*

**NOTE2: PR575912 handles propagation of step 3 in 5G21A, not handled by** FGCR-9054.\*\*\*\*

-  NRBTS/NRCELL/actDynamicPowerBackoff**is set to 2 (On, precoding dependent). (rdActDynamicPowerBackoff is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14277\_replaced([11120068](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqNjYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**
-  UE is scheduled with rank3 or rank4
-  dlMimoMode="4x4 or 4x2 open loop spatial multiplexing" and NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme="Dynamic" and No beamforming mode or subsectorization mode, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2183\_replaced([11112736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_907\_replaced([11353384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub-6UvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
 
For conditions above,
- rdStartMcsNoPrecodingTable64QAM is defined in 5G\_L2\_1317\_replaced([11184244](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27peAfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
- rdStartMcsNoPrecodingTable256QAM is defined in 5G\_L2\_1318\_replaced([11184247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27peA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
- dlQam256PowerBackoff refer to NIDD parameter [Before CB008475-A] MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlQam256PowerBackoffAbove6 in FR2 or MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlQam256PowerBackoffSub6 in FR1 [CB008475-A] MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlQam256PowerBackoff in FR1 or FR2 [End CB008475-A] ).
 
If NRBTS/NRCELL/upperMcsPowerBackoff<= rdStartMcsNoPrecoding **(default behavior)**
 
| | | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | Mcs< NRBTS/NRCELL/lowerMcsPowerBackoff*(default=14)* | NRBTS/NRCELL/lowerMcsPowerBackoff <= Mcs < NRBTS/NRCELL/upperMcsPowerBackoff *(default: 14<= Mcs <18)* | NRBTS/NRCELL/upperMcsPowerBackoff<=Mcs< rdStartMcsNoPrecoding *default value Table256QAM=20* *default value Table64QAM=25* | Mcs>=rdStartMcsNoPrecoding *Default value Table256QAM=20* *Default value Table64QAM=25* |
| Precoding | SCDD | SCDD | SCDD | No Precoding |
| rrmQam256MaxPowerBackoff(t) | 0 | MCS backoff follows linearly increasing function as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2560\_replaced([11118403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The value of the step-up is step-up1**.** | dlQam256PowerBackoff | ( dlQam256PowerBackoff \* 0.5) |
 
step-up1 = **dlQam256PowerBackoff / (NRBTS/NRCELL/upperMcsPowerBackoff - NRBTS/NRCELL/lowerMcsPowerBackoff + 1)**
 
If NRBTS/NRCELL/upperMcsPowerBackoff > rdStartMcsNoPrecoding
 
| | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| | Mcs< NRBTS/NRCELL/lowerMcsPowerBackoff*(default=14)* | NRBTS/NRCELL/lowerMcsPowerBackoff<= Mcs < rdStartMcsNoPrecoding | Mcs >= rdStartMcsNoPrecoding |
| Precoding | SCDD | SCDD | NoPrecoding |
| rrmQam256MaxPowerBackoff(t) | 0 | MCS backoff follows linearly increasing function as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2560\_replaced([11118403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The value of the step-up is step-up2**.** | ( dlQam256PowerBackoff \* 0.5 ) |
 
step-up2 = **( dlQam256PowerBackoff \* 0.5 ) / (rdStartMcsNoPrecoding– NRBTS/NRCELL/lowerMcsPowerBackoff+1)**
 
The rationale behind this update is the following : when NIDD parameter NRBTS/NRCELL.openLoopScheme="Dynamic", the precoding may change depending on the MCS. Therefore, when NIDD parameter dlQam256PowerBackoff is higher than 1.5:
- value from NIDD shall give the maximum backoff for SCDD and LCDD
- while value 1.5 shall be the maximum backoff for No precoding
 
Next, the power back-off shall be scaled to the number of allocated PRBs in DL, which are allocated by the UEs in scheduling set during slot t. The scaling of the power back-off shall be calculated by the following rule.
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula defines a variable `rrmQam256PowerBackoff[t]` as the maximum of two values. The first value is `rrm256QamMaxPowerBackoff[t]`. The second value is `-10 log10` of a fraction, where the numerator is `dlChBw[PRB]` and the denominator is `allocatedPrb[t]`, followed by a semicolon and the number 0. The formula is presented on two lines, with the second line containing the `max` function and its arguments.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6004.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
with:
t: Time (DL slot) for that the power back-off is calculated
dlChBw[PRB]: Number of PRB available for the channel bandwidth
allocatedPrb[t]: Sum of allocated PRB in DL slot t

#### 3.6.1.1.0-4 Power of PDSCH pdschPowerOffset for 1x1 Single antenna transmission (ID: 11118478)

**3.6.1.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11118481`)

Power of PDSCH
This requirement applies to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If (dlMimoMode = 1x1 Single antenna transmission), pdschPowerOffset = 0dB (rank1 only) ;

#### 3.6.1.1.0-5 Power of PDSCH pdschPowerOffset for 2x2 SU MIMO or 4x4 SU MIMO (ID: 11118485)

**3.6.1.1.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11118492`)

Power of PDSCH
This requirement applies to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**pdschPowerOffset value is 0 if PDSCH is not transmitted with any spatial multiplexing modes (see spatialMode in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14007\_replaced([11098058](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km7l5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

Furthermore, its value is 0 if any of below conditions cannot be met：

If (dlMimoMode = 4x4 or 4x2 Open / Close Loop) and (actBeamforming = TRUE) and below conditions are met, pdschPowerOffset = -3 dB :

- PdschPrecodingOption4X4 = 0 or 4, whatever the rank (because 2 beams are used for all ranks - no port selection)

- PdschPrecodingOption4X4 = 1 or 5, and  rank(PDSCH)>=3 ( because 2 beams are used for rank 3,4 - port selection up to rank2)

- PdschPrecodingOption4X4 = 2 or 6, and  rank(PDSCH)>=3 ( because 2 beams are used for rank 3,4 - port selection up to rank4)

**[CB013442-D] Note: If rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_16401\_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60, pdschPowerOffset = 0**dB **[End CB013442-D]**\*\*\*\*

[Before CB008577-B] [CB008577-A] or the cell has FDD beamforming enabled ([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode is CL 4x4: pdschPowerOffset = -3**dB. [End CB008577-A] [End CB008577-B]**

if(numOfSubSectors == 2 or 4), pdschPowerOffset = 0;

---

#### 3.6.1.1.0-6 Power of PDSCH pdschPowerOffset for 8x4 [CB008577-B] or 32x4 [End Cb008577-B] closed loop SU MIMO (ID: 11118493)

**3.6.1.1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `12814626`)

Power of PDSCH
This requirement applies to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If (dlMimoMode = Close Loop 8x4 **[CB008577-B] or 32x4** [End Cb008577-B] ), **pdschPowerOffset =**\*\*\*\*

For rank 4, -3dB;

For rank 3, -1.8dB;

For rank2,

if no port selection: -3dB (each UE has 4 streams, each stream, L1 does not scaling for each stream);

if port selection: 0dB

For rank1: -0dB (only 2 streams for each UE) ;

---

#### 3.6.1.1.0-7 Power of PDSCH pdschPowerOffset for subband BWVs (ID: 11118501)

**3.6.1.1.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11118504`)

Power of PDSCH
This requirement applies to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For PDSCH transmission with subband BWVs to be used, pdschPowerOffset = 0dB;

---

#### 3.6.1.1.0-8 Power of PDSCH pdschPowerOffset for MU-MIMO (ID: 11118507)

**3.6.1.1.0-8.0-4**  (ID: `13457113`)

Power of PDSCH
This requirement applies to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) on top of 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2565\_replaced([11118485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2567\_replaced([11118493](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLW_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) depending on dlMimoMode.

**[Before CB013712-A]**

**If NRCELL/actDlMuMimo = True**

Extra power reduction shall be applied to pdschPowerOffset of all co-scheduled users in current TTI. If no user can be paired in current TTI, the MU-MIMO related power reduction is not needed.

The extra reduced power is calculated with the below equation:

pdschPowerOffset = pdschPowerOffset - 10 \* LOG10(#paired\_users)

where

* the #paired\_users is the number of users in the PairSet in current TTI (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4366\_replaced([11141973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr2iIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[End CB013712-A]**

**If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True**

If NIDD:actDlMuPairingGroup = True, for SB BF UEs which are paired with SVD-RZF VUE, pdschPowerOffset is 0dB. For other cases, pdschPowerOffset = pdschPowerOffset + 10 \* LOG10(txPowerFactor), where txPowerFactor is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7434\_replaced([11145459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksA6MfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.6.1.1.0-9 Power of PDSCH powerReduction (ID: 11118517)

**3.6.1.1.0-9.0-4**  (ID: `13353365`)

Power of PDSCH
This requirement applies to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**powerReduction is the power reduction applied when used MCS is lower compared to the MCS recommended by the downlink link adaptation. The purpose is to reduce inter cell interference. Because required SINR for the MCSs are [Before PR864460] approximately 1dB separated [PR864460] separated by 0.9192dB [End PR864460], the difference of MCSindex is a measure of required SINR difference in dB [PR864460] times a factor of 0.9192 [End PR864460].**

If (initial PDSCH transmission and power reduction is applicable to the transmission according to rdEnablePowerReductionDlTestMode defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28575\_replaced([11120154](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqOKefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

powerReduction = max(min([PR864460] 0.9192\* [End PR864460] (rrmDlProposedMcs- rrmDlUsedMcs) - powerDownMargin, maxPowerReduction),0)

where:

rrmDlProposedMcs is the MCS recommended by the LA specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3045\_replaced([11125301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqt5svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

rrmDlUsedMcs is the MCS applied by the DL Scheduler after a possible MCS downgrade which determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4630\_replaced([11192270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvjWafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

powerDownMargin, with the purpose is to have reception margin for UE and to handle differences between MCS combinations. It shall be equal to the minimum between one or more of the following:

. 5dB, default value if no other feature is active in the slot

. rdPolitePowerDownMargin ([12884469](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_dvm9ALVDEfCQT7hYUxERAg)), if the used DL MCS was successfully reduced by the activated FD-POLITE widening (see [12533165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jm0A4Bw4EfCQJ5daVHVkgg))

. [PR864460] rdEirpEpicPowerDownMargin ([13353361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kUHg8u1sEfC3ocOh_n7w7A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), if the used DL MCS was successfully reduced by the activated FD-POLITE EPIC algorithm (see [12533541](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PnIScBxQEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) [End PR864460]

maxPowerReduction = [Before PR864460] 15 [PR864460] rdMaxPowerReduction (defined in [13353363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oYGTw-1sEfC3ocOh_n7w7A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) [End PR864460], Purpose is to limit the max power reduction.

Endif

If powerReduction is applied for initial PDSCH transmission, the same powerReduction shall be applied to PDSCH retransmissions as well.

---

#### 3.6.1.1.0-10 Power of PDSCH pdschPowOffForVonrSrbReTxn (ID: 11118526)

**3.6.1.1.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11118529`)

Power of PDSCH
This requirement applies to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

gNB-DU shall define the extra power offset pdschPowOffForVonrSrbReTxn applied to eligible PDSCH retransmissions (eligible transmission are defined as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25138\_replaced([11185420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvS3t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

pdschPowOffForVonrSrbReTxn = 10log10((Allocated #PRBs for PDSCH allocation + Allocated #PRBs for power boost)/ Allocated #PRBs for PDSCH allocation)

Allocated #PRBs for "PDSCH allocation" and allocated #PRBs for "power boost" are calculated as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25138\_replaced([11185420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvS3t_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.6.1.1.0-11 Power of PDSCH pdschRIMDLPowerReduction (ID: 11118533)

**3.6.1.1.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11118536`)

Power of PDSCH
This requirement applies to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

L2PS shall calculate pdschRIMDLPowerReduction as:

pdschRIMDLPowerReduction = 10\*rrmRimDLPowerReduction

where rrmRimDLPowerReduction is a reduction of the power for the specific DL transmission for the UE and cell due to RIM interference mitigation as provided by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29909\_replaced([11161178](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSsmPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine RIM DL power reduction parameters for transmission' in the RIM mitigated slots as determined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29878\_replaced([11161157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSslPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine RIM DL power reduction applicability'.

[CB012719-A-UPD001] If pdschRIMDLPowerReduction is applied for initial PDSCH transmission, the same pdschRIMDLPowerReduction shall be applied to PDSCH retransmissions as well. [End CB012719-A-UPD001]

---

11118582:
Power of PDSCH
If actDlSrsBm = true, then 2 oDFT beams based on SRS are determined for PDSCH transmission with rank>2. To balance two beams power received by UE, the transmitted power for 2 beams shall be adjusted by decreasing the stronger beam power and increase the weaker beam power.
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating changes in transmission power for different beams. It uses horizontal dashed lines to represent power levels and arrows to indicate changes.
The text in the image reads:
Increased TX power of weaker beam.
Equal TX power
Increased delta Pdsch Power
Reduced TX power of stranger beam
BestBeamPowerOffset
The diagram shows three horizontal dashed lines, representing different transmission power levels. The top dashed line is labeled "Increased TX power of weaker beam." Below this, a second dashed line is labeled "Equal TX power." An upward red arrow originates from the "Equal TX power" line and points to the "Increased TX power of weaker beam" line, with the text "Increased delta Pdsch Power" written next to it. Below the "Equal TX power" line, a third dashed line is labeled "Reduced TX power of stranger beam." A blue arrow originates from the "Equal TX power" line and points downwards to the "Reduced TX power of stranger beam" line, with the text "BestBeamPowerOffset" written next to it.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
The increased power deltaPdschPower for weaker beam and reduced power bestBeamPowerOffset for stronger beam are got according to the following steps:
Step 1. Calculating the power of 2 beams. The bigger value is marked as stronger beam power while another one is marked as weaker beam power
[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
Pstronger = abs(w'h,1 \* RSRS,h \* wh,1) \* abs(w'v,1 \* RSRS,v \* wv,1)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]
[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font on a white background. The equation is:
$P\_{\text{weaker}} = \text{abs}(w'*{h,2} \* R*{\text{SRS},h} \* w\_{h,2}) \* \text{abs}(w'*{v,2} \* R*{\text{SRS},v} \* w\_{v,2})$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]
Where
· [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w n,j" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are a mix of orange, yellow, and blue hues, with a soft glow effect. The text is positioned on a white background with a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is the horizontal DFT beam weight vector.
· [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "w\_{v,j}" which is a mathematical expression. The text is blurry and has a slight color tint.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] is the vertical DFT beam weight vector.
· [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "R\_SRS,h" in a stylized font. The text is blurry and appears to be a mathematical or scientific notation.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] is the horizontal covariance matrix.
· [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,v" in a stylized font. The letters are in a dark color, possibly black or dark blue, and appear to be slightly blurred. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6] is the vertical covariance matrix.
Step 2. Calculate the beam ratio and convert to dB.
[image-7][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is written as:
r = P\_weaker / P\_stronger
where:
\* 'r' is a variable.
\* '=' is the equals sign.
\* 'P\_weaker' is the numerator, representing a "weaker" power.
\* 'P\_stronger' is the denominator, representing a "stronger" power.
\* The fraction bar indicates division.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7]
[image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a light blue and white background. The equation is:
$r\_{dB} = 10\log(r)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8]
Step 3. [Before CB010602-A] The beam power difference is limited by rdBeamPowerOffsetThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15552\_replaced([11120100](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqNja_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If [image-9][image\_desc]r[dB] < -rdBeamPowerOff setThreshold[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9], then set: [image-10][image\_desc]The image contains text that reads "r[dB] = -rdBeamPowerOff setThreshold". The text is in a dark color against a white background. The font appears to be a sans-serif font. The text is slightly blurry, but still legible.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10]. [CB010602-A] The beam power difference is limited by NRCELL/beamPowerOffsetThreshold. If rdB[image-11][image\_desc]The image contains the text "< -beamPowerOff setThreshold". The text is in a light gray color against a white background. The font is a sans-serif font. The text appears to be a command or a variable name.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.012.png[/image\_path][/image-11], then set: [image-12][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a sans-serif font. The equation is:
$r\_{dB} = -beamPowerOffSetThreshold$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.013.png[/image\_path][/image-12]. (Note: The value of NRCELL/beamPowerOffsetThreshold is positive.) [End CB010602-A]
Step 4. Search the next larger entry than [image-13][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of text. The visible text appears to be "T" followed by "d" and then "B". There is also a superscript symbol above the "T" that is difficult to discern due to the blurriness. The colors are muted and the edges of the letters are indistinct.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.014.png[/image\_path][/image-13] in the second column ‘bestBeamPowerOffset [dB]’ in the following table [CB010602-A] for rank 4 or table for rank 3 [End CB010602-A]. For example, if [image-14][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of text. The visible text appears to be "T" followed by "d" and then "B". There is also a superscript symbol above the "T" that is difficult to discern due to the blurriness. The colors are muted and the edges of the letters are indistinct.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6025.014.png[/image\_path][/image-14]= -1.5, [CB010602-A] and rank = 4, [End CB010602-A] then bestBeamPowerOffset = -1 dB. And the corresponding deltaPdschPower = 0.4 dB.
[Before CB010602-A]

|  [CB010602-A] NRCELL/dlMimoMode = '4x4 or 4x2 Closed Loop Spatial Multiplexing' or '8x4 Closed Loop Spatial Multiplexing'; [End CB010602-A] |  |  |
|  UE is served with oDFT beams based on SRS [Before CB010602-A] and 8x4 MIMO with cell specific CSI-RS [End CB010602-A]; |  |  |
|  [CB010602-A] Port selection [PR673235] up to rank 4 [End PR673235] is enabled for UEs with UE specific CSI-RS; (Refer to 5G\_L2\_6956\_replaced([11186551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_276js_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB010602-A] |  |  |
|  PDSCH transmission with rank = 4 [CB010602-A] or rank = 3 [End CB010602-A]. |  |  |
| Otherwise, deltaPdschPower and bestBeamPowerOffset are set to 0. |  |  |

---

5G-L2-PS receives the power of SS Block (ssBlockPower) and the power offset csirsTrackingPowerControlOffsetSS  (refer 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_1917\_replaced([11269664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_To5L4PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB009510-B]from higher layer through the cell setup or cell reconfiguration [End CB009510-B]. These two parameters shall be used to calculate the power of CSI-RS (relative dBFS). The power (relative dBFS) per antenna port per sub-carrier of CSI-RS REs shall be calculated as:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6029.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

The calculated relative dBFS value shall be sent to 5G-L1-DL through the parameter csiTransmitPower.

---

#### 3.6.1.2.0-2 Power of CSI-RS Power of CSI-RS for beam refinement (ID: 11118605)

**3.6.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11118609`)

Power of CSI-RS
5G-L2-PS receives the power of SS Block (ssBlockPower) and the power offset csirsBeamMgmt.csirsBeamMgmtPowerControlOffsetSS from higher layer through the message PsCell\_CellSetupReq. These two parameters shall be used to calculate the power of CSI-RS for beam refinement (relative dBFS). The power (relative dBFS) per antenna port per sub-carrier of CSI-RS REs shall be calculated as:

csiTransmitPower = ssBlockPower + csirsBeamMgmt.powerControlOffsetSS

The calculated relative dBFS value shall be sent to 5G-L1-DL through the parameter csiTransmitPower in the message DlData\_CsiRsSendReq for triggering the transmission of CSI-RS for beam refinement.

Power of CSI-RS
11118635:
Power of CSI-RS
11118635:
Power of CSI-RS
11118635:
Power of CSI-RS
5G-L2-PS receives the power of SS Block **NRBTS.NRCELL.ssPbchBlockPower from higher layer through the message PsCell\_CellSetupReq and PsCell\_CellReconfigurationReq. This parameter shall be used to calculate the power of CSI-RS for feedback (relative dBFS). The power (relative dBFS) per antenna port per sub-carrier of CSI-RS REs shall be calculated as:**

*csiTransmitPower =* ssBlockPower + csiPowerOffset + deltaCsirsPower\*\*

If (UE is configured with UE specific 4 port CSI-RS and actBeamforming = TRUE)

csiPowerOffset = -3dB

Else

csiPowerOffset = 0

**[CB013442-D] If rdFddBfL3Call = true (refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_16401\_replaced([11329923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TtGWePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode = 40 or 60, csiPowerOffset = 0**dB **[End CB013442-D]**\*\*\*\*

[Before CB008577-B] [CB008577-A] or the cell has FDD beamforming enabled ([11111439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) & NRBTS.NRCELL.dlMimoMode is CL 4x4: csiPowerOffset = -3**dB [End CB008577-A] [End CB008577-B]**

if(numOfSubSectors == 2 or 4), csiPowerOffset = 0;

if UE is using subband beams for UE specific 4 port CSI-RS (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20728\_replaced([11112266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpULkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), **csiPowerOffset = 0;**

In case UE specific 4 port CSI-RS power balancing is enabled (actCsirsPowerBalance = TRUE) and oDFT beams based on SRS is used for UE specific CSI-RS transmission, the Tx power of two oDFT beams shall be adjusted as below: the Tx power of weaker beam is increased with deltaCsirsPower, while the Tx power of stronger beam is reduced with bestBeamPowerOffset relative to the increased Tx power of weaker beam.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating power adjustments for wireless beams. It shows three horizontal lines representing different power levels.
The top line, labeled "Increased TX power of weaker beam," is a dashed red line.
The middle line, labeled "Equal TX power," is a solid blue line.
The bottom line, labeled "Reduced TX power of stranger beam," is a dashed blue line.
An upward-pointing red arrow originates from the "Equal TX power" line and points to the "Increased TX power of weaker beam" line. This arrow is labeled "Increased delta CsirsPower" in red text.
A downward-pointing blue arrow originates from the "Equal TX power" line and points to the "Reduced TX power of stranger beam" line. This arrow is labeled "BestBeamPowerOffset" in blue text.
The diagram visually represents a scenario where the power of a weaker beam is increased, and the power of a stronger beam is reduced, relative to an equal power baseline. The "Increased delta CsirsPower" signifies the magnitude of the power increase for the weaker beam, and "BestBeamPowerOffset" indicates the magnitude of the power reduction for the stronger beam.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6036.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

If (UE is configured with UE specific CSI-RS) and (actDlSrsBm = TRUE) and (actCsirsBeamPowerBalance = TRUE) and (rdCSIRSprecoding4x4 = 0)

deltaCsirsPower is same to the value of deltaPdschPower in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13465\_replaced([11118538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) by assuming rank=4 (looking up the table for rank 4);

bestBeamPowerOffset is same to bestBeamPowerOffset in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13465\_replaced([11118538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Else

deltaCsirsPower = 0;

bestBeamPowerOffset = 0.

The calculated relative dBFS value csiTransmitPower and the best beam power offset bestBeamPowerOffset shall be sent to 5G-L1-DL for triggering the transmission of CSI-RS for feedback.

**IMPORTANT NOTE: csiTransmitPower in message DlData\_CsiRsSendReq has unit in dBFs and step is 0.1dB, to remove 3dB, -30 has to be applied.**

---

#### 3.6.1.2.0-4 Power of CSI-RS Power of CSI-RS for feedback(indicated by cplane) (ID: 11118639)

**3.6.1.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12877898`)

Power of CSI-RS
If (dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 and 8 ports CSI-RS) [CB008577-B] or (dlMimoMode is CL32x4 and 32/8 ports CSI-RS) [End CB008577-B] 5G-L2-PS receives the power of CSI-RS for feedback from higher layer through the message PsUser\_UserSetupReq or PsUser\_UserModifyReq. The power (relative dBFS) per antenna port per sub-carrier of CSI-RS REs shall be calculated as:

*csiTransmitPower*

The calculated relative dBFS value shall be sent to 5G-L1-DL through the parameter csiTransmitPower in the message DlData\_CsiRsSendReq for triggering the transmission of CSI-RS for feedback.

**IMPORTANT NOTE:**

csiTransmitPower in message DlData\_CsiRsSendReq has unit in dBFs and step is 0.1dB, to remove 3dB, -30 has to be applied.

Note for PR603989: Control plane always set message field “perCsiRsResConfig.isExtendedPrecoding” false from 20B release. Even this PR is raised at 21A.

---

#### 3.6.1.2.0-5 Power of CSI-RS Coexist of UE and cell specific CSI-RS for feedback (ID: 11118645)

**3.6.1.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11118648`)

Power of CSI-RS
If {actDlSrsBm = True and dlMimoMode = 8x4 Closed Loop} or {actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is True and dlMimoMode = 8x4 Closed Loop}, 8 port cell specific CSI-RS shall follow power setting in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2578\_replaced([11118639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqEZdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 4 port UE specific CSI-RS shall follow power setting in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2577\_replaced([11118612](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) under condition (dlMimoMode = 4x4 or 4x2 Open Loop / Closed Loop) and (actBeamforming = TRUE).

---

5G-L2-PS shall indicate the relative dBFS value of Power to 5G-L1-DL.

Based on the requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2579\_replaced([11118670](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqEZe_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the relative dBFS value of RIM RS power shall be calculated directly as

[image-0][image\_desc]`rimrsTransmitPower = -10log(NscRB x NRRBrim) + rimrsPowerOffset`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6043.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where,

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry close-up of text. The visible text appears to be "N RIM" on the top line and "RB" on the bottom line. The letters are in a sans-serif font and have a rainbow-like chromatic aberration effect, particularly around the edges. The background is black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6043.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] is the number of PRBs of one RIM RS frequency resource (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12631\_replaced([11117996](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAICPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "N^RBC\_sc". The text is blurry and has a chromatic aberration effect, with colors bleeding into each other. The "N" is large and bold, with a gradient of orange and yellow. The superscript "RBC" is smaller and appears in a reddish-brown color. The subscript "sc" is also smaller and is in a blue-green color. The overall impression is of a stylized or digitally altered text.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6043.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is resource block size in the frequency domain (expressed as the number of subcarriers);

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "rimrsPowerOffset" in a stylized font. The text is blurry and appears to be in a light color against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6043.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is the extra power offset given by NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/rsPowerOffset which is applied to the transmit power of RIM-RS

IMPORTANT NOTE: rimrsTransmitPower  in message DlData\_RimRsSendReq has unit in dBFs and step is 0.1dB, to add/remove 3dB, +/-30 has to be applied.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the concept of CPRI (Common Public Radio Interface) for Downlink (DL) MIMO (Multiple-Input Multiple-Output) with Beamforming (BF). The diagram shows a flow from a Baseband Unit (BBU) to a Radio Unit (RU).
The text elements in the diagram are:
\* **Title:** CPRI of DL MIMO with BF
\* **Left Side:**
\* "Maximum CPRI signal level for N simultaneous spatial streams"
\* "-18.2"
\* "negative value"
\* "BBU (L2RT--> DL PHY)"
\* **Right Side:**
\* "powerBudgetPerBeam"
\* "= pMax + 10 log10(NumTRXperPolar)"
\* "Relative dBFS = Channel/signal Tx Power per spatial stream - powerBudgetPerBeam"
\* "Channel/signal Tx Power per spatial stream (dBm)"
\* **Numerical Markers:**
\* "0 -"
\* "-18.2 -"
\* "- -" (two instances)
The diagram visually represents the relationship between signal levels, power budgets, and relative dBFS in a DL MIMO system with beamforming, likely indicating how signal power is managed and measured within the CPRI interface between the BBU and the RU. The BBU is shown as the source of the DL PHY data, which is then processed and transmitted by the RU. The right side of the diagram defines key parameters and calculations related to power management.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6046.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

NOTE: As defined in 5G\_UP\_698\_replaced([11352190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub1JQ_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), powerBudgetPerBeam = pMax + 10log10(NumTrxPerPolar) is defined, where it can be understood that the "Beam" denotes "Polar Beam". And it can be multiple spatial streams send per polar beam, where powerBudgetPerStream = pMax + 10log10(NumTrxPerPolar) - 10log10(NumStreamPerPolar).

So in short,

 -18.2dBFS is the digital domain corresponding of powerBudgetPerBeam (Polar Beam), which is in analog/RF/dB domain.

 Assume without tapering loss and DL\_gain of 0dB, then -18.2dBFS as RU input in DL = powerBudgetPerBeam with “pMax+10log10(NumOfTrxPerBeam)” as RU output in DL

NOTE: Generally, L1 assume -18.2 per stream for DL MIMO with beamforming case

* If there are 2 C2 with 1 C2 per polarization, then there are one stream per polarization, therefore corresponding to total of -18.2.
* If there are C4 with 2-stream per polarization (2 times -18.2), then -3dB is required to guarantee to the total output of -18.2.

DL eCPRI input IQ signal: 0dBFS maximum input per RE
 
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the concept of eCPRI (enhanced Common Public Radio Interface) for Downlink (DL) MIMO (Multiple-Input Multiple-Output) with Beamforming (BF). The diagram shows a Baseband Unit (BBU) connected to a Radio Unit (RU) via an eCPRI link.
Textual elements and their relationships are as follows:
**Title:**
eCPRI of DL
MIMO with BF
**BBU Component:**
BBU
(L2RT-- > DL L1H)
**Connection:**
eCPRI
**RU Component:**
RU
**Information related to signal levels and power budgets:**
\* **Maximum eCPRI signal level for N simultaneous spatial streams:** 0 dBFS
\* **Negative value:** This appears as a label pointing to a conceptual negative value, possibly related to signal attenuation or a specific calculation.
\* **powerBudgetPerBeam:**
= pMax + 10 log10(NumTRXperPolar)
\* **Relative dBFS = Channel/signal Tx Power per spatial stream - powerBudgetPerBeam**
\* **Channel/signal Tx Power per spatial stream (dBm)**
The diagram visually represents the flow of data and associated signal processing concepts within a wireless communication system. The BBU processes the data and sends it to the RU over eCPRI. The RU then transmits the signal. The text elements describe the maximum signal level, power budget calculations, and relative dBFS values, which are crucial for managing signal power and performance in a MIMO beamforming scenario.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6050.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
 
NOTE: For ABIO w/o BF, powerBudgetPerBeam = Pmax
 
As specified in 5G\_L3\_FLOW\_816, dlReferenceLevel is configured to 5G-L1-DL by higher layer where the dlReferenceLevel is calculated as per following:
                            dlReferenceLevel = 10*Log10(Nsc) – PowerBoostingMargin
where the Nsc is the number of subcarrier for a cell determined by cell bandwidth and numerology, PowerBoostingMargin is the maximum power offset between PDSCH and other downlink channels. PDSCH channel is baseline here because dlReferenceLevel assumes the Pmax is equally distributed to all REs for PDSCH in cell bandwidth.
As per 38.214 clauses 5.2.2.3.1 and 4.1, 38.213 clauses 4.1:
        Power offset of NZP CSI-RS RE to PDSCH RE can be 8 dB;
        Power offset of SSS RE to NZP CSI-RS RE can be 3 dB;
        Power offset of PSS RE to SSS RE can be 3 dB;
        Power offset of PDCCH DMRS RE to SSS RE can be 8 dB;
PowerBoostingMargin is setting to 19dB for 5G.
 
[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the concept of eCPRI (enhanced Common Public Radio Interface) for Downlink (DL) MIMO (Multiple-Input Multiple-Output) with Beamforming (BF). The diagram shows a flow from a Baseband Unit (BBU) to a Radio Unit (RU) via eCPRI.

It highlights the relationship between maximum eCPRI signal level, reference levels, power budgets per beam, and the relative dBFS of the channel/signal.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6050.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]
