#### 3.6.1.4.0-4 Power scaling Power Scaling for cell shutdown (ID: 11118702)

**3.6.1.4.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11118704`)

Power scaling
Upon reception of a PsCell\_DlCellShutdownReq, 5G-L2-PS shall initate gracefull cell shutdown by reducing downlink tx power of the SSB channel in several steps.

5G-L2-PS has to perform the following tasks:

5G-L2-PS shall calculate the stepduration for pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB using the 2 following parameters from MRBTS/NRBTS/shutdownStepAmount and MRBTS/NRBTS/shutdownWindow:

a. shutdownWindow(MRBTS/NRBTS/shutdownStepAmount) – time interval for stepwise output power;  
b. shutdownStepAmount(MRBTS/NRBTS/shutdownWindow) – number of steps for the Graceful Cell Shutdown;

1 stepduration = shutdownWindow/ shutdownStepAmount    (stepDuration is an integer of sec)

At each power reduction step of graceful cell shutdown, DL power of SSB is reduced by 3dB.

5G-L2-PS shall apply the downgrade by increasing pwrReductionPerSymb\_dB of DlData\_SlotTypeReq such that

pwrReductionPerSymb\_db = pwrReductionPerSymb\_db + 3 dB

For the 1st step the pwrReductionPerSymb\_db value should be set by:

pwrReductionPerSymb\_db default value + 3db

The effective transmit power of SSB will the configured channel transmit power - pwrReductionPerSymb\_db.

5G-L2-PS shall apply the pwrReductionPerSymb\_db for any OFDM symbol carrying SSB.

if the cell is muted, pwrReductionPerSymb\_db for any OFDM symbol carrying SSB is set to maximum powerreduction value.

---

### 3.6.1.5 Constraints from intra Power Pooling

#### 3.6.1.5.0-1 Constraints from intra Power Pooling overview of power pooling based DL power control (ID: 13237747)

**3.6.1.5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13388904`)

Constraints from intra Power Pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true,  [End CB015284-C]

During cell setup:

* gNB-DU shall calculate target PSD [Before CB015284-C]for DL layer PRB [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true, in term of DL layer PRB, else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true in term of DL cell PRB [End CB015284-C] [13244478: calculation of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_vs6l4cLSEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ).

at the SFN where gNB-DU cell scheduler received the power allocation results (see [13248843: Timing of intra power pooling procedure (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aJpBkcUKEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)), upon the allocated DL power for the cell by intra power pooling algorithm (see [13237755: Overview of Intra Power pooling procedure (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_POZQsL-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) gNB-DU scheduler shall perform following processing:

* gNB-DU shall calculate PDSCH transmission power offset ([13244501: Calculation of PDSCH power offset caused by power pooling allocation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_fX-p4cL1EfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)), that will be used for the calculation of PDSCH transmission power (see [11118372: Overview of power setting for PDSCH](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_U5RwUPvJEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* gNB-DU shall re-evaluate the number of usable CCEs for PDCCH (see [11214630: PDCCH Layer PRB usage and constraint (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) by using the maximum cell DL PRB capable of target PSD (see [13244480: Calculation of Maximum Cell DL PRB capable of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_bKUSQMLXEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) which considers the constraint from power pooling allocation .

---

#### 3.6.1.5.0-2 Constraints from intra Power Pooling Calculation of target PSD (ID: 13244478)

**3.6.1.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13388905`)

Constraints from intra Power Pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true, gNB-DU calculate target PSD on DL cell layer PRB (targetPsdOfLayerPrb), which is determined with RA capability and system bandwidth and used as the maximum allowed power level combined with all TRXs per DL layer PRB, as below:

targetPsdOfLayerPrb [mw / layerPrb] = 10^(0.1*pMax) \* NumOfTrx / (NDLPRB* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb )

[CB015284-C] else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true

gNB-DU calculate target PSD on DL cell PRB (targetPsdOfCellPrb), which is determined with RA capability and system bandwidth and used as the maximum allowed power level per DL cell PRB, as below:

targetPsdOfCellPrb [mw / CellPrb] = 10^(0.1\*pMax) \* NumOfTrx / (NDLPRB)

[End CB015284-C]

where,

* pMax[dBm], the maximum output power configured for the cell given by NRBTS/NRCEL/pMax .
* NumOfTrx is the number of TRXs for the cell, seen in [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb is the max number of layers per cell PRB from [11214135: Max number of layers per cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)
* NDLPRB is the number of cell DL PRB corresponding to the system cell bandwidth, from [11094258: Bandwidth Configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_yYrKYPvFEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

---

#### 3.6.1.5.0-3 Constraints from intra Power Pooling Calculation of Maximum DL PRB capable of target PSD (ID: 13244480)

**3.6.1.5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13388906`)

Constraints from intra Power Pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], at the SFN where gNB-DU cell scheduler received the power allocation results (see [13248843: Timing of intra power pooling procedure (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aJpBkcUKEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)), upon the power allocated by intra-power pooling,

[CB015284-C] If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [End CB015284-C] gNB-DU scheduler shall calculate the maximum DL layer PRB capable of targetPsdOfLayerPrb for DL transmission (maxLayerPrbCapableTargetPsd) . The calculation as below:

maxLayerPrbCapableTargetPsd = rounddown( AllocCellPwr \* NumOfTrx / targetPsdOfLayerPrb)

where

* targetPsdOfLayerPrb is the maximum power level combined with all TRXs on a DL layer PRB which is determined by system configuration, from [13244478: calculation of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_vs6l4cLSEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* NumOfTrx is the number of TRXs for the cell, seen in [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* AllocCellPwr, indicates the usable Cell DL power allocated by intra-power pooling (see[13237755: Overview of Intra Power pooling procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_POZQsL-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

[CB015284-C] else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed = true, gNB-DU scheduler shall calculate the maximum DL cell PRB capable of targetPsdOfCellPrb for DL transmission (maxCellPrbCapableTargetPsd) . The calculation as below:

maxCellPrbCapableTargetPsd= rounddown( AllocCellPwr\* NumOfTrx / targetPsdOfCellPrb )

where

* targetPsdOfCellPrb is the maximum power level combined with all TRXs on a DL Cell PRB which is determined by system configuration, from [13244478: calculation of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_vs6l4cLSEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* NumOfTrx is the number of TRXs for the cell, seen in [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* AllocCellPwr, indicates the usable Cell DL power allocated by intra-power pooling (see[13237755: Overview of Intra Power pooling procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_POZQsL-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).[End CB015284-C]

---

#### 3.6.1.5.0-4 Constraints from intra Power Pooling determination of used PDSCH PSD (usedPdschPSD) (ID: 13244482)

**3.6.1.5.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13388907`)

Constraints from intra Power Pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true, gNB-DU scheduler shall calculate the PSD on DL PRB used for PDSCH transmission (usedPdschPSD) based on the power pooling allocation result (AllocCellPwr from[13237755: Overview of Intra Power pooling procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_R33NUL-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) ) and the final used PDSCH layer PRB result ( rrmNumUsedPdschLayerPrbPerSlot ) (see [11214591: RRM Parameters](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_bXYimvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for each DL slot where the received allocated power limitation is valid (see [13248843: Timing of intra power pooling procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_c288YcUKEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)), as below calculation:

if rrmNumUsedPdschLayerPrbPerSlot ≤ maxLayerPrbCapableTargetPsd,

usedPdschPSD = targetPsdOfLayerPrb

else if rrmNumUsedPdschLayerPrbPerSlot > maxLayerPrbCapableTargetPsd

usedPdschPSD = min⁡( targetPsdOfLayerPrb , AllocCellPwr\* NumOfTrx / rrmNumUsedPdschLayerPrbPerSlot)

where

maxLayerPrbCapableTargetPsd is from [13244480: Calculation of Maximum DL layer PRB capable of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_bKUSQMLXEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

NumOfTrx is the number of TRXs for the cell, seen in [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

targetPsdOfLayerPrb is from [13244478: calculation of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_vs6l4cLSEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

[CB015284-C] else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true, gNB-DU scheduler shall calculate the PSD on DL Cell PRB used for PDSCH transmission (usedPdschPSD) based on the power pooling allocation result (AllocCellPwr ) and the sum number of allocated Cell RB for all PDSCHs in current DL slot where the received allocated power limitation is valid, as below calculation:

if Sum(Nrb) ≤ maxCellPrbCapableTargetPsd,

usedPdschPSD = targetPsdOfCellPrb

else if Sum(Nrb) > maxCellPrbCapableTargetPsd

usedPdschPSD = min⁡( targetPsdOfCellPrb, AllocCellPwr\* NumOfTrx / Sum(Nrb) )

where

maxCellPrbCapableTargetPsd is from [13244480: Calculation of Maximum DL PRB capable of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_bKUSQMLXEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

NumOfTrx is the number of TRXs for the cell, seen in [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

Sum(Nrb) is the calculated summary of Nrb (seen in [11192394: TBS computation algorithm](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_owwpYPvPEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for all PDSCHs in current DL slot.

targetPsdOfCellPrb is from [13244478: calculation of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_vs6l4cLSEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

[End CB015284-C]

---

#### 3.6.1.5.0-5 Constraints from intra Power Pooling Calculation of PDSCH power offset caused by power pooling allocation (ID: 13244501)

**3.6.1.5.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13388916`)

Constraints from intra Power Pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true[End CB015284-C], for each DL slot where the received allocated power result is valid(see [13248843: Timing of intra power pooling procedure (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aJpBkcUKEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)), gNB-DU scheduler shall calculate the power offset used in the PDSCH transmission power setting (see [11118372: Overview of power setting for PDSCH (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) based on the used PDSCH PSD:

[CB015284-C]If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [End CB015284-C]

pdschPwrOffsetByPwrPool(dB) = min⁡(0, 10\*log10⁡( usedPdschPSD / targetPsdOfLayerPrb) )

[CB015284-C] else PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true,

pdschPwrOffsetByPwrPool(dB) = min⁡(0, 10\*log10⁡( usedPdschPSD / targetPsdOfCellPrb) )

[End CB015284-C]

* where
* usedPdschPSD from [13244482: determination of used PDSCH PSD (usedPdschPSD) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3nZ2kMLaEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* targetPsdOfLayerPrb [CB015284-C] or targetPsdOfCellPrb [End CB015284-C] is from [13244478: calculation of target PSD (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_t3FsscLSEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = false [CB015284-C]and PwrPoolingFddAllowed = false [End CB015284-C], or if the cell does not belongs to any power pool, gNB-DU scheduler shall set pdschPwrOffsetByPwrPool(dB) as 0.

---

## 3.6.2 EIRP Control

### 3.6.2.0-3 EIRP Control Document Owner Deputy Alois Herzog (ID: 11118718)

### 3.6.2.1 EIRP Measurements

#### 3.6.2.1.0-1 EIRP Measurements online modification of EIRP parameters (ID: 11118723)

**3.6.2.1.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `13404911`)

EIRP Measurements
The EIRP parameters shall be updated when online modification is triggered.

The IE cellSegmentGridChange indicates whether cell segments need to be reinitialized.

In case no change is applied to the cell segment grid :  
- new normalizedBeamGain and maxBeamGain parameters shall be applied starting from next sampling period. Note that only changes relative to minSignificantNormalizedBeamGain are expected.   
   By supporting tiltOffset / leftEdgeAngle / rightEdgeAngle / upperEdgeAngle / lowerEdgeAngle/ basicBeamSet / customBeamSetName**online modification, the beam weight of SSB/refined beam and DFT/PMI beam may be online modified.       When online modification of beam weight is triggered, normalizedBeamGain is expected to be updated. For normalizedBeamGain of PMI beam, L2 shall recalculate the new normalizedBeamGain for PMI beam according to [11118827](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqGOqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).**

* upon modification of powerReductionFactor, assessment on cell segment monitoring shall be reevaluated as per [11118921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and if cell segment is already monitored, its EIRP token bucket shall be updated as per [11118994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHczvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

[CB014326-A] EIRP headroom in the corresponding cell segments shall also be reevaluated as per [13404896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ae2cAykEfGu_4itz1o3RA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End CB014326-A]

* upon modification of minGuaranteedBudgetRatioMode or minGuaranteedBudgetRatio, the L2-PS shall re-evaluate rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod defined in [11118951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and trigger an update procedure as per [11118987](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHczPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)
* **upon modification of NRCELL/eirpControl/smoothingEffect, gNB shall compute the new set of Lyapunov parameter according to [11119052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqID1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and apply them on the next measurement period**

-**upon modification of NRCELL/eirpControl/actEpic, gNB shall apply the new associated criteria for CS list addition, PRB (EPIC disabled) or MCS reduction (EPIC enabled), and computation for the number of tokens (EPIC disabled) or allowance (EPIC enabled) starting on the next measurement period**

[CB014326-B]

-**upon modification of NRCELL/eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow and/or NRCELL/eirpControlTimeAveragingWindowStepSize, gNB shall apply the new values at the begining of the next eirp measurement period (defined by the previous value of eirpControlTimeAveragingWindowStepSize if applicable). In such case, all EIRP token budgets and EIRP consumption measurements shall be reinitialized along with their respective counters.**

[End CB014326-B]

[Before CB014326-B] Note: eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow online modification is not supported. [End CB014326-B]

---

#### 3.6.2.1.1 Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power

##### 3.6.2.1.1.0-1 Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power Transmit Power per Beam (ID: 11118740)

**3.6.2.1.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11118744`)

Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power
For the purpose of EIRP measurements, the L2-PS shall derive the actual normalized transmitted power per beam for the given time slot.

The actual normalized transmitted power is derived for a transmitted channel or signal as the product of the number of scheduled REs, the number of logical antenna ports used for the transmission and the configured EPRE in dBFS (converted in linear domain), ie relative to the maximum transmitted power per logical antenna port.

---

##### 3.6.2.1.1.0-2 Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power Symbols per SS/PBCH blocks (ID: 11118748)

**3.6.2.1.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11118751`)

Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power
Each SS/PBCH block is transmitted over:

* 127 REs on symbol 0 for PSS
* 127 REs on symbol 2 for SSS
* 240 REs on symbol 1, 96 REs on symbol 2 and 240 REs on symbol 3 for PBCH and associated DMRS

EPRE of SS/PBCH block is retrieved from ssBlockPower in dBFS from CellSetup message [CB009510-B] and CellReconfiguration message. [End CB009510-B]

An offset may be applied to the SS/PBCH power transmission based on parameter pwrReductionPerSymb\_db from DlData\_SlotTypeReq.

it is assumed rdSyncSignalsTxMode always equal to 2 and included in powerBudgetPerBeam already.

---

##### 3.6.2.1.1.0-3 Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power Number of RE for CSI-RS resources (ID: 11118754)

**3.6.2.1.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11118758`)

Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power
The number of RE for CSI-RS resources depends on the antenna port configuration and the number of RB configured.

EPRE for CSI-RS for tracking is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2575\_replaced([11118592](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

EPRE for CSI-RS for beam management is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2576\_replaced([11118605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDybfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

it is assumed rdSyncSignalsTxMode always equal to 2 and included in powerBudgetPerBeam already.

EPRE for CSI-RS for channel measurement is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2577\_replaced([11118612](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.6.2.1.1.0-4 Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power Number of RE transmitted (ID: 11118761)

**3.6.2.1.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11118764`)

Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power
The number of RE transmitted for PDCCH and related DMRS is derived from the selected aggregation level ALy as nRE = y CCE x 6 RB per CCE x 12 RE per RB.

same EPRE is applied to PDCCH and related DMRS and it is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2552\_replaced([11118347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.6.2.1.1.0-5 Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power PDSCH and related DMRS (ID: 11118768)

**3.6.2.1.1.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11118778`)

Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power
The number of RE transmitted for PDSCH depends on the length of the PDSCH allocation, the number of allocated DMRS symbols and the DMRS configuration type and the presence of PTRS. The number of DMRS symbols depends on whether of single or double DMRS and the presence of additional DMRS symbols.

EPRE for PDSCH and related DMRS are defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The PTRS EPRE to PDSCH EPRE offset is given in table 4.1-2 in 38.214 §4.1 with epre-Ratio is assumed to be set to 0.

\*\*DRMS symbols are counted as PDSCH symbols

If the transmission is performed over two beams in the case of SU-MIMO 4x4 or 8x4,

[CB008322-E] - if the beams for PDSCH is sub-band short-term beams, these beams are converted to one beam per UE regardless of logical DMRS port (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22030\_replaced([11118888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1sPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

* else:  [End CB008322-E] the contribution of each beam shall be considered according to the relative number of logical antenna port configured for each beam (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6591\_replaced([11139260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krmDcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note that in the case of No beamforming mode, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2183\_replaced([11112736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_907\_replaced([11353384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub-6UvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and (dlMimoMode = 4x4 or 4x2 Open / Close Loop), the transmission is actually performed on a single beam even if a fake second best beam is added for antenna port mapping.

PDSCH EPRE in 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO or CL 8x4 MIMO shall include pdschPowerOffset as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note: DL PTRS is enabled only for TDD FR2.

---

##### 3.6.2.1.1.0-6 Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power Average transmitted power and Average normalized transmitted power (ID: 11118781)

**3.6.2.1.1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11118788`)

Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power
The average transmitted power per beam is the accumulated power over the sampling period averaged in time.

The time averaged normalized transmitted power per beam is the accumulated power over the sampling period normalized by the number of DL symbols in the sampling period (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2597\_replaced([11118792](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqFnnvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and used as an input for EIRP control.

If actDlSrsBm = false, then

The set of beams includes the SSB and the refined beams.

If dlMimoMode = "CL 8x4 MIMO" and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false, the set of beams shall be extended to the PMI beams.

Else

The set of beams includes the SSB and the refined beams.

If dlMimoMode = “OL 4x4/4x2 MIMO” or “CL 4x4/4x2 MIMO”, then

The set of beams shall be extended to the SRS based oDFT beams.

If dlMimoMode = “CL 8x4 MIMO”, then

The set of beams shall be extended to PMI beams and the SRS based oDFT beams.

[CB008322-E] If NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm is true, then

Realtime updated subband short-term beams shall be considered. [End CB008322-E]

EndIf

In case of two beams for PDSCH, the transmitted power per beam in a time slot is adjusted if bestBeamPowerOffsetIndex (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10176\_replaced([11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is not equal to 0. The transmitted power for weaker beam is equal to pdschTbTransmitPower, and the transmitted power for stronger beam is equal to pdschTbTransmitPower + bestBeamPowerOffset (here the calculation is in decibel domain).

The average transmitted power shall be reported in the PM counters ACTUAL\_TX\_POWER\_BEAM\_ for each SSB and each refined beam. The average transmitted power for the whole set of set of beams shall be reported in PM counter ACTUAL\_TX\_POWER\_CELL. The average transmitted power is multipled by the maximum transmitted power per component carrier (as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2550\_replaced([11118320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqB9PfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) converted in linear domain, and accumulated to be reported in ACTUAL\_TX\_POWER\_xxx PM counters.

Note: Given the multiplicity of PMI beams, it is left to implementation to record the normalized Tx Power per PMI beam.

Unit for ACTUAL\_TX\_POWER\_xxx PM counters is mW

Every time a sample is accumulated, EIRP\_SAMPLES PM counter shall be incremented.

---

##### 3.6.2.1.1.0-7 Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power Number of DL symbols per sampling period (ID: 11118792)

**3.6.2.1.1.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `12655871`)

Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power
In FDD, there are 14 DL symbols per slot.

In TDD, the number of DL symbols over the sampling period is derived from the tddFrameStructure from the cell configuration as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2320\_replaced([11114706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

On a FDD carrier shared with LTE [CB007372-M] when NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss is set to "false ' [End CB007372-M] , the number of DL symbols over the sampling period is derived from the current DL sharing pattern (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2304\_replaced([11171916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuIaFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). There are 12 DL symbols in every DL slot available for 5G (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2307\_replaced([12774285: DL symbols available for 5G](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_v4UUVYpNEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))).

[CB007372-M] For a FDD cell shared with LTE when NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss is set to "true' ,  there are 12 DL symbols in every DL slot available for 5G in the shared part of spectrum and 14 symbols

in every DL slot in the NR dedicated part of the spectrum [End CB007372-M]

DL symbols in DL slots reserved for LTE shall not be considered [CB007372-M] when NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss is set to "false' [End CB007372-M]

On a FDD carrier shared with LTE when the DL slot contains LTE CRS, 5G-L2-PS shall exclude the RE of the LTE CRS from the power calculations.

Note: Slots that carry msg2 are only 10 symbols long [CB007372-M] when NRCELL.actAsymmetricDss is set to "false' [End CB007372-M] . The power for those slots shall be computed on the corresponding basis.

**Note 2: For the number and the mapping of LTE CRS REs according to the number of LTE CRS ports (see  5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7622\_replaced([11325223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TsrfvvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2996\_replaced([11125095](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsrlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 36.211 §6.12 and:**

* for PDSCH LTE CRS ratematching, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_453\_replaced([11098260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km9bEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* for PDSCH LTE CRS puncturing, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_477\_replaced([11098701](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km_3V_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.6.2.1.1.0-8**  (ID: `11118798`)

Actual Normalized Transmitted Power and Average Transmitted Power
Reporting the actual transmitted power in the cell over the sliding window

At every sampling period n, the L2-PS shall determine the actual transmitted power in the cell over the configured sliding window as the average of the total actual transmitted power from the past sampling periods within the sliding window

For this purpose, the L2-PS shall store the total transmitted power in every sampling period for the duration of the sliding window in a circular buffer.

L2-PS shall report at every miNrEirp interval :

- MAX\_CELL\_TX\_POWER\_SLIDING, the maximum value over all sampling periods k within the reporting interval in segment s = x - 1

- MIN\_CELL\_TX\_POWER\_SLIDING, the minimum value over all sampling periods k within the reporting interval in segment s = x - 1

- CELL\_TX\_POWER\_SLIDING, the cumulated value over all sampling periods k within the reporting interval in segment s = x - 1

---

#### 3.6.2.1.2 Actual Normalized EIRP and Actual EIRP

##### 3.6.2.1.2.0-1 Actual Normalized EIRP and Actual EIRP Actual Normalized EIRP over the sampling period (ID: 11118804)

**3.6.2.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11118810`)

Actual Normalized EIRP and Actual EIRP
If EIRP control is active, L2-PS shall measure the actual normalized EIRP as the normalized EIRP per cell segment time averaged over the sampling period of NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControlTimeAveragingWindowStepSize.

In GoB system, the gain of the beam is independent of the time such that the EIRP per beam can be derived from the time averaged normalized power contribution of each beam over the sampling period (as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2594\_replaced([11118781](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqFnm_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) multiplied by the individual normalizedBeamGain in each cell segment.

The normalized EIRP per cell segment is approximated by the sum of the individual normalized EIRP contributions from each beam of the predefined beam set.

The set of predefefined beams includes the SSB and the refined beams. The normalizedBeamGain of each SSB and each refined beam is defined in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2046\_replaced([11277824](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpOjGfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If dlMimoMode = "CL 8x4 MIMO"  and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false, the set of predefined beams shall be extended to the PMI beams. The normalizedBeamGain for the PMI beams is computed as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2606\_replaced([11118827](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqGOqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Since normalizedBeamGain for PMI beams calculation may take several seconds, before the calculation is ready, the normalized beamGain of SSB for all UEs shall be used for EIRP monitor and control.

Note: Given the multiplicity of PMI beams, it is left to implementation to record the normalized Tx Power per PMI beam or to accumulate the normalized EIRP directly on a slot basis.

**[CB008322-E] Beside the GoB beams of the cell, if NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm is true, 5G-L2-PS shall measure the actual normalized EIRP for subband short-term beams if they are used. Before normalizedBeamGain is ready, 5G-L2-PS shall assume UE is scheduled via SSB beams for EIRP monitor.**

Note: normalizedBeamGain of subband short-term beams is updated per sampling period instead of per beam update period. **[End CB008322-E]**

---

##### 3.6.2.1.2.0-2 Actual Normalized EIRP and Actual EIRP actual EIRP computation (ID: 11118814)

**3.6.2.1.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13322259`)

Actual Normalized EIRP and Actual EIRP
The actual EIRP shall be derived from the normalized EIRP (as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2601\_replaced([11118804](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqGOovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) multiplied by the technology duty cycle and maximum steerable gain in linear domain.

The technology duty cycle is 1 in FDD and correponds to the ratio of DL symbols in TDD from the tddFrameStructure from the cell configuration as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2320\_replaced([11114706](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

On an FDD carrier shared with LTE [CB007372-M] and with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-M], the technology duty cycle is the ratio of DL symbols available for 5G in the current DL sharing pattern (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2304\_replaced([11171916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuIaFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). There are 12 DL symbols in every DL slot available for 5G (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2307\_replaced([12774285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_v4UUVYpNEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))). DL symbols in DL slots reserved for LTE shall not be considered.

**[CB007372-M] On an FDD carrier shared with LTE and with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true, the technology duty cycle is 1. There are 14 DL symbols in every DL slot available for 5G (see [12774285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_v4UUVYpNEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). [End CB007372-M]**

On a FDD carrier shared with LTE when the DL slot contains LTE CRS, 5G-L2-PS shall exclude the RE of the LTE CRS from the power calculations.

Note: Slots that carry msg2 are only 10 symbols long [CB007372-M] when NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-M]. The power for those slots shall be computed on the corresponding basis.

Note 2: For the number and the mapping of LTE CRS REs according to the number of LTE CRS ports (see  5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7622\_replaced([11325223](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TsrfvvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2996\_replaced([11125095](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsrlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 36.211 §6.12 and:

* for PDSCH LTE CRS ratematching, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_453\_replaced([11098260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km9bEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* for PDSCH LTE CRS puncturing, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_477\_replaced([11098701](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km_3V_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The maximum steerable gain, or maxBeamGain, is defined in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2046\_replaced([11277824](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpOjGfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The actual EIRP shall be accumulated in linear domain and reported in PM counter ACTUAL\_EIRP\_.

The maximum actual EIRP per cell segment over one sampling period is reported in PM counter MAX\_ACTUAL\_EIRP\_.

Unit of ACTUAL\_EIRP\_ and MAX\_ACTUAL\_EIRP\_ is **mW**

Note: Segment 0 is reserved for the back of the antenna for future use.

---

##### 3.6.2.1.2.0-3 Actual Normalized EIRP and Actual EIRP Reporting the actual EIRP headroom over the sliding window (ID: 13404896)

**3.6.2.1.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13404898`)

Actual Normalized EIRP and Actual EIRP
For each cell segment s, the gNB-DU shall compute the actual EIRP threshold as follows:

rrmActEirpThreshold(s) = Ptx\* Ftdc \* G\_MLB \* FPR(s)

Where:

* Ptx is the transmit power per beam as defined in [1111874](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqFAjvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kqfajvvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")
* Ftdc is the technology duty cycle as defined in [11118814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqGOpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kqgopfvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9") ignoring DSS specific updates of the duty cycle
* G\_MLB is the maximum steerable gain in linear domain in linear form
* FPR(s) is the Power Reduction Factor configured for the current segment as provided in NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControlPowerReductionFactorList and then converted to linear form

Then, at every sampling period n, the gNB-DU shall determine the actual EIRP headroom per cell segment s over the configured sliding window as:

rrmActEirpHeadroom(s) = rrmActEirpThreshold(s) / rrmMaxActualEirp(s,n)

Where:

* rrmActEirpThreshold(s) is the max actual EIRP in the segment for the current measurement period as per [11118814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqGOpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kqgopfvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")
* rrmMaxActualEirp(s,n) is the Max actual EIRP as computed in [11118814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqGOpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kqgopfvsee-aqvopbp1qhq?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9")

---

##### 3.6.2.1.2.0-4 Actual Normalized EIRP and Actual EIRP Reporting the actual normalized EIRP over the sliding window (ID: 11118822)

**3.6.2.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11118823`)

Actual Normalized EIRP and Actual EIRP
At every sampling period n, the L2-PS shall determine the actual normalized EIRP per cell segment over the configured sliding window as the average of the normalized EIRP from the past sampling periods within the sliding window :

rrmNormalizedEirpSliding(s,n) = sum ( rrmNormalizedEirp(s,i) ) / W with i = [n-W+1 .. n]

where :

- n is the current sliding window

- i is the index of the sampling period within the sliding window

- W is the number of sampling periods in the sliding window, ie eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow/eirpControlTimeAverageWindowStepSize

- rrmNormalizedEirp(s,i) is the rrmNormalizedEirp in segment s during sampling period i

L2-PS shall convert rrmNormalizedEirpSliding into actual EIRP as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13214\_replaced([11118814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqGOpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and report at every miNrEirp interval :

- MAX\_EIRP\_SLIDING\_SEGMENT\_x, the maximum value over all sampling periods k within the reporting interval in segment s = x - 1

- MIN\_EIRP\_SLIDING\_SEGMENT\_x, the minimum value over all sampling periods k within the reporting interval in segment s = x - 1

- EIRP\_SLIDING\_SEGMENT\_x, the cumulated value over all sampling periods k within the reporting interval in segment s = x - 1

---

)) for this UE as below: [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in dark blue text on a white background. The formula is: BeamGain(b, s) = $\frac{1}{2 N} \sum_{n} |\sum_{m} Coef_{m,n} * S_{m,s}|^2$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_6099.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] where b is subband BF UE index, m is DFT beam index, s is segment index, Sm,s is the DFT beam response on segment s which is sent from L3; n is short-term beam index which has range of 1~8 depending on number of BWVs per subband from L1. [End PRxx] where maxBeamGain is from CPRT and if it is in dB, it shall be converted to linear value. Convert beamGain in dB, which is expressed by beamGain_dB, if beamGain_dB (b,s) &lt; eirpControlPowerReductionFactorList_dB(s) + minSignificantNormalizedBeamGain_dB, normalizedBeamGain(b,s) shall be forced to 0). *** Note: minSignificantNormalizedBeamGain is the default value of NIDD:minSignificantNormalizedBeamGain. (ID: 12749475)

#### 3.6.2.1.3-2 Normalized beamforming gain calculation for PMI beams

**3.6.2.1.3-2.0-2**  (ID: `11118910`)

Normalized beamforming gain calculation for PMI beams
Whenever NRCELL.actSuperCell is enabled, each virtual SSB beam used in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1925\_replaced([11111622](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpPTAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be considered as a beam for the purpose of EIRP measurements and control. In such case, the number of beams in EIRP related algorithms shall be equal to the number of subcells in the supercell: NRCELL.numOfSuperSubcells.

[CB009543-C1]

In the case of a FDD supercell, virtual SSB beams should be defined for the purpose of EIRP measurements and control in a similar fashion as in TDD following 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1925\_replaced([11111622](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpPTAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): Each subcell should be associated to a single virtual SSB beam and a single segment. When performing EIRP measurements, it is expected in the FDD case that the emission in all segments should be proportional as the DL channels are duplicated. The proportionality factor should depend on both NRCELL.pMax and NRCELL.eirpControlPowerReductionFactorList and only the segment with the most challenging set of parameters need to be considered for the purpose of EIRP control.

[End CB009543-C1]

Furthermore, the number of segments defined shall be equal to NRCELL.numOfSuperSubcells and the normarlizedBeamGain parameter received at cell setup or updated according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2586\_replaced([11118720](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqFAiPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall have a size equal to the NRCELL.numOfSuperSubcells \* numberCellSegments.

---

##### 3.6.2.1.3.0-4 Normalized beamforming gain calculation for PMI beams Calculate the beamforming gain for each PMI beam (ID: 11118860)

**3.6.2.1.3.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12749804`)

Normalized beamforming gain calculation for PMI beams
12749804:

12749804:
Normalized beamforming gain calculation for PMI beams

Normalized beamforming gain calculation for PMI beams
12749804:
Normalized beamforming gain calculation for PMI beams
L2-PS shall calculate the beam gain for each PMI beam with algorithm below:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in black text on a white background. The formula is: BeamGain(b, s) = |Pb,s|² / (TRX number). The text is clear and legible.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6096.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

- [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Pb,s" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient of orange, yellow, and blue, with a slight glow effect. The background is white, and the text is framed by a thick black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6096.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]: the PMI beam response in segment S, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2609\_replaced([11118856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqGOrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

- [image-2][image\_desc]BeamGain (b, s)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6096.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]: the PMI beam gain in segment S;

If (MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMimoMode = 70) and (NRBTS/actNr​L​B​mMimoR​T​X​Power​Saving is true), both legacy and power saving beamset for PMI (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2514\_replaced([11293281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqDCfvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and corresponding DFT beam (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2058\_replaced([11277968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpPKMPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be generated by CPRT. TRX number shall be equal to**half for power saving beamset BeamGain calculation.**

Covert the BeamGain into normlaizedBeamGain with algorithm below:

normalizedBeamGain(b,s) = BeamGain(b,s)/(maxBeamGain)

[PRxx] Note: normalizedBeamGain(b,s) has maximum value 1 from the 1st release that introduce this function.

[End PRxx]

where **maxBeamGain is from CPRT and if it is in dB, it shall be converted to linear value.**

---

### 3.6.2.2 EIRP budget

#### 3.6.2.2.1 Determination of cell segments to monitor

##### 3.6.2.2.1.0-1 Determination of cell segments to monitor Determination of normalized EIRP budget (ID: 11118921)

**3.6.2.2.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11118928`)

Determination of cell segments to monitor
L2-PS shall determine for each segment the normalized EIRP budget of each beam with a non null normalized gain in the segment as :

rrmNormalizedEirpBudget (b,s) = powerReductionFactor\_lin(s) / normalizedBeamGain(b,s)

where

* normalizedBeamGain is configured for each beam b and cell segment s by CP-RT for SSB, refined beams, SRS based oDFT beams, SRS based oDFT beams with tapering. For PMI beams, it is computed according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2606\_replaced([11118827](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqGOqfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [CB008322-E] For subband beams, it is computed according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22030\_replaced([11118888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1sPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008322-E]
* powerReductionFactor\_lin is the linear value of powerReductionFactor configured in MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControlPowerReductionFactorList for each cell segment s

A beam with null gain in a segment can be considered as having the highest budget in the segment.

If actDlSrsBm = false, then

{

The set of beams includes the SSB and the refined beams.

If dlMimoMode = "CL 8x4 MIMO"  and actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false, the set of beams shall be extended to the PMI beams.

Note: Given the multiplicity of PMI beams, it is left to implementation to record the normalized EIRP budget per PMI beam.

}

Else

{

1) The set of predefined beams includes the SSB and the refined beams.

2) If dlMimoMode = “OL 4x4/4x2 MIMO” or “CL 4x4/4x2 MIMO”, the set of predefined beams shall be extended to SRS based oDFT beams.

3) If dlMimoMode = "CL 8x4 MIMO", the set of predefined beams shall be extended to the PMI beams and SRS based oDFT beams.

4) If NIDD NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True and DL tapering is enabled (see NIDD parameters of dlMuMimoTaperingH and dlMuMimoTaperingV), the set of beams includes SRS based oDFT beams with tapering as well.

[CB008322-E] 5) If NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm is true, subband beams which are updated at runtime shall be included. Note: due to high processing load, normalizedBeamGain(b,s) is updated per sampling period which may be longer than subband beam update period. [End CB008322-E]

}

---

##### 3.6.2.2.1.0-2 Determination of cell segments to monitor The beams and segments over which it shall be monitoring EIRP (ID: 11118932)

**3.6.2.2.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11118939`)

Determination of cell segments to monitor
For each beam, L2-PS shall determine the segments over which it shall be monitoring EIRP, if any.

A beam with a null gain in a segment is assumed not to be significantly contributing to the EIRP of the segment. It can be excluded from the EIRP control of this segment.

The segments to monitor EIRP are the ones with rrmNormalizedEirpBudget smaller than 1, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8084\_replaced([11118921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The L2-PS shall maintain a list of all segments to monitor.

For each segment to monitor, rrmMaxTokenRateConsumption is defined as the inverse of the smallest rrmNormalizedEirpBudget. [CB008322-E] subband beams which are not GoB beams shall not be included in rrmMaxTokenRateConsumption determination. Rationale: subband beams are updated at real time and here assume their gain can be represented by oDFT SRS beams. [End CB008322-E]

Note that rrmNormalizedEirpBudget is not expected to be null as powerReductionFactor is a negative value in dB.

---

#### 3.6.2.2.2 Cell segments token buckets

##### 3.6.2.2.2.0-1 Cell segments token buckets EIRP budget and EIRP token definition (ID: 11118946)

**3.6.2.2.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11118948`)

Cell segments token buckets
The EIRP budget over one cell segment is represented by a number of tokens where one normalized EIRP token represents the maximum power that can be used to transmit over one OFDM symbol with the maximum number of layers in SU-MIMO and maximum beam gain such that the normalized EIRP budget is respected.

The EIRP budget is split in two parts :

-    The first part is the minimum available power in any sampling period (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2618\_replaced([11118951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s)

- The second part can be flexibly used by the DL scheduler over the sliding window and forms the EIRP bucket (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2620\_replaced([11118968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize(s)

Every cell segment has the same number of tokens available over the time average sliding window equal to:

rrmEirpBudget = eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow \* rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod

where :

* eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow is configured in MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow and converted in number of sampling periods
* rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod is the number of available DL OFDM symbols in a sampling period derived from the technology duty cycle as per (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13214\_replaced([11118814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqGOpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) multiplied by the maximum MU-MIMO order

Over one sampling period, the maximum number of consumed tokens for a given cell segment is equal to:

rrmMaxEirpConsumedTokensPerPeriod(s) = rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod \* rrmMaxTokenRateConsumption(s)

where rrmMaxTokenRateConsumption(s) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2614\_replaced([11118932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1u_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 3.6.2.2.2.0-2 Cell segments token buckets Guaranteed number of EIRP tokens per sampling period (ID: 11118951)

**3.6.2.2.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11118955`)

Cell segments token buckets
In every sampling period, a minimum number of EIRP tokens per cell segment, rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s), shall always be available.

rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) = rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod \* rrmEirpMinTokenRatio(s)

where :

* rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod is the number of tokens over a sampling period as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2616\_replaced([11118946](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmEirpMinTokenRatio(s) = minGuaranteedBudgetRatio, if the minimum guaranteed budget is defined as an actualEirpBudgetRatio
* minGuaranteedBudgetRatio is received from the cell configuration

This minimum budget can only be spent in the given sampling period.

Any unused tokens from this budget at the end of the sampling period shall be collected in the unused minimum EIRP budget as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2622\_replaced([11118981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcyvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: maxPowerBudgetRatio is not supported

---

##### 3.6.2.2.2.0-3 Cell segments token buckets EIRP consumed tokens for each monitored cell segment (ID: 11118959)

**3.6.2.2.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11118965`)

Cell segments token buckets
The L2PS shall evaluate the number of token consumed in each cell segment. rrmConsumedTokens(s,k), is the number of consumed tokens from the bucket s during the period k (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4695\_replaced([11192990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvo18_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), ie the number of tokens consumed above rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2618\_replaced([11118951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

* if  k >= 0, rrmConsumedTokens(s,k) is derived from the rrmNormalizedEirp(s) from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2616\_replaced([11118946](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) converted in tokens (assuming rrmNormalizedEirp(s) is the accumulated value over the sampling period and normalized compared to pMax),

ie, rrmConsumedTokens(s,k) = max(0, rrmNormalizedEirp(s)/powerReductionFactor\_lin(s) - rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s))

[Before PR741703]

* if k<0, rrmConsumedTokens(s,k) is equal to (rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod - rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod) tokens, ie the EIRP budget has been consumed evenly over the sliding window before the initialization

[PR741703]

* if k<0, rrmConsumedTokens(s,k) is equal to (1-rdInitialTokenBucketRatio)\*(rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod - rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod) tokens, ie (1-rdInitialTokenBucketRatio) of the EIRP budget has been consumed evenly over the sliding window before the initialization while rdInitialTokenBucketRatio of the EIRP budget is available in the token bucket at initialization. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25880\_replaced([11120105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqNjbfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rdInitialTokenBucketRatio definition.

[End PR741703]

---

##### 3.6.2.2.2.0-4 Cell segments token buckets EIRP token buckets for each monitored cell segment (ID: 11118968)

**3.6.2.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11118971`)

Cell segments token buckets
The L2PS shall maintain one normalized EIRP token bucket for each segment to monitor (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2616\_replaced([11118946](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The token buckets have a maximum number of rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize tokens and a current number of rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket tokens.

rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize is the maximum number of tokens in the bucket and is equal to:

rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize(s)  = eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow \* (rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod - rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s)),

where :

* eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow is configured in MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControlPowerReductionFactorList and converted in number of sampling periods
* rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod is the number of tokens over a sampling period as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2616\_replaced([11118946](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2618\_replaced([11118951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If the minimum guaranteed budget is defined as a power ratio, then rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize and rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod are segment dependent.

The L2-PS shall evaluate, for each token bucket, the number of rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket at the start of next period as follows:

If rrmConsumedTokens(s,n-w) >= abs(rrmDeltaEirpControlToken(n))

rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket(s,n+1) = min[rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket(s,n) + rrmConsumedTokens(s,n-w) + rrmDeltaEirpControlToken(s,n) - rrmConsumedTokens(s,n), rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize]

rrmDeltaEirpControlToken(s,n+1) = 0

Else

rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket(s,n+1) = min[rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket(s,n) - rrmConsumedTokens(s,n), rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize]

rrmDeltaEirpControlToken(s,n+1) = rrmConsumedTokens(s,n-w) + rrmDeltaEirpControlToken(s,n)

where :

* rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket(s,0) = rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize - sum(rrmConsumedTokens(s,k), k=-w+1 to -1)
* w is the eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow is configured in MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControlPowerReductionFactorList and converted in number of sampling periods
* rrmConsumedTokens(s,k), is the number of consumed tokens from the bucket s during the period k as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30001\_replaced([11118959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note: rrmNormalizedEirp(s) shall be stored over eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow before being converted in EIRP tokens to remain independent of the applied powerReductionFactor in segments as it may change during the sliding window

* rrmDeltaEirpControlToken(s,0) = 0
* rrmDeltaEirpControlToken(s,n) is updated upon online modification of powerReductionFactor (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2626\_replaced([11118994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHczvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or upon update of the minimum guaranteed tokens (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2624\_replaced([11118987](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHczPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If after the token bucket evaluation, rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket is negative, then the negative budget is propagated to the next sampling budget using rrmEirpTokenDeficit = rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket and rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket is reset to 0. Otherwise rrmEirpTokenDeficit = 0.

Note: the number of tokens in the bucket may become negative if the DL scheduler cannot reduce the RB allocations such that the token consumption remains below rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod.

---

##### 3.6.2.2.2.0-5 Cell segments token buckets EIRP enhanced token buckets for each monitored cell segment (ID: 11118974)

**3.6.2.2.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11118978`)

Cell segments token buckets
The L2PS shall maintain one normalized EIRP token bucket for each segment to monitor (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2616\_replaced([11118946](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The token buckets have a maximum number of *rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize tokens and a current number of* rrmEirpControlTokenInTheEnhancedBucket tokens.\*\*

*rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize is the maximum number of tokens in the bucket and is equal to:*

*rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize(s)  =* eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow \* (*rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod -* rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s)),\*\*\*\*

where :

* *eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow is configured in* MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControlPowerReductionFactorList and converted in number of sampling periods\*\*
* *rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod is the number of tokens over a sampling period as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2616\_replaced([11118946](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*
* *rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2618\_replaced([11118951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*

If the minimum guaranteed budget is defined as a power ratio, then *rrmEirpControlTokenBucketSize and* rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod are segment dependent.\*\*

The L2-PS shall evaluate, for each token bucket, the number of *rrmEirpControlTokenInTheEnhancedBucket at the start of next period as follows:*

First, define ω such that:

For i=w-1..1

|   ω = max(ω + *rrmConsumedTokens(n-i), 0)*

Then, we compute the number of tokens in the bucket as:

*rrmEirpControlTokenInTheEnhancedBucket (s,n+1) =* w*(*rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod - *rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod) - ω*\*\*\*

where :

* w is the *eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow is configured in* MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControlPowerReductionFactorList and converted in number of sampling periods\*\*
* *rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2616\_replaced([11118946](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*
* *rrmConsumedTokens(s,k), is the number of consumed tokens from the bucket s during the period k as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30001\_replaced([11118959](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*

Note: *rrmNormalizedEirp(s) shall be stored over* eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow before being converted in EIRP tokens to remain independent of the applied *powerReductionFactor in segments as it may change during the sliding window*\*\*

If after the token bucket evaluation, *rrmEirpControlTokenInTheEnhancedBucket is negative, then the negative budget is propagated to the next sampling budget using* rrmEirpTokenDeficit = *rrmEirpControlTokenInTheEnhancedBucket and* rrmEirpControlTokenInTheEnhancedBucket is reset to 0. Otherwise *rrmEirpTokenDeficit = 0.*\*\*\*\*

Note: the number of tokens in the bucket may become negative if the DL scheduler cannot reduce the RB allocations such that the token consumption remains below rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod.

---

##### 3.6.2.2.2.0-6 Cell segments token buckets Unused minimum EIRP budget maintenance (ID: 11118981)

**3.6.2.2.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11118984`)

Cell segments token buckets
For each cell segment, the unused minimum EIRP budget rrmUnusedEirpMinBudget(s,n) shall be maintained over the sliding window for the purpose of minimum guaranteed budget adjustment and updated every sampling period.

The L2-PS shall evaluate, for each token bucket, the number of tokens in rrmUnusedEirpMinBudget at the start of next period as:

rrmUnusedEirpMinBudget (s,n+1) = min[rrmUnusedEirpMinBudget (s,n) + rrmConsumedTokensFromMin (s,n-w) - rrmConsumedTokensFromMin (s,n), rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s)\* w]

where:

* rrmUnusedEirpMinBudget (s,0) = rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) \* w - sum(rrmConsumedTokensFromMin (s,k), k=-w+1 to -1)
* w is the eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow is configured in MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControlPowerReductionFactorList and converted in number of sampling periods
* rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) is the number of guaranteed tokens per period as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2618\_replaced([11118951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmConsumedTokensFromMin (s,k), is the number of consumed tokens below rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) during the period k (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4695\_replaced([11192990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvo18_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* if k >= 0, rrmConsumedTokensFromMin (s,k) is derived from the rrmNormalizedEirp(s) from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2616\_replaced([11118946](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) converted in tokens (assuming rrmNormalizedEirp(s) is the accumulated value over the sampling period and normalized compared to pMax),

ie, rrmConsumedTokensFromMin (s,k) = rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) if (rrmNormalizedEirp(s)/powerReductionFactor\_lin(s) > rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) ), rrmConsumedTokensFromMin (s,k) = rrmNormalizedEirp(s)/powerReductionFactor\_lin(s) otherwise

* if k<0, rrmConsumedTokensFromMin (s,k) is equal to rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s), ie the EIRP budget has been consumed evenly over the sliding window before the initialization

---

##### 3.6.2.2.2.0-7 Cell segments token buckets Procedure to update guaranteed number of EIRP tokens per sampling period (ID: 11118987)

**3.6.2.2.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11118990`)

Cell segments token buckets
Upon the request to update the minimum guaranteed tokens per sampling period rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod from rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod\_old to rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod\_new, 5G-L2-PS shall proceed as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2626\_replaced([11118994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHczvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If a request to update the minimum guaranteed tokens per sampling period is received while another one is pending, the older one shall be cancelled and the latest received shall be processed.

---

##### 3.6.2.2.2.0-8 Cell segments token buckets EIRP token bucket update upon online modification of powerReductionFactor (ID: 11118994)

**3.6.2.2.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11118997`)

Cell segments token buckets
Upon online modification of powerReductionFactor for a given cell segment being monitored from powerReductionFactor\_old to powerReductionFactor\_new, the number of EIRP tokens in the token bucket shall be updated for the current sampling period n as follows :

5G-L2-PS shall reinitialize the different token buckets. During this initialization, if rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod\_new < rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod\_old then rrmConsumedTokens(s,k) shall be set to:

 rrmInitialConsumedTokens = max( 2\*rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod\_new - rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod\_old - rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod\_new, 0), if k<-1

 max(rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod\_new - rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod\_new - rrmInitialConsumedTokens,0) \*eirpControlTimeAveragingWindow + rrmInitialConsumedTokens, if k=-1

---

##### 3.6.2.2.3.0-2 Available tokens within a sampling period Load criteria for enhanced token bucket activation (ID: 11119020)

**3.6.2.2.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11119024`)

Available tokens within a sampling period
When NRCELL/eirpControl/smoothingEffect is not 0, the gNB shall evaluate if the scheduler is in overload control mode. To do so, gNB shall first set

rrmEirpEnableOverloadControl as the value of rdEnableEirpPerformanceImprovements (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29811\_replaced([11120178](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqOKgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB013773-C]

Then, if rdEnableEirpPerformanceImprovements is true, 5G-L2-PS shall compute the ratio, eirpCellNbUeCs1Ratio, of UEs in the CS1 list over the maximum number of UEs in the CS1 list (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8945\_replaced([11174992](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kufmffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) average over last EIRP measurement period.

If eirpCellNbUeCs1Ratio is strictly lower than rdEirpCellNbUeCs1Threshold\_percent (defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29985\_replaced([11120217](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqOxhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then rrmEirpEnableOverloadControl  shall be set to false. [End CB013773-C]

 rrmEirpControlSmoothedBucket(s) [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
= max(min(θVQ.Qn(s) + θTB.γnTB + θconst.γnTB), C̄)
The equation involves the following mathematical symbols and terms:
- '=': equals sign
- 'max': maximum function
- 'min': minimum function
- '(': opening parenthesis
- ')': closing parenthesis
- 'θVQ': theta raised to the power of VQ
- '.': multiplication dot
- 'Qn(s)': Q subscript n of s
- '+': plus sign
- 'θTB': theta raised to the power of TB
- 'γnTB': gamma subscript n raised to the power of TB
- 'θconst': theta raised to the power of const
- 'C̄': C with a macron (overline)
The text "72" appears below the equation, but it is unclear if it is related to the equation or a separate annotation.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6135.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is: $Q\_{n+1} = \max(Q\_n + rrmConsumedTokens(s,n) - \bar{C}, 0)$. The equation defines $Q\_{n+1}$ in terms of $Q\_n$, a function $rrmConsumedTokens(s,n)$, and a constant $\bar{C}$. The $\max$ function indicates that $Q\_{n+1}$ will be the larger of the two values: $Q\_n + rrmConsumedTokens(s,n) - \bar{C}$ or $0$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6135.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]
With rrmConsumedTokens is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2620\_replaced([11118968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqHcxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

##### 3.6.2.2.3.0-5 Available tokens within a sampling period Computation of the available EIRP tokens per DL slot to the DL scheduler (ID: 11119080)

**3.6.2.2.3.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11119089`)

Available tokens within a sampling period
The number of available tokens in a segment s for a sampling period, *rrmEirpControlAvailableTokens(s), is equal to:*

**[Before CB013773-A]**

*rrmEirpControlAvailableTokens(s) =* rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket(s) + *rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) + rrmEirpTokenDeficit(s).*\*\*

**[CB013773-A]**

*rmEirpControlAvailableTokens(s) =* rrmEirpControlTokens(s) + rrmEirpTokenDeficit(s).\*\*

Where *rrmEirpControlTokens(s) is equal to* rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket(s)+ *rmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) if* NRCELL/eirpControl/smoothingEffect is 0 and to *rrmEirpControlSmoothedBucket(s) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29995\_replaced([11119026](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqID1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) otherwise.*\*\*\*\*

**[End CB013773-A]**

If rrmEirpControlAvailableTokens(s) for segment s is smaller than rrmMaxTokenRateConsumption(s) \* rrmNumberOfAvailableTokensPerPeriod, then the number of tokens for the segment shall be monitored on a slot basis over the sampling period and a PRB reduction may be applied on PDSCH transmissions (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4349\_replaced([11177928](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuzIc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In this case the EIRP control is considered as active for the DL scheduler.

For the next sampling period, the DL scheduler shall be provided for each segment s with EIRP control active:

* the number of EIRP tokens from the bucket which is *rrmEirpControlTokenInTheBucket(s)* *+ rrmEirpTokenDeficit(s)* *[CB013773-A] or* rrmEirpControlTokens(s) - *rmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) + rrmEirpTokenDeficit(s)* *[End CB013773-A]****\****\*
* the EIRP token rate per DL symbol

*rrmEirpControlAvailableTokensPerSymbol(s) =* rrmMinEirpTokensPerPeriod(s) / number of DL symbols in the samplingPeriod\*\*

* for each beam, the number of consumed EIRP tokens per scheduled RB relative to PDSCH EPRE,

*rrmNumberOfEirpTokenPerRb(b,s) =* normalizedBeamGain(b,s) / (*powerReductionFactor\_lin(s) \** rrmMaxNumPrbDl)\*\*\*\*

where *rrmMaxNumPrbDl is the maximum number of RBs according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*

If *actDlSrsBm = false, then*

{

The set of beams includes the SSB and the refined beams.

If *dlMimoMode = "CL 8x4 MIMO"  and* actCellCsirsTddOnSsbBf is false, the set of beams shall be extended to the PMI beams.\*\*

Note: Given the multiplicity of PMI beams, it is left to implementation to derive *rrmNumberOfEirpTokenPerRb per PMI beam for each sampling period or to rescale the* rrmNumberOfEirpTokenPerRb on a need basis in the DL scheduler.\*\*

}

Else

{

1. The set of predefined beams includes the SSB and the refined beams.

2. If *dlMimoMode = “OL 4x4/4x2 MIMO” or “CL 4x4/4x2 MIMO”, the set of predefined beams shall be extended to SRS based oDFT beams.*

3. If *dlMimoMode = "CL 8x4 MIMO", the set of predefined beams shall be extended to the PMI beams and SRS based oDFT beams.*

4. If NIDD *NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True and DL tapering is enabled (see NIDD parameters of* dlMuMimoTaperingH and *dlMuMimoTaperingV), The set of beams shall be extended to SRS based oDFT beams with tapering. Values of* normalizedBeamGain(b, s) for tapered beams can be found in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8084\_replaced([11118921](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqG1uPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

5. If *NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm is true, subband beams which are updated at runtime shall be included. Note: due to high processing load,* normalizedBeamGain(b,s) is updated per sampling period which may be longer than subband beam update period. *rrmNumberOfEirpTokenPerRb(b,s) shall be updated at the begining of a new sampling period.*\*\*

}

---

### 3.6.2.3 EIRP-aware FD-POLITE Inner-loop Control (EPIC)

#### 3.6.2.3.0-1 EIRP-aware FD-POLITE Inner-loop Control (EPIC) FD-POLITE EPIC activation (ID: 12533536)

**3.6.2.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12533537`)

EIRP-aware FD-POLITE Inner-loop Control (EPIC)
If NRBTS/NRCELL/actFdPolite is enabled and NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControl/actEpic is enabled then gNB-DU shall evaluate if FD-POLITE EPIC MCS and Power reduction algorithm should be performed. EPIC MCS and Power reduction algorithm shall be performed if the following conditions are fulfilled:

* [CB013505-A] EIRP control is active on at least one segment (see [11192990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvo18_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) [End CB013505-A]
* EPIC algorithm is not suspended due to load (see [12533550](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_cjQ8QRxREfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

[CB013505-A-UPD002] Note: Due to implementation restrictions of FD-POLITE being executed per subcell, FD-POLITE EPIC algorithm shall also be executed per subcell (see [11177427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_YuOPUPvOEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The EIRP budget allocated to each subcell running the of FD-POLITE EPIC algorithm shall be determined according to [12805143: EIRP budget repartition per subcell for EPIC](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HtcfFp7WEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End CB013505-A-UPD002]

---

#### 3.6.2.3.0-2 EIRP-aware FD-POLITE Inner-loop Control (EPIC) EPIC dynamic activation an deactivation based on load (ID: 12533550)

**3.6.2.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12533551`)

EIRP-aware FD-POLITE Inner-loop Control (EPIC)
If NRBTS/NRCELL/eirpControl/actEpic is enabled, and if NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) is set to 0 and HwVariant used is not ABIL,

* If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See [11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_h-Ph0vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) value of the gNB-DU U-Plane, is greater than or equal to the value set for activation threshold of rdEirpEpicOlcDlPerCent (see [12533649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9iE28BxiEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))  
  then, gNB-DU shall suspend FD-POLITE EPIC MCS and Power reduction algorithm processing
* Else if the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric, given by l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See [11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_h-Ph0vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) value of the gNB-DU U-Plane, is below the value set for deactivation threshold of rdEirpEpicOlcDlPerCent (see [12533649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9iE28BxiEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))  
  then, gNB-DU shall resume above FD-POLITE EPIC MCS and Power reduction algorithm processing

---
