12533542:
EIRP-aware FD-POLITE Inner-loop Control (EPIC)
12533542:
EIRP-aware FD-POLITE Inner-loop Control (EPIC)
**Purpose**
In order to mitigate the risks of PRB blanking in segments under EIRP control, the EIRP-aware POLITE inner-loop Control (EPIC) algorithm aims at reducing the EIRP emissions by reducing the MCS and Power used for [CB013505-A-UPD005] non GBR traffic [End CB013505-A-UPD005] PDSCH communications towards the UEs.
 
**Inputs**
\* UEs MCS, Power 𝑃𝑢, SINR 𝑆𝐼𝑁𝑅𝑢 and PRB demand [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical symbol. It is the letter "A" with a subscript "u" and a horizontal bar above it. The symbol is rendered in a dark color, likely black or a very dark gray, against a white background. The font appears to be a serif font, common in mathematical notation.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301201.png[/image\_path][/image-0] after legacy FD scheduling PRB allocations or after FD-POLITE PRB widening if it is active in this slot (see [12533182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oNYRdxw6EfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
[CB013505-A-UPD005] Note: 𝑃𝑢 is computed as pdschTbTransmitPower following [11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End CB013505-A-UPD005]
\* 𝛼𝑢,𝑠: the beam gain associated to the UE u in each segment s
[CB013505-A-UPD005] Note: In cases where the UE is scheduled with more than one beam, 𝛼𝑢,𝑠 shall be computed as the sum of the contribution of the beams of user u in the segment s, in linear form. [End CB013505-A-UPD005]
\* NRCELL/eirpControl/epicMcsThreshold: The minimum MCS for UEs under EPIC MCS reduction
\* rdEirpEpicFairness: the fairness of the EPIC algorithm (see [12533640](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6mqEIBxhEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
 
**Algorithm**
1. Compute the following for each user u:
• The maximum TX power: [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression consists of a capital letter "P" with a bar above it and a subscript "u" below and to the right of the "P". The "P" is bold and appears to be in a serif font. The bar above the "P" is also bold. The subscript "u" is smaller than the "P" and is also bold.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301202.png[/image\_path][/image-1]=𝑃𝑢
• The minimum TX power: 𝑃𝑢=[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression consists of a capital letter "P" with a bar above it and a subscript "u" below and to the right of the "P". The "P" is bold and appears to be in a serif font. The bar above the "P" is also bold. The subscript "u" is smaller than the "P" and is also bold.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301202.png[/image\_path][/image-2].𝑆𝐼𝑁𝑅𝑢(NRCELL/eirpControl/epicMcsThreshold) / 𝑆𝐼𝑁𝑅𝑢
With 𝑆𝐼𝑁𝑅𝑢(NRCELL/eirpControl/epicMcsThreshold) being the planned SINR at MCS=NRCELL/eirpControl/epicMcsThreshold for user u while retaining its current Tx Power
Note: Alternatively, the SINR ratio can be substituted by and MCS difference between the current and UE MCS NRCELL/eirpControl/epicMcsThreshold in dB as per [11118517: powerReduction](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [PR864460] multiplied by 0.9192
Then compute 𝑃𝑢= max(𝑃𝑢,[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression consists of a capital letter "P" with a bar above it and a subscript "u" below and to the right of the "P". The "P" is bold and appears to be in a serif font. The bar above the "P" is also bold. The subscript "u" is smaller than the "P" and is also bold.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301202.png[/image\_path][/image-3] \* rdMaxPowerReduction) (for rdMaxPowerReduction see [13353363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oYGTw-1sEfC3ocOh_n7w7A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), the value of rdMaxPowerReduction should be converted to linear form to be used in this formula) [End PR864460]
• The noise power: 𝑁0,𝑢=𝑃𝑢 / 𝑆𝐼𝑁𝑅𝑢
2. Define the following functions:
• Approximation function that maps Tx power 𝑃𝑢 for user 𝑢 and its spectral efficiency:
𝑟𝑢(𝑝𝑢)=2.78.log10(1+𝑃𝑢/𝑁0,𝑢)
• Define in each segment s the Lagrangian multiplier:
h𝑢,𝑠(𝑃𝑢) = 1/𝛼𝑢,𝑠([image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical symbol. It is the letter "A" with a subscript "u" and a horizontal bar above it. The symbol is rendered in a dark color, likely black or a very dark gray, against a white background. The font appears to be a serif font, common in mathematical notation.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301201.png[/image\_path][/image-4]𝑟𝑢(𝑃𝑢))−𝛿.2.78/(ln(10).(𝑁0,𝑢+𝑃𝑢))
o Where 𝛿 is defined by rdEirpEpicFairness
3. Compute in each segment the limits of the Lagrangian multiplier:
• 𝜈𝑠=min𝑢(h𝑢,𝑠([image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression consists of a capital letter "P" with a bar above it and a subscript "u" below and to the right of the "P". The "P" is bold and appears to be in a serif font. The bar above the "P" is also bold. The subscript "u" is smaller than the "P" and is also bold.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301202.png[/image\_path][/image-5]))
• [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical symbol. It is a Greek letter nu (ν) with a bar over it and a subscript "s". The symbol is rendered in a bold, italicized font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301206.png[/image\_path][/image-6]=max𝑢(h𝑢,𝑠(𝑃𝑢))
[CB013505-A-UPD005] Note: Case were [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical symbol. It is a Greek letter nu (ν) with a bar over it and a subscript "s". The symbol is rendered in a bold, italicized font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301206.png[/image\_path][/image-7] < 𝜈𝑠 are possible. In such case we should still iterate through the different UEs as detailed below. [End CB013505-A-UPD005]
4. Compute the outer loop dichotomy (see [12533547](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_92qFARxQEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
[Before PR864460]
𝜈∗= epic\_outer\_dichotomy\_search([image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression starts with a summation symbol (Σ). Following the summation symbol, there is a term denoted as $\bar{A}*{u,s}$. This term is multiplied by $\alpha*{u,s}$. The expression continues with $v^{2p}(v, u)$. The entire expression is enclosed in parentheses.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-05131314.png[/image\_path][/image-8],gk , 𝜈𝑠, [image-9][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical symbol. It is a Greek letter nu (ν) with a bar over it and a subscript "s". The symbol is rendered in a bold, italicized font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301206.png[/image\_path][/image-9])
[PR864460]
𝜈∗= epic\_outer\_dichotomy\_search([image-10][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is:
$$ \frac{N\_{Re}}{PRF\_s} \sum \overline{A}*{u,s} \alpha*{u,s} \mathbf{v2p}(v, u)) N\_{symb,u} $$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01151132.png[/image\_path][/image-10],gk , 𝜈𝑠, [image-11][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical symbol. It is a Greek letter nu (ν) with a bar over it and a subscript "s". The symbol is rendered in a bold, italicized font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301206.png[/image\_path][/image-11])  [End PR864460]
• 𝝂𝟐𝒑(𝜈,𝑢)= epic\_inner\_dichotomy\_search(h𝑢(𝑃𝑢),𝜈 , Pu,[image-12][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression consists of a capital letter "P" with a bar above it and a subscript "u" below and to the right of the "P". The "P" is bold and appears to be in a serif font. The bar above the "P" is also bold. The subscript "u" is smaller than the "P" and is also bold.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301202.png[/image\_path][/image-12]) – inner loop dichotomy (see [12533544](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_k2JN4hxQEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
where:
• gk is the number of token available in the current slot for segment k (rmAvailableEirpTokensInCurrentSlot, see [12526294](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-_HiABrIEfC3upM2pE5-4w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [12805143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HtcfFp7WEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) when applicable) [CB013505-A-UPD005] and deprived of the EIRP impact of other transmission than non-GBR data [End CB013505-A-UPD005]
• [PR864460] [image-13][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a black, sans-serif font. The expression is "NRe". The "N" is a capital letter, and the "Re" is a subscript.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01121326.png[/image\_path][/image-13] is the number of ressource element per PRB
• [image-14][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression $N\_{symb,u}$. The expression consists of the letter 'N' followed by a subscript. The subscript is composed of the word "symb" and the letter "u" separated by a comma. The font used is a serif font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01131331.png[/image\_path][/image-14] is the number of symbols used for the UE u PDSCH transmission
• [image-15][image\_desc]The image contains the text "PRF" followed by a subscript "s". The letters are in a dark gray color against a white background. The font is a serif font.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01131331.png[/image\_path][/image-15] is the power reduction factor in the current segment s from NRCELL.EirpControl.PowerReductionFactorList converted into linear form
Note: LTE CRS RE are not considered when performing EPIC budget consumption estimate as it is assumed to have neglectable impact [End PR864460]
**Outputs**
Update the power for each UE u to the optimal power allocation 𝑃𝑢∗= 𝜈2𝑝(𝜈∗,𝑢) and to the corresponding MCS that maximize spectral efficiency (subject to the target BLER). [CB013505-A-UPD005] Once EPIC as been run in all segments under EIRP control, the resulting MCS shall then be used to compute pdschTbTransmitPower once again for each impacted UE according to [11118372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End CB013505-A-UPD005] [PR864460] The minimum between the optimal power computed by EPIC and pdschTbTransmitPower shall be used for the UE PDSCH transmission slot s [End PR864460]
[CB013505-A-UPD005] Note: EPIC should be run and all segments under EIRP control. This implies that some UEs affecting two or more segments may be subject to multiple consecutive MCS reduction due to EPIC. In such case, the MCS and power of previous EPIC iterations shall be used for the next EPIC processing. [End CB013505-A-UPD005]

12533548:
EIRP-aware FD-POLITE Inner-loop Control (EPIC)
**Purpose**
This algorithm describes the dichotomy search function used in the outer loop of the EPIC algorithm: dichotomy\_search(f,y,𝑥,[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. The horizontal line above the "X" is also black and appears to be of similar thickness to the strokes of the "X". The overall impression is that of a symbol or a logo.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301204.png[/image\_path][/image-0]). It is defined as the function that computes the point in [𝑥,[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. The horizontal line above the "X" is also black and appears to be of similar thickness to the strokes of the "X". The overall impression is that of a symbol or a logo.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301204.png[/image\_path][/image-1]] that minimizes |𝑓(𝑥)−𝑦|. This search should be done in inverse scale on the x axis as this results in a quasi linear function and thus faster convergence. The search interval is limited by the intersection between the current limits and y.
**Inputs**
\* f(x): the functions to resolved
\* y: the result of the function on the parameter x to be found
\* [𝑥,[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. The horizontal line above the "X" is also black and appears to be of similar thickness to the strokes of the "X". The overall impression is that of a symbol or a logo.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301204.png[/image\_path][/image-2]] : the maximum and minimum values for x
\* rdEirpEpicSearchSteps: the maximum number of steps of the dichotomy search (see [12533645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_zcQdgBxiEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
\* [Before PR864460] rdEirpEpicSearchTolerance [PR864460] rdEirpEpicSearchToleranceOuter [End PR864460]: the tolerance towards the accuracy of the resulting x (see [12533647](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_4qmKoBxiEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
**Algorithm**
\* If f([image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. The horizontal line above the "X" is also black and appears to be of similar thickness to the strokes of the "X". The overall impression is that of a symbol or a logo.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301204.png[/image\_path][/image-3]) >= y then return [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. The horizontal line above the "X" is also black and appears to be of similar thickness to the strokes of the "X". The overall impression is that of a symbol or a logo.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301204.png[/image\_path][/image-4]
If f(𝑥) <= y then return 𝑥
\* Set l := 𝑥 & r := [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. The horizontal line above the "X" is also black and appears to be of similar thickness to the strokes of the "X". The overall impression is that of a symbol or a logo.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301204.png[/image\_path][/image-5]
\* Set X, the proportional factor of the intersection point as: X := (y−f(r))/(f(l)−f(r))
\* Set m, the intersection point x coordinate in inverse scale, as: [Before PR864460] m := 1/r + X(1/l−1/r) [PR864460] m := 1/(1/r + X(1/l−1/r)) [EndPR864460]
\* While (r-l) > [Before PR864460] rdEirpEpicSearchTolerance [PR864460] rdEirpEpicSearchToleranceOuter [End PR864460] and the number of iteration is less than rdEirpEpicSearchSteps
+ Set X, the proportional factor of the intersection point as: X := (y−f(r))/(f(l)−f(r))
+ Set m, the intersection point x coordinate in inverse scale, as: m := 1/r + X(1/l−1/r)
+ Set m:= 1/m
+ If f(m) < y then Set r := m
+ Else Set l := m
\* return m
**Outputs**
x value such that f(x)=y with a precision of rdEirpEpicSearchTolerance if achievable within rdEirpEpicSearchSteps or less.

**Purpose**
This algorithm describes the dichotomy search function used in the inner loop of the EPIC algorithm: dichotomy\_search(f,y,𝑥,[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. The horizontal line above the "X" is also black and appears to be of similar thickness to the strokes of the "X". The overall impression is that of a symbol or a logo.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301204.png[/image\_path][/image-0]). It is defined as the function that computes the point in [𝑥,[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. The horizontal line above the "X" is also black and appears to be of similar thickness to the strokes of the "X". The overall impression is that of a symbol or a logo.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301204.png[/image\_path][/image-1]] that minimizes |𝑓(𝑥)−𝑦|.
**Inputs**
\* f(x): the functions to resolved
\* y: the result of the function on the parameter x to be found
\* [𝑥,[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. The overall impression is that of a symbol or a logo.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301204.png[/image\_path][/image-2]] : the maximum and minimum values for x
\* rdEirpEpicSearchSteps: the maximum number of steps of the dichotomy search (see [12533645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_zcQdgBxiEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
\* [Before PR864460] rdEirpEpicSearchTolerance [PR864460] rdEirpEpicSearchToleranceInner [End PR864460]: the tolerance towards the accuracy of the resulting x (see [Before PR864460] [12533647](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_4qmKoBxiEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [PR864460] [13352323](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_a7h6Z-0_EfC3ocOh_n7w7A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End PR864460])
**Algorithm**
\* If f([image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. The "X" is rendered in a bold, black font, with the top and bottom points of the "X" extending slightly beyond the main body of the letter. \* Set l := 𝑥 & r := [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a stylized letter "X" with a horizontal line above it. \* Set m := (r+l)/2
\* While (r-l) > [Before PR864460] rdEirpEpicSearchTolerance [PR864460] rdEirpEpicSearchToleranceInner [End PR864460] and the number of iteration is less than rdEirpEpicSearchSteps
+ Set m := (r+l)/2
+ If f(m) < y then Set r := m
+ Else Set l := m
\* return m
**Outputs**
x value such that f(x)=y with a precision of rdEirpEpicSearchTolerance if achievable within rdEirpEpicSearchSteps or less.

$g\_{k,i} = g\_k \frac{\sum\_{u \in subcell\_i} \alpha\_{u,k} \cdot \overline{A\_u}}{\sum\_{u \in U\_{subcells}} \alpha\_{u,k} \cdot \overline{A\_u}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-10081352.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

* [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical symbol. It is the letter "A" with a subscript "u" and a horizontal bar above it. The font appears to be a serif font, common in mathematical notation.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301201.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is PRB demand for user u after legacy FDM PRB allocations and before any FD-POLITE PRB widening
* 𝛼𝑢,k: the beam gain associated to the UE u in each segment k

In such cases, the FD-POLITE EPIC algorithm detailed in [12533541](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PnIScBxQEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) shall be executed per subcells and the number of tokens available in that algorithm (defined as gk=rrmAvailableEirpTokensInCurrentSlot) should be substituted by [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a dark gray, serif font. The main character is a lowercase 'g' with a subscript 'h' and another subscript that appears to be a Greek letter 'a' with a bar over it.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-10021119.png[/image\_path][/image-4].

[CB013505-A-UPD005] Note: when FD-POLITE is run per subcell, UEs in MU-MIMO pairing are expected to belong to different subcells and the MCS and power reduction due to EPIC of UEs under MU-MIMO pairing may lead to a different level inter user interference compared to what was computed prior by the gNB in the MU-MIMO algorithm. It is assumed that such difference only marginally degrades MU-MIMO performances at most. [End CB013505-A-UPD005]

---

If artificial load is enabled (either through NRCELL/actConfDlInterferenceGen, NRCELL/actEmfTestMode or NRCELL/targetTotalLoad>0) and if a dummy PDSCH load is present and affects a segment under EIRP control (see [11184003: Beam configuration for DL artificial load](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvPNUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), then:

[Before CB013505-B-UPD004]

The associated fake UE shall be considered as a normal UE for the purpose of FD-POLITE EPIC algorithm.

[CB013505-B-UPD004]

After legacy FD scheduling PRB allocations or after FD-POLITE PRB widening, gNB-DU shall handle UEs created for artificial load traffic outside of the FD-POLITE EPIC algorithm as follows.

gNB-DU shall evaluate if the EIRP token demand in a given EIRP controlled segment, taking into account the dummy PDSCH load, is greater than the number of tokens available in the current slot for segment s (rrmAvailableEirpTokensInCurrentSlot(s), see [12526294](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-_HiABrIEfC3upM2pE5-4w)). If so, then gNB-DU shall:

* Compute the minimum TX power 𝑃𝑢 of the dummy load by subtracting from its maximum TX power [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression consists of a capital letter "P" with a bar above it and a subscript "u" below and to the right of the "P". The "P" is bold and appears to be in a serif font. The bar above the "P" is also bold. The subscript "u" is smaller than the "P" and is also bold.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301202.png[/image\_path][/image-0] the difference between the current MCS of the dummy load MCSu,max and NRCELL/eirpControl/epicMcsThreshold in dB as per [11118517: powerReduction](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* 𝑃𝑢 = min([image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression consists of a capital letter "P" with a bar above it and a subscript "u" below and to the right of the "P". The "P" is bold and appears to be in a serif font. The bar above the "P" is also bold. The subscript "u" is smaller than the "P" and is also bold.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301202.png[/image\_path][/image-1] - MCSu,max + NRCELL/eirpControl/epicMcsThreshold, [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression consists of a capital letter "P" with a bar above it and a subscript "u" below and to the right of the "P". The "P" is bold and appears to be in a serif font. The bar above the "P" is also bold. The subscript "u" is smaller than the "P" and is also bold.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301202.png[/image\_path][/image-2])
* If the EIRP token demand assuming a Tx power of 𝑃𝑢 for the dummy load is still above the number of tokens available:
* Set the power of the dummy load to 𝑃𝑢 and subtract dummy load EIRP impact from the number of tokens available in the current slot for segment s and proceed with EPIC algorithm as per [12533541: EIRP Aware MSC and Power reduction](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PnIScBxQEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* Else:
* Iterate through the MCS range [NRCELL/eirpControl/epicMcsThreshold, MCSu,max-1] in a decreasing order until the EIRP token demand is lower than the number of tokens available in the current slot assuming a Tx power 𝑃𝑢,i of the dummy load.  
  Where:
  + MCSu,i is ith MCS in the MCS range for the dummy load defined above
  + 𝑃𝑢,i = [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression consists of a capital letter "P" with a bar above it and a subscript "u" below and to the right of the "P". The "P" is bold and appears to be in a serif font. The bar above the "P" is also bold. The subscript "u" is smaller than the "P" and is also bold.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04301202.png[/image\_path][/image-3] - MCSu,max + MCSu,i
* Set the power of the dummy load to 𝑃𝑢,i and stop further FD-POLITE EPIC processing for this segment.

[End CB013505-B-UPD004]

## 3.6.3 UL Power Control

### 3.6.3.0-3 UL Power Control Document Owner Deputy Xianlei Zhang; Marilyn Ma (ID: 11119104)

### 3.6.3.1 Closed Loop Power Control for PUSCH

#### 3.6.3.1.0-1 Closed Loop Power Control for PUSCH Determination of the UE PATHLOSS (ID: 11119109)

**3.6.3.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13383275`)

Closed Loop Power Control for PUSCH
The calculation of the UE Pathloss shall be done according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2748\_replaced([11121531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYik_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The pathloss related to the UL branch shall be calculated for the PCell  and [CB014067-A]  each active  [End CB014067-A] FR1 SCell with UL configured as the difference of the UE’s PUSCH transmission power and the UL receive power detected at the gNB. For this purpose, the UE’s PUSCH transmission power shall be evaluated based on the type 1 PHR received continuously with the data stream in UL.

Note:

* the expectation is that the PHR is received every 20ms or earlier depending of operator parameter setting (parameter “tPeriodicPhr”).
* parameter "refPathloss" set by operator defines the reference pathloss to be used when the PHR is not received yet.

---

If (NIDD:actUlMuMimo is disabled) OR (NIDD:actUlMuMimo is enabled [CB010708-I] and NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming = 4RX [End CB010708-I] and NIDD:nrCellType is xDL4UL)

The gNodeB shall calculate Interference and noise term I according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1652\_replaced([11108250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koo2FvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) over the allocated cell BW, excluding fake UE for RTWP measurements (5G\_UP\_ALG\_16488\_replaced([11108683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kouVo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ;

At each slot, the term I please note that this term includes the Noise as well;

Else if ((NIDD:actUlMuMimo is enabled) AND ((NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is set to 4RX and NIDD:nrCellType is xDL8UL) OR (NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is set to 8RX) [CB010708-I] OR (NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is set to 16RX)))[End CB010708-I] :

At each slot i, the term K1allocBW (i) (measurement of interference and noise as well) is averaged on all PRBs of 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8118\_replaced([11108307](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kopdJvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), excluding fake UE for RTWP measurements (5G\_UP\_ALG\_16488\_replaced([11108683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kouVo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6153.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0], where K1prb is the noise per prb averaged over all the receiving antennas (spatial streams), and numOfStreams is decided as below:

[Before CB010708-I]

- numOfStreams is equal to NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming.

[CB010708-I]

-  If NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is equal to 16RX, numOfStreams is decided by rdSuUeReceiverSize (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27595\_replaced([11114156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- Else numOfStreams is equal to NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming.

[End CB010708-I]

The unit of [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the following text: K1allocBW(j, subcell) and K1prb(i)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6153.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] is dB.

A new average term is calculated at each slot with the method of the sliding window and the averaging is proportioned to the duration of the sliding window (i.e. if the averaging window is 20ms, the samples of K1allocBW collected during last 20ms are used in the calculation);

The time averaging period of the sliding window is defined by operator by setting the parameter „clpcPusch.interferAveMeasPeriod“, larger values of this parameter correspond generally to a less fluctuant value of K1alloc\_ave;

The time averaging period defined by parameter „clpcPusch.interferAveMeasPeriod“ is expected to be 100ms or above (according to our simulations);

The gNodeB shall then calculate the average value K1alloc\_ave over an averaging window as defined in the following:

K1alloc\_ave(i) = 1/S\*([image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression written in a large font. The expression is:
$$ \sum\_{x=1}^{x=1-5} $$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6153.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] K1allocBW (x))              (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2636\_replaced([11119117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-1)

Where:

1. Term „i“ is the slot index

2. Term „S“ is the number of slots in the averaging time window defined by „clpcPusch.interferAveMeasPeriod“

Note:

* Please consider that the number of slots in the averaging time is conditioned by the configured numerology (i.e. by the configured subcarrier spacing: in case of 15Khz Subcarrier spacing there is 1 slot per subframe, while for 30KHz Subcarrier spacing there are 2 slots per subframe).
* Please consider that in TDD the number of slots in the averaging time is as well conditioned by the UL/DL ratio, therefore by the same setting of „clpcPusch.interferAveMeasPeriod“ the calculated K1wb\_ave may fluctuate largely than in FDD with the same averaging period.
* Please consider that the system keeps track of the average I+N got in the cell during last day and when no I+N are available because missed UL scheduling, it uses this average value.

It shall calculate Target SINR **on Pcell and FR1 SCell configured with UL and activated** every time the Pathloss or the measured Interference is updated.\*\*\*\*

The formula to be used for the PUSCH Target SIR calculation shall be:

If NRBTS/NRCELL/actAveRxAntPwr is set to 'False' [CB008465-AA] and UL CoMP is NOT active ([12740784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PBhWcXv0EfCiUemk-K-C4g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) [End CB008465-AA] then

* TargetSINR-PUSCH = P0\_PUSCH + SCSFactor + AntennaFactor – (1-α)\*Pathloss – Interference + OffsetPusch

(5G\_UP\_ALG\_2638\_replaced([11119168](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-1)     

else

* **Target**SINR-PUSCH **= P**0\_PUSCH **+ SCSFactor****– (1-α)*Pathloss – Interference + Offset\*\*Pusch******\******\***\*

(5G\_UP\_ALG\_2638\_replaced([11119168](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-3)

**Where:**

1. SCSFactor: this term keeps care of the element scs described by NRBTS/NRCELLGRP/scs, which defines the subcarrier spacing and consequently the effective BW of a single PRB.   
The correction term can be calculated in this way: 10\*(log10 scs/15).

2. AntennaFactor: this term introduces a correction related to the number of RX antenna in the cell, and shall be correspond to  10\*(log10 #of RX antennas). If NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is set to 16RX, the number of RX antenna is decided by the number of RX antenna for UE rdSuUeReceiverSize (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27595\_replaced([11114156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))); Else, it is equal to the number of antennas can be extrapolated from the element “ulSubcellType” as described in 5G\_UP\_2142\_replaced([11381236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uero9fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

3. The term Pathloss is determined as described in Requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2634\_replaced([11119109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

4. The term Interference corresponds to K1alloc\_ave and it is determined as described in Requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2636\_replaced([11119117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) by formula 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2636\_replaced([11119117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-1, this term contains the noise component as well and it is calculated only on all the allocated PRB;

5. P0\_PUSCH and alpha are operator parameter settings, already defined with the implementation of the UL Open Loop Power Control; P0\_PUSCH  will sum of [image-0][image\_desc]The image is entirely black, with no discernible features, text, or objects.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6160.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0](

 If NIDD parameter NRCELL.actSliceBasedUlPwrCtrl is FALSE, refer to NRCELL.ulPowerControlCommon.p0NominalPusch.

 If NIDD parameter NRCELL.actSliceBasedUlPwrCtrl is TRUE, refer to P0\_Nominal\_PUSCH in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_13916\_replaced([11270513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_To9dVfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) during runtime reconfiguration. Rationale: 5G\_UP\_12270\_replaced([11353010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub728fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

) and [image-1][image\_desc]The image is entirely black, with no discernible features, text, or objects.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6160.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1](refer to NRBTS/NRCELL/ulPowerControlCommon/p0UePusch) once it is configured according to TS38.213.(**Note: Runtime reconfiguration of PCell [image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6160.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]is supported for FR1 UL CA during SCell reconfiguration with SCell UL configured according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2698\_replaced([11120363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqP_rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) including SCell additio, SCell release and so on).**

6. OffsetPusch is:

 If NIDD parameter NRCELL.actSliceBasedUlPwrCtrl is FALSE, is **defined by the operator parameter ”clpcPusch.targetSinrOffset”.**

 If NIDD parameter NRCELL.actSliceBasedUlPwrCtrl is TRUE, refer to targetSinrOffset in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_13916\_replaced([11270513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_To9dVfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) during runtime reconfiguration. Rationale: 5G\_UP\_12270\_replaced([11353010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub728fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The above calculated PUSCH Target SINR shall be clipped against a max and a min value configured by operator:

TargetSINR-PUSCH =max (min (TargetSINR-PUSCH,T\_SINRPUSCH\_max),T\_SINRPUSCH\_min                (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2638\_replaced([11119168](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-2)

Where:

* T\_SINRPUSCH\_max = clpcPusch.maxTargSinr where “clpcPusch.maxTargSinr" is a new operator configurable parameter;
* T\_SINRPUSCH\_min is operator configurable by the new parameter “clpcPusch.minTargSinr".

Closed Loop Power Control for PUSCH
If NRBTS/NRCELL/actAveRXAntPwr is set to 'True' [CB008465-AA] or UL CoMP is active ([12740784](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PBhWcXv0EfCiUemk-K-C4g)) [End CB008465-AA] then

* //Note of the author: this correction is introduced to let the gNB-DU better cope with malfunctioning customer equipment, and it is intended to keep minimal the effort of the implementation. //
* For each scheduled UE, the gNodeB shall recursively calculate the effective received Signal power for PUSCH as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1688\_replaced([11108734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kou8tfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) vs. the interference and Noise as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1652\_replaced([11108250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koo2FvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* The **M1**ant**measures, described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1688\_replaced([11108734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kou8tfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), of the UL received power for [Before CB008465-AA] Ant0 and Ant1 [CB008465-AA] serving cell antennas [End CB008465-AA] are providing the RSSI value for [Before CB008465-AA] Antenna 0 and Antenna 1 [CB008465-AA] serving cell antennas [End CB008465-AA].**\*\*\*\*
* The two **M1**ant above mentioned should be harmonic averaged on their linear values at every slot.\*\*\*\*(An example of how harmonic average is done is already described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3084\_replaced([11131461](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* The result **M1**HarmAve of the harmonic averaging shall be converted from linear to logarithmic (please note: this measure is reported UE specifically).\*\*\*\*
* The measure **K1**allocBW, described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1652\_replaced([11108250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koo2FvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), of the UL received noise on allocated PRB is averaged per slot and shall be logarithmic (please note: this measure is reported on cell base).\*\*\*\*
* The **M1**HarmAve and **K1**allocBW values provided at each slot (where UE has sent data in UL) shall be averaged over a sliding averaging window defined by parameter “clpcPusch.sinrAveMeasSamples” and set by operator. SINRUE\_AVE shall be calculated on Pcell and FR1 SCell configured with UL and activated .***\****\*
* SINRUE\_AVE(i) =[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation.
  The equation is:
  $$ \sum\_{N=-S+1}^{S} \frac{M1HarmAve(x) - K1allocBW(x)}{S} $$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6164.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0](5G_UP_ALG_2640_replaced([11119228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-2)

else

* For each scheduled UE, the gNodeB shall recursively calculate the effective received Signal power for PUSCH as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1684\_replaced([11108694](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kouVp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) vs. the interference and Noise as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1652\_replaced([11108250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koo2FvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* The measure **M4, described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7068\_replaced([11108698](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kouVqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), of the UL received power is averaged per slot and shall be logarithmic (please note: this measure is reported UE specifically).**
* The measure **K1**allocBW, there described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1652\_replaced([11108250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koo2FvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), of the UL received noise on allocated PRB is averaged per slot and shall be logarithmic (please note: this measure is reported on cell base).\*\*\*\*
* The **M4 and**K1**allocBW values provided at each slot (where UE has sent data in UL) shall be averaged over a sliding averaging window defined by parameter “clpcPusch.sinrAveMeasSamples” and set by operator. SINRUE\_AVE shall be calculated on Pcell and FR1 SCell configured with Ul and activated.**\*\*\*\*
* SINRUE\_AVE(i) = ([image-1][image\_desc]$\sum\_{x=i-s+1}^{i} M4(x) - K1 allocBW(x)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6164.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1])\*1/S  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2640\_replaced([11119228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-1)

Where:

* SINRUE\_AVE is expressed in dB
* The averaging factor S is: S = clpcPusch.sinrAveMeasSamples

Note:

* The number of samples S, in a given interval of time, depends on the subcarrier spacing
* The number of samples S, in a given interval of time, is as well conditioned by the UL/DL slot ratio in case of TDD.
* The number of samples clpcPusch.sinrAveMeasSamples is the largest possible for the averaging window, but there are conditions (e.g. seldom scheduling of UE in UL) where this number can be smaller; consequently, the average may be done on a smaller number of samples, because of the presence of samples that undergo to the following condition:
* if the last sample S is older than a given number of subframes (defined by a dedicated r&d parameter and set to 1000ms), all samples are discarded.
* if the last sample update S comes after “clpcPusch.tIntervalSinrUpd” subframes, then all the samples but last are discarded.
* By extreme conditions, therefore, it may happen that SINRUE\_AVE(i) = M4(i) - K1allocBW(i)
*  minimal number of 3 samples S shall be required to consider meaningful the calculation of SINRUE\_AVE(i); in case the value is calculated with less than 3 samples  the system shall generate automatically a TPC command = 0dB.)
* After Scell activation, the 1st sliding window begins from the slot where the 1st UL transmission for FR1 CA UE is scheduled on Scell.

13383442:
Closed Loop Power Control for PUSCH
Restriction for uplink closed loop power control implementation:
1. DCI format 2\_2 is not supported;
2. Dual state TPC is not supported.
 
SINRUE\_AVE and TargetSINR-PUSCH shall be expressed in dB.
 
 
Calculates PUSCH TPC when PUSCH is scheduled:
 ΔPUSCH = TargetSINR-PUSCH - SINRUE\_AVE    (see [11119253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)-1)
Where:
1. SINRUE\_AVE is provided by Requirement  [11119228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)-1.
2. TargetSINR-PUSCH is provided by Requirement [11119168](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)-1.
 
 
Indicates PUSCH TPC to L1 by encoding DCI format 0\_1 [11198812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwLBc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) the logic is as follows:
  If (ΔPUSCH ≤ δSINR\_1) then {TPC = -1}
  Else if (δSINR\_1 < ΔPUSCH ≤ δSINR\_2) then {TPC = 0}
  Else if (δSINR\_2 < ΔPUSCH ≤ δSINR\_3) then {TPC = +1}
  Else {TPC = +3}     ([11119253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)-2)
 
 [docx\_desc]
[/docx\_desc][docx\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/attachments/m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file6174\_0.docx[/docx\_path]  
 
If the measured RSSI ([11108492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kor5YfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is equal or larger than **rdMaxRssiPuschCLPC ([11120121](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqOKcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the value TPC will be limited as following to avoid the risk of power saturation at antenna reception, which will cause a not desirable escalation in the UE power.**
               TPCfinal = -1dB
 
If RIM UL mitigation extension is triggered and stopping UL close loop power control ([11163444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktZaQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the value TPC will be limited as following to stop close loop power control during remote interference.
               TPCfinal = 0dB
 
Note:
\* DeltaSINR\_x are 3 predefined values that operator may choose by configuring the parameter clpcPusch.sinrThresholdIndex; the values shown in the above picture correspond to predefined triplet 1 (see req. [11352892](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub6o2fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Each pre-defined triplet sets the thresholds under or beyond those a given TPC command is sent to UE (specifically dedicated to PUSCH).
\* In case the value of the signal component in the SINRUE\_AVE calculation was averaged over a single sample the TPC command is forced always to value TPC = 0dB (this is coherent with statement in item 5 of [11119357](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
\* When the UE report a PHR equal to or smaller than 0dB the TPC command is always forced to 0dB, when TPC > 0dB.
\* For an FR1 Ul CA UE, the TPC command shall be forced to value TPC = 0dB on SCell, when the buffer split status is "stop split" specified in [11122476](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). Note: In case the buffer split status is "stop split", the TPC value associated to a ReTX shall be the same one used in the corresponding NewTx.
\* For an FR1 UL CA UE, during the transient period of SCell addition according to [11120306](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqPYnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and SCell release according to [11120596](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqSb5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) as well as SCell change/swap and there is [image-0][image\_desc]The image is entirely black, with no discernible features, text, or objects.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6174.002.png[/image\_path][/image-0]reconfiguration(refer to NRBTS/NRCELL/ulPowerControlCommon/p0UePusch), the TPC command shall be forced to value TPC = 0dB. **Note: For FR1 UL CA with TDD PCell and FDD SCell, no FDD SCell scheduling is allowed in UL overlapping slot, and no power split is needed for SCell. Therefore when SCell reconfiguration including SCell addition, SCell release as well SCell change/swap, gNB will not reconfigure [image-1][image\_desc]The image is entirely black, with no discernible features, text, or objects.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6174.003.png[/image\_path][/image-1]. For inter-band FDD + FDD UL CA**and inter-band TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA**, [CB014067-A] and inter-band  [End CB014067-A]when SCell reconfiguration including SCell addition, SCell release as well as SCell change/swap, gNB will not reconfigure [image-2][image\_desc]The image is entirely black, with no discernible features, text, or objects.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6174.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2], since dynamic power split solution is disabled (refer to [11119486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and not applied to inter-band FDD + FDD UL CA**and inter-band TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA**, [CB014067-A] and inter-band TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 + FDD FR1 UL CA, [End CB014067-A]** and there is no benefit due to separate MPR applied on each UL serving cell for inter-band UL CA (see 3GPP 38.101-1 chapter 6.2A.2.3).***\******\***
 
\* If a TPC <> 0dB has been sent, a TPC penalty timer is triggered and no new TPC <> 0dB can be sent until this penalty timer has expired.
\* The penalty timer is operator configurable by the new parameter “clpcPusch.tTpcPenalty"described in req. [11352892](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub6o2fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
\* When a ReTX is sent, the TPC value associated to it shall be the same one used during the corresponding NewTx; no penalty timer should be considered in such ReTx cases.
File: Drawings of PUSCH TPC to L1 by encoding DCI format 0\_1 and 1\_1.docs

#### 3.6.3.1.0-6 Closed Loop Power Control for PUSCH Timing skipping and mutual coordination of the computations (ID: 11119357)

**3.6.3.1.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `12807135`)

Closed Loop Power Control for PUSCH
The U-Plane can skip the PUSCH power control computation for UEs which have total buffered bytes = 0 **or fake data buffer raised by DRB priority Proactive Uplink Grant triggered([11204049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_rRmZAPvQEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**when the HARQ feedback is Dtx and its associated PUSCH transmission is triggered by one of the following conditions:\*\*\*\*

·    Low Priority Proactive Uplink Grant (sent only to simulate a "positive SR" with a smaller periodicity than the configured one in the UE) when Proactive Grant Type is  Skippable-Dynamic or Skippable-Dynamic-Enhanced (se [11195286: Low Priority Proactive Grants](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7J1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

·    Uplink grant requested by the L2-HI for DRB to speed up the reception of the RLC status (see [11203852: UL Grant for RLC Status PDU](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwhmxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), if the UE is configured with the RRC Information Element Skippable-Dynamic or Skippable-Dynamic-Enhanced.

·    UL grant triggered only for Time Alignment (TA) update (see [11195652: UL TA Grant Scheduling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv9mHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), if the UE is configured with Skippable-Dynamic or Skippable-Dynamic-Enhanced RRC IE.

·    TCP Boost Proactive Uplink Grant (see [11195403: TCP Boost Proactive Grant Scheduling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7w8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), if the UE is configured with Skippable-Dynamic or Skippable-Dynamic-Enhanced RRC IE

·    UL grant after the reception of a BSR equal to 0. It refers to the case when UL grant is sent just prior to have total buffered bytes = 0 due to delay in getting buffer status from L2-LO. The grant is sent but subsequent DTX due to grant being skipped by UE is ignored (see PR624410) if if the UE is configured with Skippable-Dynamic or Skippable-Dynamic-Enhanced RRC IE.

·    DRB priority Proactive Uplink Grant  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30332\_replaced([11195558](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv8_CfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

·    **DRAFT: UL Grant (DG) after proactive DC-GBR buffer increase with CG (see [11173454: Anticipative buffer correction in case that the opportunity of CG initial transmission is missed](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuTZNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)**

·    UL grant triggered by the false detection of a positive SR ([Before PR847304-26R1] false alarm is confirmed when the associated initial PUSCH transmission is Dtx [PR847304-26R1] as per [11114555](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpl4UfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)[End PR847304-26R1]) during DRX inactive time, if the rdFalseAlarmSrSkipPwrctrl is set to true (see [12718652: rdFalseAlarmSrSkipPwrCtrl](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VByAGuhEfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

·    Periodic Configured Grant (CG) PUSCH transmission, if the rdPeriodicCgDtxSkipPwrCtrl is true ([12718663: rdPeriodicCgDtxSkipPwrCtrl](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ekSEMGuiEfCRGai1q1VTeQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

When the PUSCH power control computation is skipped:

·    Force TPC to 0dB.

·    Skip the Target SINR calculation process (i.e. do not update the value) described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2638\_replaced([11119168](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

·    Skip the SINRUE\_AVE calculation (do not update).

When the PUSCH power control computation is triggered, the following procedure is applied:

·    Pathloss calculations of Requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2634\_replaced([11119109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be done per UE base and shall be done at most at every PHR reported by UE. If UE is scheduled regularly and often the PHR periodicity may be considered equivalent to the PL calculation periodicity.

·    Interference and Noise level is already reported by L1 at each slot and the average process described in Requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2636\_replaced([11119117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be, therefore, performed at each slot as well, while the delivery of the averaged value to the Target SINR calculation process for a given UE, described in Requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2638\_replaced([11119168](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), shall be done at each scheduling event of the given UE.

·    The TargetSINR-PUSCH  target SINR calculation for PUSCH, described in Requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2638\_replaced([11119168](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqIq6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), for a given UE shall be repeated at each scheduling event of the given UE, because at each scheduling event at least the I+N averaged values changes and regularly even PL may have been changed.

·    The calculations described in Requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2640\_replaced([11119228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) related to the calculation of the SINRUE\_AVE shall be repeated per scheduling event (i.e. at every time the given UE is scheduled these calculations shall be performed again).

·    The SINRUE\_AVE calculation, provided by requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2640\_replaced([11119228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), shall be passed to TPC calculation, described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2642\_replaced([11119253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), only if the time interval between this last calculation and the second last is smaller than a given time threshold defined by operator parameter  "clpcPusch.tIntervalSinrUpd", otherwise this is considered only as bases for the next possible SINRUE\_AVE calculation (in other words: the last SINRUE\_AVE calculation is kept for the further calculation but it is not passed to the TPC calculation process and TPC is forced to 0dB).

·    Once the above described actions have been done, at every scheduling event of a given UE, the TPC is calculated according to Requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2642\_replaced([11119253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) logic described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2642\_replaced([11119253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-2, if the constraints here described in above item 5 are satisfied, otherwise TPC is set to 0dB.

If the new calculated TPC is different from 0, it will be sent only if a TPC penalty timer "clpcPusch.tTpcPenalty" (that measures the time since the last TPC different from 0 has been sent) has been expired; otherwise, the TPC shall be forced to 0 (this limit has been added to avoid that the TPC reacts too nervously at each event and it is a kind of minimal period the system shall grant before a new effective TPC command is sent to UE).

The TPC penalty timer "clpcPusch.tTpcPenalty" for PUSCH is described in req. 5G\_UP\_5034\_replaced([11352892](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub6o2fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and, according to simulation performed, set to value 50ms has shown a better performance of the algorithm.

#### 3.6.3.1.0-7 Closed Loop Power Control for PUSCH Interference and noise term I (ID: 11119367)

**3.6.3.1.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11119370`)

Closed Loop Power Control for PUSCH
Interference and noise term I in 4RX

### 3.6.3.2 Closed Loop Power Control for PUCCH

#### 3.6.3.2.0-1 Closed Loop Power Control for PUCCH Received PUCCH SINR calculation (ID: 11119377)

**3.6.3.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11119382`)

Closed Loop Power Control for PUCCH
According to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1690\_replaced([11108782](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kovjxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) the estimate of PUCCH UL Received Power and according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1656\_replaced([11108410](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koqrRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) L1 the estimate of PUCCH Interference and Noise power are provided by L1 to 5G-L2-PS for long term averaging. This is done per each UE.

The above estimate are respetively called M5 and K2allocBW,and their values provided at each slot (where UE has sent data in UL) shall be first converted into logaritmic scale (if not already provided in that form) and then averaged over a sliding averaging window defined by parameter “clpcPucch.sinrAveMeasSamples” and set by operator.

Per each UE, the gNodeB shall then periodically calculate the effective received SINR for PUCCH: SINRreceived,Pucch.

The averaging method for the PUCCH signal component shall follow the one described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2640\_replaced([11119228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the averaging of PUSCH SINR.

However, the number of samples S is determined by a specifically PUCCH dedicated parameter “clpcPucch.sinrAveMeasSamples” and the update interval required mentioned in that requirement should be smaller than “clpcPucch.tIntervalSinrUpd” in the case of this PUCCH averaged SINR calculation (which is as well a PUCCH dedicated parameter).

In this way it is allowed to operator to set different averaging windows between PUCCH and PUSCH.

Note:

 Only the SR measures corresponding to positively received SR samples shall be utilized for the SINR computation of PUCCH

 [CB007103-B]The measurements of PUCCH F3 during transient phase with DMRS sequence reconfiguration (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22731\_replaced([11140896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krv0ffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall not be utilized for the SINR computation of PUCCH [End CB007103-B]

 The number of samples clpcPucch.sinrAveMeasSamples is the largest possible for the averaging window, but there are conditions (e.g. seldom scheduling of UE in UL, slow pacing of PUCCH) where this number can be smaller; consequently the average may be done on a smaller number of samples, because of the presence of samples that undergo to the following condition:

o if the last sample S is older than a given number of subframes (defined by a dedicated r&d parameter and set to 1000ms), all samples  are discarded;

o if the last sample update S comes after “clpcPucch.tIntervalSinrUpd” subframes, then all the samples but last are discarded.

 By extreme conditions, therefore, it may happen that the averaged value correspond to a single punctual value (one single sample to be averaged)

 Therefore, a minimal number of  3 samples S shall be required to consider meaningful the calculation of SINRreceived,Pucch(i); in case the value is calculated with less than 3 samples  the system shall generate automatically a TPC command = 0dB.)
