11119403:
Closed Loop Power Control for PUCCH
Restricted in uplink closed loop power control implementation:
1. DCI format 2\_2 is not supported
2. Dual state TPC is not supported
SINRreceived,Pucch is calculated as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2647\_replaced([11119377](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJ5BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and shall be express in dB.
 
Caculates PUCCH TPC when PDSCH is scheduled:
 
 DeltaPucch= TSINR\_PUCCH - SINRreceived,Pucch   (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3079\_replaced([11131196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krBbu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-1)
Where:
 
1. SINRreceived,Pucch  is provided in dB by req. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2647\_replaced([11119377](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJ5BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
2. TSINR\_PUCCH is the target PUCCH SINR value of parameter 'clpcPucch.targetSinr' configured by operator.
 
Indicates PUCCH TPC to L1 by encoding DCI format 1\_1 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4443\_replaced([11178081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku0Wk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) the logic is as follows:
 
 if (DeltaPucch ≤ DeltaSINR\_1) then (TPC= -1)
 else if (DeltaSINR\_1 < DeltaPucch ≤ DeltaSINR\_2) then (TPC= 0)
 else if (DeltaSINR\_2 < DeltaPucch ≤ DeltaSINR\_3) then (TPC= +1)
 else (TPC= 3)      (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3079\_replaced([11131196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krBbu_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-2)
[docx\_desc]
[/docx\_desc][docx\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/attachments/m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file6187\_0.docx[/docx\_path]
[PR815039]
If the measured RSSI (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1664\_replaced([11108492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kor5YfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal or larger than rdMaxRssiPucchCLPC (5G\_UP\_ALG\_33023\_replaced([11120134](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqOKdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the value TPC will be limited as following to avoid the risk of power saturation at antenna reception, which will cause a not desirable escalation in the UE power.
               TPCfinal = -1dB
[END PR815039]
 
Note:
\* DeltaSINR\_x are 3 predefined values that operator may choose by configuring the parameter clpcPucch.sinrThresholdIndex; the values shown in the above picture correspond to predefined triplet 1 (see req. 5G\_UP\_5035\_replaced([11352905](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub6o3PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Each pre-defined triplet sets the thresholds under or beyond those a given TPC command is sent to UE (specifically dedicated to PUCCH).
\* In case the value of the signal component in the SINRreceived,Pucch calculation was averaged over a single sample the TPC command is forced always to value TPC = 0dB (this is coherent with statement in item 2 of 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2651\_replaced([11119407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJ5C_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
\* Incremental PUCCH TPC commands shall be sent even when the reported PHR has negative values
\* If the a TPC <> 0dB has been sent, a TPC penalty timer is triggered and no new TPC <> 0dB can be sent until this penalty timer has expired.
\* The penalty timer is operator configurable by the new parameter “clpcPucch.tTpcPenalty" described in req. 5G\_UP\_5035\_replaced([11352905](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub6o3PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
 
\* PUCCH TPC commands shall be sent at every DL ReTX  maintaining the TPC value of the related NewTx. During the ReTx the penalty timer is not taken in consideration.

---

#### 3.6.3.2.0-3 Closed Loop Power Control for PUCCH Timing and mutual coordination of the calculations (ID: 11119407)

**3.6.3.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12791510`)

Closed Loop Power Control for PUCCH
1. Received SINR calculation for PUCCH, described in Requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2647\_replaced([11119377](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJ5BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), for a given UE shall be repeated at each PUCCH event of the given UE.

2. The  calculation, provided by requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2647\_replaced([11119377](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJ5BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), shall be passed to TPC calculation, described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2649\_replaced([11119386](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJ5B_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), only if the time interval between this last calculation and the second last is smaller than a given time threshold defined by operator parameter "clpcPucch.tIntervalSinrUpd"; otherwise, this is considered only as bases for the next possible SINRreceived,Pucch calculation (in other words: the last SINRreceived,Pucch calculation is kept for the further calculation but it is not passed to the TPC calculation process and TPC command for PUCCH is forced to 0).

3. Once the above described actions have been done, at [PR851714] ~~every~~ next [END PR851714] scheduling event of a given UE, the TPC is calculated according to Requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2649\_replaced([11119386](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJ5B_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) logic described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2649\_replaced([11119386](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJ5B_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))-2, if the constraints here described in above item 2 are satisfied, otherwise TPC is set to 0.

If the last calculated TPC is different from 0dB, it will be sent only if the TPC penalty timer (that measures the time since the last TPC different from 0dB has been sent) has been expired [PR851714] and at least one new measure has triggered a new SINR calculation for PUCCH;[END PR851714] otherwise, the TPC shall be forced to 0 (this limit has been added to avoid that the TPC reacts too nervously at each event and it is a kind of minimal period the system shall grant before a new effective TPC command is sent to UE).

The TPC penalty timer for PUCCH is described in req. 5G\_UP\_5035\_replaced([11352905](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub6o3PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and, according to simulation performed, set to value 50ms has shown a better performance of the algorithm and shall be used as first implementation.

4. If, after the execution of the above steps, it results that TPC value other than zero shall be transmitted, in case that the DL DCI 1\_1 corresponds to a BWP switch then the TPC shall be calculated as MAX (computed TPC, 0).

File: Drawings of PUSCH TPC to L1 by encoding DCI format 0\_1 and 1\_1.docs  
Folder: <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:f:/r/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Drawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G/User%20Plane?csf=1&web=1&e=V8ishU>

---

### 3.6.3.3 Closed Loop Power Control for SRS

#### 3.6.3.3.0-1 Closed Loop Power Control for SRS SRS TPC command determination (ID: 11119416)

**3.6.3.3.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13485356`)

Closed Loop Power Control for SRS
In the SRS power control equation 'hb,f,c(i,l)'  is the Closed Loop Power Control component.

According to 3GPP it is possible to configure SRS CLPC such that it has the same TPC command of PUSCH.

Therefore, with uplink closed loop power control feature, the term 'hb,f,c(i,l)' shall be equal to term 'fb,f,c(i,l)' calculated for PUSCH.

For NSA and SA, when (actUlClosedLoopPwrCtrl is set to ‘23’ or ‘123’) [05602058] AND [actSeparateSrsSrsCLPC (in cell configuration) equals to False] [End 05602058]:

Under this configurations PUSCH and SRS shall have the same CLPC correction and, therefore, the IE srs-optional PowerControlAdjustmentStates shall not be sent to obtain sameAs-Fci1 behavior”.

**Note:**

* For UEs with subband BF configured (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21269\_replaced([11156460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0yhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[CB010332-C] or for UEs with SRS for Positioning configured (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27467\_replaced([11157876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks-jh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** [End CB010332-C], SRS CLPC is not enabled for these UEs via setting srs-PowerControlAdjustmentStates as separateClosedLoop.\*\*\*\*

Please, refer to requirement 5G\_UP\_526\_replaced([11351195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubr_V_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_5310\_replaced([11363512](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZqkY_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and in particular to the requirement dedicated to IE srs-PowerControlAdjustmentStates 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_5350\_replaced([11363961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZuOxvvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (this IE is optional and it shall not be included when actUlClosedLoopPwrCtrl is set to ‘23’ or ‘123’).

---

### 3.6.3.4 Calculation of power offset between SRS and PUSCH?

#### 3.6.3.4.0-1 Calculation of power offset between SRS and PUSCH? Calculation of power offset between SRS and PUSCH (ID: 11119432)

**3.6.3.4.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `13019763`)

Calculation of power offset between SRS and PUSCH?
L2PS shall calculate powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe (also called P\_SRS\_Boost) as follows :​

If the first PHR has not been received yet, powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe is set to transmissionComb.

If PHR has been received,

If UE is scheduled with aperiodic SRS,

powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe = 10^((P\_SRS + 10 Log (transmissionComb)  –  P\_PUSCH\_Scaled) /10)

where,

- P\_PUSCH\_Scaled=min(P\_Cmax, P0\_PUSCH+10log(2^µ *n\_prb\_srs)+ alpha\_pusch* PL)

* P\_Cmax: Maximum UL transmission power received with the PHR​ refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2748\_replaced([11121531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYik_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ​Mapping to dBm value is based on 3GPP 38.133 Table 10.1.18.1-1
* P0\_PUSCH: as received in user setup​
* µ: SCS numerology​
* alpha\_pusch= (alpha+3)/10, if alpha != 0

=  0, otherwise,

- PL: Pathloss as calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2746\_replaced([11121446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYikPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

- n\_prb\_srs: SRS bandwidth obtained from SRS configuration of the user.

Hypothesis to compute the offset is that SRS is used as reference for the number of PRBs

For aperiodic SRS, **L2 shall perform rrmSinrCorrection based on SRS PRB numbers (to replace rrmNumPuschPrb [i,j,t] with SRS PRB numbers in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9935\_replaced([11130229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq_mgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and calculate rrmAvgSinrUl  considering MPR ( based on SRS PRB bandwidth and position to calculate MPR in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3078\_replaced([11130719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krANl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

If UE is scheduled with periodic SRS,

powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe = 10^((P\_SRS + 10 Log (transmissionComb \*\*\* n\_prb\_pusch/ n\_prb\_srs)  –  P\_PUSCH) /10)\*\*

where,

- P\_PUSCH=min(P\_Cmax, P0\_PUSCH+10log(2^µ *n\_prb\_pusch)+ alpha\_pusch* PL +rrmAdjustedAccumulatedTpcPO)

* P\_Cmax: Maximum UL transmission power received with the PHR​ refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2748\_replaced([11121531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYik_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ​Mapping to dBm value is based on 3GPP 38.133 Table 10.1.18.1-1
* P0\_PUSCH: as received in user setup​
* µ: SCS numerology​
* alpha\_pusch= (alpha+3)/10, if alpha != 0

=  0, otherwise,

- PL: Pathloss as calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2746\_replaced([11121446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYikPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* n\_prb\_pusch :  last PUSCH scheduled in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5026\_replaced([11201742](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwZD4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or **(for C8 subcells and rdCompensateIrcGain=true (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19667\_replaced([11141270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**from last PUSCH transmission (i.e. final stage of all scheduling decisions 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5026\_replaced([11201742](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwZD4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5108\_replaced([11203573](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwfxlPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ...)\*\*\*\*

-  rrmAdjustedAccumulatedTpcPO:

If (NRBTS/NRCELL/actUlClosedLoopPwrCtrl is puschSrs or pucchPuschSrs):

L2-PS shall keep the accumulated δ\_srs that is sum of δ\_srs that is indicated by the non-DTX PUSCH TPC (not TPC comment field) for this UE on the BWP of periodic SRS. \*\*\* Note for periodic SRS for positioning the BWP can be dedicated BWP or power saving BWP (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1872\_replaced([11111200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*

\*For UEs with SRS for SB BF configured (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21269\_replaced([11156460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0yhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) OR for UEs with SRS for Positioning configured (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27467\_replaced([11157876](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks-jh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [05602058] OR actSeparateSrsCLPC (in cell configuration) equals to True [End 05602058]:

rrmAdjustedAccumulatedTpcPO is accumulated δ\_srs and cut within range -rdMaxAccumulatedTpcPO(5G\_UP\_ALG\_27300\_replaced([11120145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqOKd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to + rdMaxAccumulatedTpcPO;

~~\*For UEs with SRS for WB BF configured:~~

~~rrmAdjustedAccumulatedTpcPO is 0.~~

For all else cases, rrmAdjustedAccumulatedTpcPO is 0.

Hypothesis to compute the offset is that PUSCH is used as reference for the number of PRBs . For periodic SRS, L2 shall perform rrmSinrCorrection based on rmNumPuschPrb[i,j,t]=n\_prb\_pusch in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9935\_replaced([11130229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq_mgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and calculate rrmAvgSinrUl considering MPR based on PUSCH PRB bandwidth and position to calculate MPR in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3078\_replaced([11130719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krANl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For both periodic and aperiodic SRS, P\_SRS is computed as follows:

- P\_SRS = min (P\_Cmax , P0\_SRS + 10Log (2^µ \* n\_prb\_srs) + alpha\_srs\* PL)​

- P0\_SRS: P0 for **[CB015640-A] codebook**[End CB015640-A] SRS, refer to 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_5286\_replaced([11362984](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZm6B_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))\*\*\*\*

- µ: SCS numerology​

- alpha\_srs  = (alpha+3)/10, if alpha != 0

= 0, otherwise,

- PL: Pathloss as calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2746\_replaced([11121446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqYikPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

- n\_prb\_srs: as obtained from SRS configuration of the user

- transmissionComb: TransmissionComb for SRS, refer to 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_5286\_replaced([11362984](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wZm6B_vjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note: Power DIFF (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21401\_replaced([11157103](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for evaluation of SRS configuration for SB BF  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21269\_replaced([11156460](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks0yhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is considered later in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2140\_replaced([11154089](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqafPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It is known that for UEs with SB BF the powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe is not optimized because accumulated TPC is not accurate when CLPC is enabled for PUSCH but disabled for periodic SRS. It is also known that accumulated TPC should be maintained per BWP and reset according to 3GPP’s definition and aperiodic SRS branch is also impacted but these will be followed by later task due to effort reason.

5G-L2-PS shall compensate the IRC gain if the functionality is enabled; **For SRS received with  4, 8 or 16** streams **cf. 5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and when**NRCELL\ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGain =true***\****\*

as follows :

**Step A:** 5G-L2-PS shall compute **srs\_boost\_wo\_irc\_gain=powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe to be used in step D in case powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe capping occurs.**\*\*\*\*

Step B: **5G-L2-PS shall compute powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe inclusing IRC gain :**

powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe = powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe **/ 10^(rrmSrsIrcGain/10)**

please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19671\_replaced([11140233](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rrmSrsIrcGain computation.

Step C: **5G-L2-PS shall compute powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe inclusing IRC gain**

powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe = max( rdUlSrsPowerOffsetMin, min (powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe, rdUlSrsPowerOffsetMax)),

where rdUlSrsPowerOffsetMin and rdUlSrsPowerOffsetMax are decribed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24313\_replaced([11141470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24311\_replaced([11141458](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krze0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Step D :  In case of capping, L2 shall compute rrmSrsIrcGain after capping:

- Either rrmSrsIrcGainAfterCapping  = 10\*log10(srs\_boost\_wo\_irc\_gain/rdUlSrsPowerOffsetMax) to be used in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19678\_replaced([11140301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19680\_replaced([11140371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe is capped with maximum value ;

- Or  rrmSrsIrcGainAfterCapping = 10\*log10(srs\_boost\_wo\_irc\_gain/rdUlSrsPowerOffsetMin) to be used in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19678\_replaced([11140301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19680\_replaced([11140371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe is capped with minimum value;

Note2: transmissionComb: NRCELL/srsForBeamMgmt-comb.

Note3: The formula of the powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe is unchanged with introduction of closed loop power control as long as PUSCH and SRS receives the same TPC commands cf. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2654\_replaced([11119416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJ5DvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

Note4: After initialized from cell setup, P0\_PUSCH and P0\_SRS can be updated by P0\_Nominal\_PUSCH and P0\_Nominal\_SRS per slice-based uplink power control cf. 5G\_UP\_12374\_replaced([11353014](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub728vvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_13916\_replaced([11270513](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_To9dVfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

​The Value of powerOffsetSrsToPuschPerAllocatedRe shall be included in the UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message.

---

#### 3.6.3.4.0-2 Calculation of power offset between SRS and PUSCH? Calculation of power boost for PUSCH (ID: 11119457)

**3.6.3.4.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11119472`)

Calculation of power offset between SRS and PUSCH?
5G-L2-PS shall compute  PBoost  for PUSCH reception and send it to 5G-L1-UL for the SNR and TPMI calculation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6716\_replaced([11103708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knzvpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as follows :

1. For UL subcells configured with [CB013202-A] 4, [End CB013202-A] 8 or 16 spatial streams (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and  [Before CB013202-A] rdCompensateIrcGain = true (cf. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19667\_replaced([11141270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  [CB013202-A] NRCELL\ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGain =true  [End CB013202-A],

[CB013202-C]

If NRCELL.actUlMuMimo=true and NRCELL.actPmiSinrUlMuMimo=true,

DU shall compute PBoost  ( linear scale) equal to number of cdm groups without data / 10^( max(min(rrmPuschIrcGain, rdUlPuschIrcGainMax),rdUlPuschIrcGainMin ) /10)

 rdUlPuschIrcGainMin 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31204\_replaced([11141444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3zvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),  in case of actual capping to maximum or minimum value before Pboost transmission then capped value rdUlPuschIrcGainMax or rdUlPuschIrcGainMin  should be used in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19677\_replaced([11140280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19679\_replaced([11140353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

else [End CB013202-C]

DU shall compute PBoost  ( linear scale) equal to number of cdm groups without data / 10^( min(rrmPuschIrcGain, rdUlPuschIrcGainMax) /10)

  rdUlPuschIrcGainMax described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24309\_replaced([11141429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kry3zPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),  in case of actual capping to maximum value before Pboost transmission then capped value rdUlPuschIrcGainMax should be used in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19677\_replaced([11140280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19679\_replaced([11140353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krtYO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB013202-C] or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30787\_replaced([11140179](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB013202-C]

with :

 cdm group without data (3GPP section 38.214 6.2.2) configured in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3098\_replaced([11137832](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krbravvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = longTermDiff [End CB013202-C]

 rrmPuschIrcGain is computed from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19670\_replaced([11140163](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB013202-C] When NRCELL.ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGainMethod = shortTermDiff

 rrmPuschIrcGain is computed from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30791\_replaced([11140190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB013202-C]

For PUSCH received with [CB013202-A] 4, [End CB013202-A] 8 or 16 streams cf. 5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and when [Before CB013202-A] rdCompensateIrcGain = false (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19667\_replaced([11141270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB013202-A] NRCELL\ulSuMimoEnh.enhRankSelectIrcGain =false  [End CB013202-A] or fake UEs (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17489\_replaced([11215719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxU4CvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) no matter rdCompensateIrcGain (cf. 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19667\_replaced([11141270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kryQvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true or false, PBoost  ( linear scale) equals to cdm group without data.

1. For other subcells , PBoost  ( linear scale) shall be set to INVALID value. INVALID value shall be chosen as 0.

UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
For a UE configured with FR1 inter-band UL CA, since MPR is applied to inter-band UL CA by UE according to chapter 6.2A.2.3 of 38.101-1, to schedule all available PUSCH on both PCell and SCell can achieve better performance according to shannon theory, comparing with dynamic power split solution descirbed below. Then UE TX power shall not be split dynamically in UL overlapping slots, and all available PRBs can be allocated for PUSCH on both PCell and [CB014067-A] each active [End CB014067-A] SCell  in any UL slot.

Note:

* If actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to FALSE, OR (actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE AND 5QI1 DRB is not configured for the UE)

For FDD + TDD FR1 R15 UL CA UE or inter-band FDD + FDD UL CA UE or (inter-band TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA UE with PPowerClass,PCell for TDD PCell equal to or less than PPowerClass,CA), [CB014067- A] or  (inter-band  UL CA UE with PPowerClass,PCell for TDD PCell equal to or less than PPowerClass,CA)[End CB014067-A] in case transform precoder is enabled on PCell and [image-0][image\_desc]$\tilde{P}\_{\text{CMAX,PCell}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-10291203.png[/image\_path][/image-0] is equal to PCMAX, UL transmission shall be suspended on SCell [CB014067-A] (on two SCells for 3CC) [End CB014067-A] ,referring to [11122349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

Else if (actForcedDftSOfdmVonrUl is set to TRUE AND 5QI1 DRB is configured for the UE)

* For FDD + TDD FR1 R15 UL CA UE or inter-band FDD + FDD UL CA UE or inter-band TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA UE [CB014067-A] or TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 + FDD FR1 UL CA UE [End CB014067-A], with PPowerClass,PCell for TDD PCell equal to or less than PPowerClass,CA), in case transform precoder is enabled on PCell and [image-1][image\_desc]$\tilde{P}\_{\text{CMAX,PCell}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-10291203.png[/image\_path][/image-1] is equal to PCMAX, UL transmission shall be suspended on [CB014067-A] each active [End CB014067-A] SCell, if the rrmUlProposedMcs in PCell (as per [11131696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krD38vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the UE is less than rdTpEnabledScellStateCheckLowerMcsThresh.
* For FDD + TDD FR1 R15 UL CA UE or inter-band FDD + FDD UL CA UE or inter-band TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 UL CA UE,  [CB014067-A] or in 3CC  TDD +TDD +FDD UL CA UE [End CB014067-A] with PPowerClass,PCell for TDD PCell equal to or less than PPowerClass,CA), in case transform precoder is enabled on PCell and [image-2][image\_desc]$\tilde{P}\_{\text{CMAX,PCell}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-10291203.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is equal to PCMAX, UL transmission shall be triggered on  [CB014067-A] each active [End CB014067-A] SCell, if the rrmUlProposedMcs in PCell (as per [11131696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krD38vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the UE is greater than or equal to  rdTpEnabledScellStateCheckUpperMcsThresh

Where:

* [image-3][image\_desc]$\tilde{P}\_{\text{CMAX,PCell}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-10291203.png[/image\_path][/image-3] and PCMAX refer to [11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), and shall be converted to the same unit for comparison.
* rrm64qamTpMcs is defined in [11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
* PPowerClass,PCelland PPowerClass,CArefer to [11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
* rdTpEnabledScellStateCheckUpperMcsThresh is defined in [12693931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_l0x8cFjBEfCIAJ9nOfeS0w)
* rdTpEnabledScellStateCheckLowerMcsThresh is defined in [12693922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZMSnZFjAEfCIAJ9nOfeS0w)
* For TDD FR1 + FDD UL CA UE, [CB014067-A] or in 3CC: TDD FR1 + TDD FR1 + FDD FR1 UL CA UE, in the 2CC [End CB014067-A] the UE shall be scheduled in TDD PCell only [CB014067-A] and in 3CC in any TDD Cell [End CB014067-A] in UL overlapping slots except UE which is selected into allow-list (refer to [11208767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwwQQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or is configured with simultaneousPUCCH-PUSCH-SamePriority-r17  ~~parallelTxPUCCH-PUSCH-SamePriority-r17~~. Rationale: according to 38.213 chapter 9, k1 shall be greater than k2 if A/N is multiplexed in corresponding PUSCH. Based on current k1min on FR1 TDD cell and k2 on FDD cell, it may cause issue for A/N multiplexing in PUSCH on FDD SCell, if PUSCH is scheduled on FDD SCell in UL overlapping slots.
* k1min refers to [11116112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp1I5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ);
* k2 refers to [11116264](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp2XB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ);

For a UE configured with FR1 intra-band UL CA, in case transmission buffer is split in UL between PCell and [CB014067-A] each active [End CB014067-A] SCell  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10377\_replaced([11122349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), MPR can't be known for the scheduling since L2PS on one serving cell can’t know whether UE is scheduled on the other serving cell in the same slot before the scheduling, then dynamic power split solution doesn't apply and all available PUSCH can be scheduled on both PCell and SCell. Please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10377\_replaced([11122349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for suspending/resuming UL scheduling on SCell.

An UL overlapping slot is defined as an UL slot on a serving cell overlapping with at least one UL slot which is not muted according to [11114713](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpnGfvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) on another serving cell on air, otherwise, it's an UL non-overlapping slot.

[CB014067-A] Note: Following the implementation of CNI-137616-B, dynamic TX power functionality has been removed from all features. As a result, 3CC UL UE does not incorporate this capability.[End CB014067-A]

The non power limited TX power per PRB means PUSCH transmission power per PRB UE delivers before UE reaches power limitation. The PHR report contains the power headroom (PH) and the max power per CC (PCMAX,c). In addition, the number of PRBs used to transmit the PHR report is known. According to 3GPP 38.213 Chapter 7.1.1, the non power limited TX power per PRB is calculated as below:

If PHR report is based on a real transmission (V = 0)

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

else if PHR report is based on a reference format (V = 1)

[Before PR668422]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[PR668422]

if (cell c is SCell and it's the 1st PHR report after SCell activation and PH is POWER\_HEADROOM\_63) [PR683687] or

(for cell c, last rdNumOfConsecVPHR63 PHR reports including the current one are all based on a reference format and PH is POWER\_HEADROOM\_63 in each of these reports) [End PR683687]

[image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

else

[image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

if PH is POWER\_HEADROOM\_63

[image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

Note:

* Rationale for POWER\_HEADROOM\_63 handling: PH for PHR based on reference format is calculated based on P0\_PUSCH(j=0) which is possibly configured with a value much less than P0\_PUSCH(j=2), then POWER\_HEADROOM\_63 for PHR report based on a reference format can be reported easily. Since POWER\_HEADROOM\_63 corresponds to PH>=38 according to chapter 10.1.17 of 38.133, nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB can't be calculated accurately in case POWER\_HEADROOM\_63 is reported in PHR report based on a reference format.
* SRI-PUSCH-PowerControl is not supported yet, according to 3gpp 38.213 Chapter 7.1.1, if SRI-PUSCH-PowerControl is not provided to the UE, parameter set configuration j = 2 for PUSCH transmission with grant.
* Currently P0-PUSCH-AlphaSetId = 0 defined in 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_10000\_replaced([11350319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wX4btPvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), pusch-PathlossReferenceRS-Id = 0 defined in 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_4064\_replaced([11350352](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wX4buvvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and PUSCH power control adjustment state l = 0 defined in 5G\_CP\_IF\_RRC\_4082\_replaced([11350270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_wX30rfvjEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are used for PHR report based on real PUSCH transmission. According to Chapter 7.7.1 of 38.213, for a Type 1 power headroom report based on a reference transmission, [image-5][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]is obtained using [image-6][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6], p0-PUSCH-AlphaSetId = 0, pusch-PathlossReferenceRS-Id = 0, and PUSCH power control adjustment state l = 0 are always used, so the gap for nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB based on real PHR and virtual PHR is [image-7][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7].

[End PR668422]

Where:

-  V refers to 38.321 Chapter 6.1.3.9;

-  i: UE index;

-  c: cell index;

-  [image-8][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8]: numerology of serving cell c;

-  [image-9][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9]: Time the latest PHR of serving cell c is received;

-  [image-10][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10]: [image-11][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.012.png[/image\_path][/image-11] of UE i in serving cell c at time [image-12][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6221.013.png[/image\_path][/image-12] in the PHR report;

For a UE configured with FR1 Ul CA, split TX power shall be initialized on Pcell and Scell for the below cases:

 Case1: First time UE transmission buffer split is started after Scell activation;

 Case2: UE transmission buffer split is started after rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower milliseconds since UE transmission buffer split is stopped specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10919\_replaced([11119940](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

 Case3: First time UE transmission buffer split is started after Ul scheduling is resumed on Scell in Ul overlapping slots specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10923\_replaced([11119968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

 Case4: Ul scheduling is resumed for a UE configured with FDD + FR1 TDD UL CA on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10923\_replaced([11119968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

 **[CB006137-BB] Case5: Ul Scell is recovered from overheating status specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2874\_replaced([11123313](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiThPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** [End CB006137-BB]\*\*\*\*

For Case 1 and Case2 **[CB006137-BB] and Case5** [End CB006137-BB], initial split TX power on Pcell and Scell is calculated as below:\*\*\*\*

-  [image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3], ***\*Note: the unit for [image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]is mW,  [image-5][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]and [image-6][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6]shall be converted to mW from dBm for the calculation.***\*

For Case 3 and case 4, initial split TX power on Pcell and Scell is calculated as below:

**[Before CB006137-BC]**

[image-10][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10]

**[CB006137-BC]**

if it's case 4 (Note: It's PCell resume, for case 4, j is PCell, and k is SCell)

pwrAfterResuming = max{rdMinSplitTxPower, convertToMw[nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB(i, j, t) + maxTpc]  x minNumPrbsUl(j)} + rdNumOfPwrAdjStepForResumeCheck x ueSplitPowerAdjStep;

else if it's case 3 (Note: It's SCell resume, for case 3, j is SCell, and k is PCell)

pwrAfterResuming = rdMinSplitTxPower + rdNumOfPwrAdjStepForResumeCheck x ueSplitPowerAdjStep;

**[End CB006137-BC]**

[image-11][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.012.png[/image\_path][/image-11]

[image-12][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.013.png[/image\_path][/image-12]

initialSplitTxPower(i, k, t) = [image-13][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.014.png[/image\_path][/image-13]- rdUePowerReserved - initialSplitTxPower(i, j, t);

Where:

-  rdMinInitSplitTxPower is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10926\_replaced([11119985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  rdMinSplitTxPower is R&D parameter, and refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10942\_replaced([11120009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

**[CB006137-BC]**

-  convertToMw is to convert dBm to mW;

* nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10873\_replaced([11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  maxTpc is 3 dB which is the maximum TPC value (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2642\_replaced([11119253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to prevent ping pong for CLPC; with OLPC, maxTpc is 0 dB;

-  minNumPrbsUl(j) is the minimal allowed PRBs on cell j, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

**[End CB006137-BC]**

-  rdNumOfPwrAdjStepForResumeCheck is R&D parameter, and refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11215\_replaced([11120042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8W_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  ueSplitPowerAdjStep is NIDD parameter on Pcell, and shall be converted to mW from dBm;

-  i, t, [image-14][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.015.png[/image\_path][/image-14] and  rdUePowerReserved are same as above;

-  j, k are cell index, for Case 3, j is Scell, and k is Pcell, for Case 4, j is Pcell, and k is Scell;

-  [image-15][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.016.png[/image\_path][/image-15]and  [image-16][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.017.png[/image\_path][/image-16]refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10873\_replaced([11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

Every time the split TX power is initialized for UE i on both Pcell and Scell, UE i is initialized in non over power state.

**Note:**

* The unit for initialSplitTxPower is mW, [image-17][image\_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6223.018.png[/image\_path][/image-17] shall be converted to mW from dBm for the calculation.
* Split TX power shall be initialized based on case2 on Pcell and Scell, if UE transmission buffer split is started after rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower milliseconds since UE transmission buffer split is stopped, regardless of case3 or case4.

Efficiency per PRB means the number of bits per milliwatt for one PRB UE delivers and is defined as below:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6225.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6225.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Where:

-  i: UE index;

-  t: Time the calculation relates to;

-  [image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6225.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

-  j: cell index;

-  TBS computation is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5084\_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  rrmMaxNumPuschPrb(j) is the number of PRBs available for PUSCH in the particular bandwidth system on cell j;

-  corrected MCS(i,j,t) is calculated according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5016\_replaced([11201086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwULYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with rrmNumPuschPrb set to Max[maxPrbBasedOnSplitTxPower, 1];

-  maxPrbBasedOnSplitTxPower refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10883\_replaced([11119896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  rank(i,j,t): MIMO layer;

-  nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB(i,j,t) refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10873\_replaced([11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and shall be converted from dBm to mW;

-  weightRatioOfUePwrScellVsPcell is NIDD parameter on Pcell.

UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
For a UE configured with FR1 Ul CA, split TX power adjustment step is defined as below:

If UE is in over power state

Choose cell j0 with the biggest efficiencyPerPRB(i, j0, t);

splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep(i, j0, t) = ueSplitPowerAdjStep;

split TX power adjustment step for cell j1 as below:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6227.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

else

splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep(i, Pcell, t) = ueSplitPowerAdjStep;

splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep(i, Scell, t) = ueSplitPowerAdjStep;

Where:

-  i: UE index;

-  t: time the calculation relates to;

-  ueSplitPowerAdjStep is NIDD parameter on Pcell, and shall be converted to mW from dBm;

-  rdMinSplitTxPowerAdjStep is R&D parameter, defines the minimum split power adjustment step, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10935\_replaced([11119990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

Split TX Power adjustment step for UE i on Pcell and Scell shall be updated in the below cases:

 UE i is switched to over power state from non over power state, or to non over power state from over power state.

 Every time PHR report is received and UE i is in over power state.

-  Evaluating whether an FR1 UL CA UE is in over power state refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10903\_replaced([11119931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuP_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

* The unit for splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep is mW.

11119892:
UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
For a UE configured with FR1 UL CA, if one Ul scheduling on any cell j in an Ul overlapping slot requires more power than the given split power, then the split TX power is adjusted as below from the next slot:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6230.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

splitTxPower(i,j,t+1) = splitTxPower(i,j,t) + splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep(i,j,t);

splitTxPower(i,k,t+1) = splitTxPower(i,k,t) - splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep(i,j,t); (k != j)

Where:

-  i is UE index;

-  j, k are cell index;

-  t: Time the calculation relates to;

-  splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10877\_replaced([11119861](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  rdUePowerReserved is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10938\_replaced([11119997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  rdMinSplitTxPower is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10942\_replaced([11120009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  [image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6230.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10879\_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  [image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6230.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10873\_replaced([11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  Checking whether UE requires more power than the split TX power refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10890\_replaced([11119904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

**Note:**

* The unit for splitTxPower is mW, and [image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6230.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] shall be converted to mW from dBm for the calculation.
* In case the PRBs for retransmission is above maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on a cell in an Ul overlapping slot, the split TX power shall not increase by one step on the cell.
* According to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10919\_replaced([11119940](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), in case UE transmission buffer split is stopped, in the first rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower milliseconds since the UE transmission buffer split is stopped, split tx power shall not be adjusted between PCell and SCell.

**[CB006137-C]**

* The split TX power shall not be adjusted between PCell and SCell in case the UE is considered to require more power than the split Tx Power based on the scheduling on a severing cell in an Ul non overlapping slot (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10890\_replaced([11119904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[End CB006137-C]**

-  rrmMaxNumPuschPrb(j) is the number of PRBs available for PUSCH in the particular bandwidth system on cell j.

#### 3.6.4.0-11 UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA Check whether UE requires more power than the split TX power (ID: 11119904)

[Before CB006137-C]

For a UE configured with FR1 UL CA, the UE is considered to require more power than the given split TX power on a serving cell in the below cases:

* Case1: The UE can't be forwarded to FD scheduler for initial transmission due to the limitation of maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on the cell in an Ul overlapping slot according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4871\_replaced([11196450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwCepPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Case2: No more PRBs can be allocated for initial transmission to the UE due to the limitation of maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on the cell in an Ul overlapping slot according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5010\_replaced([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4999\_replaced([11199901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwQhDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB006137-C]

For a UE configured with FR1 UL CA in power split mode (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10871\_replaced([11119486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* The UE is considered to require more power than the given split TX power on PCell in an Ul overlapping slot in the below cases:
* Case1: The UE can't be forwarded to FD scheduler for initial transmission due to the limitation of maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on PCell in an Ul overlapping slot according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4871\_replaced([11196450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwCepPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Case2: No more PRBs can be allocated for initial transmission to the UE due to the limitation of maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on PCell in an Ul overlapping slot according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5010\_replaced([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_UP\_ALG\_4999\_replaced([11199901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwQhDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and for the UE configured with FR1 Ul inter-band CA,  [image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6235.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0];
* The UE is considered to require more power than the given split TX power on SCell in an Ul overlapping slot in the below case:
* Case1: More PRBs than maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower are allocated for initial transmission to the UE on SCell in an Ul overlapping slot and for the UE configured with FR1 Ul inter-band CA, [image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6235.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1];
* The UE is considered to require more power than the split TX power based on the scheduling on a serving cell in an Ul non overlapping slot as below:

If the number of scheduled PRBs for initial transmission is above maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on the serving cell in the Ul non overlapping slot and for the UE configured with FR1 Ul inter-band CA,[image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6235.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2];

Where:

-  maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10883\_replaced([11119896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  i is the UE's index;

-  j is the cell index;

-  t is the Ul overlapping slot in question;

-  [image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6235.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3], [image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6235.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]and [image-5][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6235.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10873\_replaced([11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  MPR and DeltaMPR256QAM refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11120\_replaced([11130873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krA0p_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  convertToMw is to convert dBm to mW;

[End CB006137-C]

Note:

* if maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower is equal to rrmMaxNumPuschPrb (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10883\_replaced([11119896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) on a cell, the UE is always considered to be satisfied with the given split TX power on the cell.

#### 3.6.4.0-12 UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA Evaluate whether UE is in over power state (ID: 11119931)

**3.6.4.0-12.0-2**  (ID: `11119937`)

UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
For a UE configured with FR1 Ul CA, L2PS on Pcell evaluates whether the UE is in over power state periodically when [Before CB006137-C]UE TX power is split on Pcell and Scell in Ul overlapping slots [CB006137-C] UE is in power split mode (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10871\_replaced([11119486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB006137-C].

if the UE is in non over power state currently

In an evaluation period (rdPeriodForOverPowerEva) for the UE:

condition1: More power than the split TX power is required on Pcell in at least one Ul  [Before CB006137-C] overlapping slot or the number of scheduled PRBs for initial transmission is above maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on Pcell in at least one Ul non overlapping slot, if there are Ul non overlapping slots on Pcell [CB006137-C] slot [End CB006137-C].

condition2: More power than the split TX power is required on Scell in at least one Ul [Before CB006137-C] overlapping slot, or the number of scheduled PRBs for initial transmission is above maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on Scell in at least one Ul non overlapping slot, if there are Ul non overlapping slots on Scell [CB006137-C] slot  [End CB006137-C].

if condition1 and condition2 meet

UE enters over power state;

else

UE keeps in non over power state;

else

In rdNumForNonOverPowerCheck consecutive evaluation periods (rdPeriodForOverPowerEva) for the UE:

condition1: No more power than the split TX power is required on Pcell in any Ul [Before CB006137-C] overlapping slot, and the number of scheduled PRBs for initial transmission is not above maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on Pcell in any Ul non overlapping slot, if there are Ul non overlapping slots on Pcell [CB006137-C] slot [End CB006137-C].

condition2: No more power than the split TX power is required on Scell in any Ul [Before CB006137-C] overlapping slot, and the number of scheduled PRBs for initial transmission is not above maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on Scell in any Ul non overlapping slot, if there are Ul non overlapping slots on Scell [CB006137-C] slot [End CB006137-C].

[Before CB006137-C]

condition3: There is no scheduling for initial transmission on Pcell in any Ul slot and no more power than the split TX power is required on Pcell in any Ul overlapping slot.

condition4: There is no scheduling for initial transmission on Scell in any Ul slot and no more power than the split TX power is required on Scell in any Ul overlapping slot.

[End CB006137-C]

if condition1 or condition2 [Before CB006137-C] or condition3 or condition4 [End CB006137-C] meets

UE enters non over power state;

Else

UE keeps in over power state;

Where:

* rdPeriodForOverPowerEva is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11993\_replaced([11120016](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8U_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Checking whether UE need more power than the split TX power in Ul overlapping slots [CB006137-C] and Ul non overlapping slots [End CB006137-C] refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10890\_replaced([11119904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10883\_replaced([11119896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* rdNumForNonOverPowerCheck is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10944\_replaced([11120023](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8VfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.6.4.0-13 UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA Adjust UE TX power on Pcell while UE transmission buffer split is stopped (ID: 11119940)

**3.6.4.0-13.0-2**  (ID: `11119947`)

UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
For a UE configured with FR1 UL CA, while UE transmission buffer split is stopped, UE TX power is adjusted on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots as below:

If UE transmission buffer split is stopped due to Scell release or Scell change [CB006137-C] or Scell swap [End CB006137-C] or Scell overheating (5G\_UP\_ALG\_2871\_replaced([11123293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqiTgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If Ul scheduling is suspended on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Ul scheduling shall be resumed on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots;

The UE shall be scheduled without the limitation of split TX power on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots, and the split TX power update on Pcell and Scell shall be stopped.

else

In the first rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower milliseconds since the UE transmission buffer split is stopped:

if Ul scheduling is not suspended on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots

PRBs for initial transmission shall be capped by maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots, but the split TX power on Pcell and Scell shall not be adjusted.

Note:

-  Split TX power is still reserved for retransmission on Scell.

After rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower milliseconds since the UE transmission buffer split is stopped:

If Ul scheduling is suspended on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Ul scheduling shall be resumed on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots;

The UE shall be scheduled without the limitation of split TX power on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots, and the split TX power update on Pcell and Scell shall be stopped.

-  maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10883\_replaced([11119896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-  rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower is R&D parameter, and refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10946\_replaced([11120029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8V_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

* In case Scell is not deactivated or released after UE transmission buffer split is stopped:

If UE transmission buffer split is started in the first rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower milliseconds since the UE transmission buffer split is stopped

If Ul scheduling is suspended on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The UE shall be scheduled without the limitation of split TX power on Scell in Ul overlapping slots, and the split TX power update on Pcell and Scell shall be stopped.

else

The respective latest split TX power shall be applied on Pcell and Scell.

else if UE transmission buffer split is started after rdTimerForReinitSplitTxPower milliseconds since the UE transmission buffer split is stopped

split TX power is reinitialized on Pcell and Scell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10879\_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* triggers of transmission buffer split refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10281\_replaced([11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* condition of transmission buffer split refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9496\_replaced([11122831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqgeXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

---

#### 3.6.4.0-14 UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA Suspend Ul scheduling in overlapping slots on a cell due to too low split TX power (ID: 11119951)

**3.6.4.0-14.0-2**  (ID: `11119964`)

UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
11119964:

11119964:
UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
11119964:
UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
11119964:
UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
11119964:
UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
11119964:
UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
11119964:
UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
11119964:
UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
11119964:
UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
For a UE configured with FR1 UL CA, Ul scheduling shall be suspended for the UE on serving cell j1 in Ul overlapping slots due to too low split TX power.

Condition1: the UE is in over power state and

More power than the split TX power is required on cell j0 in Ul overlapping slot t and

splitTxPower(i,j0,t) + splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep(i,j0, t) > Pcmax(i, t) – rdUePowerReserved - rdMinSplitTxPower and[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black. There is no discernible content, text, or objects.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6244.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[Before PR683687]

Condition2: More power than the split TX power is required on cell j0 in Ul overlapping slot t-1 and

convertToMw[nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB(i, j1, t) + TPC(i, j1) to be transmitted] \* minNumPrbsUl(j1) > max{splitTxPower(i, j1, t), rdMinSplitTxPower};

[PR683687]

Condition2: The UE is in over power state and

More power than the split TX power is required on cell j0  in Ul overlapping slot t-1 and

maxPrbBasedOnSplitTxPower(i, j1, t) is below minNumPrbsUl(j1) and

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black. There is no discernible content, text, or objects.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6244.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Condition3:

The UE is in power split mode and

maxPrbBasedOnSplitTxPower(i, j1, t) is below minNumPrbsUl(j1) for the latest rdNumOfMaxPrbBasedOnSplitPwrCheck (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19298\_replaced([11120060](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqNjYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) checks; note: The check is executed, every time PHR report for cell j1 is received and UE is in power split mode. If UE exits power split mode, the check shall be stopped and counter shall be reset to 0.

[End PR683687]

[Before CB006137-C]

note: To reduce efforts and complexity of implementation, for condition2, cell j1 is only applied to PCell in CB006137-BC to keep the same as CB006137-C, since PRBs allocated for PUSCH are not capped by maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower on Scell in Ul overlapping slots in CB006137-C.

[CB006137-C]

Note: For condition2 [PR683687] and condition3 [End PR683687], cell j0 is only applied to SCell and cell j1 is only applied to PCell, since PRBs allocated for PUSCH are capped by maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower only on PCell in Ul overlapping slots.

[End CB006137-C]

If condition1 or condition2 [PR683687] or condition3 [End PR683687] meets

It's considered that the split TX power is too low on cell j1;

if cell j1 is Scell

if UE transmission buffer split is started

if there are only Ul overlapping slots on Scell for UE i

UE transmission buffer split shall be stopped;

else if cell j1 is Pcell

if UE i is configured with FDD + FR1 TDD UL CA

Ul scheduling shall be suspended for UE i on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots;

UE i shall be scheduled without the limitation of split TX power on Scell in Ul overlapping slots;

The split TX power update for UE i shall be stopped on Pcell and Scell;

Where:

-  i is UE index;

-  j0, j1 are cell index;

-  t is time the calculation relates to;

-  u(j0) is numerology of serving cell j0;

-  u(j1) is numerology of serving cell j1;

-  over power state refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10903\_replaced([11119931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuP_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-  efficiencyPerPRB refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10875\_replaced([11119847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  rdEffiThreshForUlScheSuspension is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13551\_replaced([11120047](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8XfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  splitTxPower, splitTxPowerAdjustmentStep, Pcmax, rdUePowerReserved (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10938\_replaced([11119997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdMinSplitTxPower (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10942\_replaced([11120009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10881\_replaced([11119868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  Checking whether UE requires more power than the split TX power refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10890\_replaced([11119904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  Adjusting split TX power refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10881\_replaced([11119868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

[Before PR683687]

-  convertToMw is to convert dBm to mW;

-  nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10873\_replaced([11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  TPC(i, j1) to be transmitted is the TPC command calculated by CLPC, but not transmitted yet for UE i on cell j1, PUSCH TPC command refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2642\_replaced([11119253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with OLPC, it's always 0;

[End PR683687]

-  minNumPrbsUl(j1) is the minimal allowed PRBs on cell j1:

If UL PTRS configured on cell j1

minNumPrbsUl(j1) = minAllowedPuschPrbUlPtrs; (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6845\_replaced([11197403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwHXIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the details)

else

minNumPrbsUl(j1) = minSupportedNumPrbsUl; (see 5G\_L2\_1136\_replaced([11183158](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27hiIfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-  Stopping UE transmission buffer split refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10516\_replaced([11122476](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

[CB006137-C]

-  maxPrbBasedOnSplitPower refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10883\_replaced([11119896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

[End CB006137-C]

[PR683687]

* power split mode is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10871\_replaced([11119486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* rdNumOfMaxPrbBasedOnSplitPwrCheck refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19298\_replaced([11120060](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqNjYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End PR683687]

Note:

* For a UE configured with FDD + FR1 TDD UL CA, there are only Ul overlapping slots on Scell.
* If split TX power is below the minimum split TX power on SCell and UE transmission buffer split is stopped to SCell and then SCell is deactivated due to inactivity timer expiration, PCell shall start to evaluate uplink buffer status (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9698\_replaced([11121066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqWGTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) only after a prohibit timer expired. The prohibit timer is specified by the R&D parameter rdProhibitBufEvalULFR1 [5G\_UP\_ALG\_12693\_replaced([11124165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqoaKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))]. The rationale for this prohibit timer is to avoid frequent ping-pong between SCell activation due to uplink buffer request --> split TX power is below the minimum split TX power on SCell --> SCell deactivation due to inactivity timer expiration --> SCell activation due to uplink buffer request again.

---

#### 3.6.4.0-15 UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA Resume Ul scheduling in overlapping slots on a cell where the scheduling is suspended due to too low split TX power (ID: 11119968)

**3.6.4.0-15.0-2**  (ID: `11119979`)

UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
11119979:
UL Power Control/Split for FR1 UL CA
For a UE configured with FR1 Ul CA which Ul scheduling is suspended in Ul overlapping slots on cell j1 due to too low split TX power according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):

if during rdNumForMinSplitTxPowerCheck consecutive evaluation periods (rdPeriodForOverPowerEva), [Before CB006137-C]the number of PRBs scheduled for any Ul transmission is always not above prbBasedOnSpecifiedSplitPower [CB006137-C] the required power based on scheduled PRBs (reqPowerBasedOnSchePRBs) is always not above specifiedSplitPower for any Ul transmission [End CB006137-C] on cell j0 in Ul overlapping slots or there is no any Ul scheduling on cell j0 in Ul overlapping slots

If cell j1 is Pcell

If the UE is configured with FDD + FR1 TDD UL CA

Initialize the split TX power on Pcell and Scell according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10879\_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

Ul scheduling shall be resumed for the UE on Pcell in Ul overlapping slots;

else if cell j1 is Scell which is active

If there are only Ul overlapping slots on Scell for the UE

Trigger UE transmission buffer split;

Where:

[Before CB006137-C]

-  prbBasedOnSpecifiedSplitPower is calculated according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10883\_replaced([11119896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with splitTxPower set to the below value:

If cell j0 is PCell:

{

temp = Pcmax(i, t) – rdUePowerReserved - rdMinSplitTxPower  - rdNumOfPwrAdjStepForResumeCheck \* ueSplitPowerAdjStep;

}

else if cell j0 is SCell

{

temp = Pcmax(i, t) – rdUePowerReserved - max{rdMinSplitTxPower, convertToMw[nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB(i, j1, t) + maxTpc]  \* minNumPrbsUl(j1)} - rdNumOfPwrAdjStepForResumeCheck \* ueSplitPowerAdjStep;

}

splitTxPower = max(temp, 0);

[CB006137-C]

-  reqPowerBasedOnSchePRBs is calculated for the UE configured with FR1 Ul inter-band CA as below:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6247.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]reqPowerBasedOnSchePRBs = convertToMw(temp0);

-  specifiedSplitPower is calculated as below:

If cell j0 is PCell:

{

temp1 = Pcmax(i, t) – rdUePowerReserved - rdMinSplitTxPower - rdNumOfPwrAdjStepForResumeCheck \* ueSplitPowerAdjStep;

}

else if cell j0 is SCell

{

temp1 = Pcmax(i, t) – rdUePowerReserved - max{rdMinSplitTxPower, convertToMw[nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB(i, j1, t) + maxTpc]  \* minNumPrbsUl(j1)} - rdNumOfPwrAdjStepForResumeCheck \* ueSplitPowerAdjStep;

}

specifiedSplitPower = max(temp1, 0);

[End CB006137-C]

-  Pcmax refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10879\_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  rdUePowerReserved is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10938\_replaced([11119997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  rdMinSplitTxPower is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10942\_replaced([11120009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  convertToMw is to convert dBm to mW;

-  nonPowerLimitedTxPowerPerPRB refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10873\_replaced([11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the unit is dBm;

[CB006137-C]

-  schePRBs(i, j0, t) is the granted PRBs for PUSCH for UE i on cell j0 in slot t;

-  [image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_6247.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10873\_replaced([11119621](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the unit is dBm;

-  MPR and DeltaMPR256QAM refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11120\_replaced([11130873](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krA0p_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

[End CB006137-C]

-  i is UE index;

-  t is time the calculation relates to;

-  maxTpc is 3 dB which is the maximum TPC value (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2642\_replaced([11119253](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqJR9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to prevent ping pong for CLPC; with OLPC, maxTpc is 0 dB;

-  minNumPrbsUl(j1) is the minimal allowed PRBs on cell j1, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  rdNumOfPwrAdjStepForResumeCheck is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11215\_replaced([11120042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8W_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

-  ueSplitPowerAdjStep is NIDD parameter on Pcell, and shall be converted to mW from dBm for the calculation.

-  rdNumForMinSplitTxPowerCheck is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10948\_replaced([11120035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8WfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-  rdPeriodForOverPowerEva is R&D parameter, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11993\_replaced([11120016](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqM8U_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-  Triggering UE Transmission Buffer Split refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10281\_replaced([11122608](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqf3TvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR683687]

Note: After UL scheduling is suspended on PCell in UL overlapping slots, in special cases, radio link quality becomes back to good on PCell but much power is still required on SCell and no free power for PCell, UL shceudling can't be resumed on PCell in UL overlapping slots. In burst data scenarios, this issue can be mitigated since split TX power will be reinitialized in case buffer split is restarted after buffer split stop. After UL scheduling is suspended on SCell in UL overlapping slots, only if there are free power for SCell, UL scheduling can be resumed on SCell in UL overlapping slots.

[End PR683687]

## 3.6.5 R&amp;D Parameters

### 3.6.5.0-1 R&amp;D Parameters rdMinInitSplitTxPower (ID: 11119985)

**3.6.5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11119989`)

R&D Parameters
Defines the minimum initial split TX power for a UE configured with FR1 Ul CA.

Value range: 0 ... 200

Default value: 50

Unit: mW

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10879\_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 3.6.5.0-2 R&amp;D Parameters rdMinSplitTxPowerAdjStep (ID: 11119990)

**3.6.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11119993`)

R&D Parameters
Defines the minimum split TX power adjustment step for a UE configured with FR1 Ul CA.

Value range: 0.01 ... 0.09

Default value: 0.05

Unit: mW

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 0.01

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10877\_replaced([11119861](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 3.6.5.0-3 R&amp;D Parameters rdUePowerReserved (ID: 11119997)

**3.6.5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11120000`)

R&D Parameters
Defines UE TX power reserved not for transmission in Ul overlapping slots to mitigate possible NACK issue on Scell due to the time difference to synchronize split TX power between Pcell and Scell for a UE configured with FR1 Ul CA.

Value range: 0 ... 100

Default value: 0

Unit: mW

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10879\_replaced([11119799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLHLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10881\_replaced([11119868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqLuNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10921\_replaced([11119951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10923\_replaced([11119968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqMVRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**3.6.5.0-12.0-1**  (ID: `11120056`)

R&D Parameters
Defines the number of consecutive PHR reports based on a reference format with PH reported as POWER\_HEADROOM\_63.  Non power limited TX power will be configured to a set value in case consecutive rdNumOfConsecVPHR63 PHR reports are received.

Value range: 10… 100

Default value: 20

Unit:

Online modifiable: No

StepSize: 10

### 3.6.5.0-13 R&amp;D Parameters rdNumOfMaxPrbBasedOnSplitPwrCheck (ID: 11120060)

**3.6.5.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `11120063`)

R&D Parameters
Defines the number of consecutive checks for checking whether according to the given split TX power, the maximum PRBs for Ul transmission with the required TX power is below the minimal allowed UL PRBs on PCell for an FR1 UL CA UE which is in power split mode.

Value range: 10 ... 100

Default value: 40

Unit:

Online modifiable: No
