### 3.6.5.0-22 R&amp;D Parameters rdMaxAccumulatedTpcPO (ID: 11120145)

**3.6.5.0-22.0-1**  (ID: `11120149`)

R&D Parameters
Short description: This parameter defines the maximum absolute value for accumulated TPC at gNB side for estimation of SRS and PUSCH power offset.

Rationale: As defined by 3GPP, accumulated TPC shall be used for UE to decide SRS and PUSCH transmission power but due to some misalignment between gNB and UE, the absolute value of accumulated TPC can be very large so this parameter is added to verify the impact.

Value range: 0...50

Default value: 0

Step size: 1

Unit: dB

Online modifiable: yes

Performance impact: minor.

Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10497\_replaced([11119432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Trigger for deletion: When the R&D parameter has been replaced by a NIDD parameter.

Owner: Carle Lengoumbi Tacail

---

### 3.6.5.0-23 R&amp;D Parameters rdEnablePowerReductionDlTestMode (ID: 11120154)

**3.6.5.0-23.0-3**  (ID: `11120166`)

R&D Parameters
rdEnablePowerReductionDlTestMode

Short description: This parameter activates the power reduction on PDSCH to avoid inter-cell interference.

Rationale: Activate the algorithm of power reduction on PDSCH. The power reduction applied when used MCS is lower compared to the MCS recommended by the downlink link adaptation. The purpose is to reduce inter cell interference. Because required SINR for the MCSs are approximately 1dB separated, the difference of MCSindex is a measure of required SINR difference in dB.

Value range: bitfield:

0b0 (disabled, corresponds to boolean FALSE),

0b1 (enabled for all transmissions except RACH, corresponds to boolean TRUE),

0b11 (enabled for all transmissions except RACH without SRB),

0b101 (enabled for all transmissions except RACH without VoNR),

0b111 (enabled for all transmissions except RACH without SRB and without VoNR)

0b1001 (enabled for all transmissions including RACH, corresponds to boolean TRUE),

0b1011 (enabled for all transmissions including RACH without SRB),

0b1101 (enabled for all transmissions including RACH without VoNR),

0b1111 (enabled for all transmissions including RACH without SRB and without VoNR)

Default value:

[Before 04200008] 0b1 (enabled for all transmission except RACH)

[04200008] 0b111 (enabled for all transmissions except RACH without SRB and without VoNR)

[End 04200008]

Unit: -

Online modifiable: No

Performance impact: major. Intercell interference will impact throughput and BLER.

Step Size: -

Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2572\_replaced([11118517](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Trigger for deletion: When the R&D parameter has been replaced by a NIDD parameter.

Owner: Jin Shi

---

### 3.6.5.0-29 R&amp;D Parameters rdEirpCellNbUeCs1Threshold_percent (ID: 11120217)

**3.6.5.0-29.0-1**  (ID: `11120221`)

R&D Parameters
Short description: This parameter defines the limit above which the EIRP enhancement are disabled in the DL Scheduler.

When the number of UEs in the CS1 list becomes higher than or equal to this percentage of the averaged maximum number of UEs allowed in the CS1 list, the EIRP enhanced token bucket shall be replaced by the legacy token bucket.

Value range: 0..100

Default value: 90

Unit: Percent

Online modifiable: Yes

Performance impact: Decrease CPU load

Step Size: 1

Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29993\_replaced([11119020](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqID0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Trigger for deletion: This R&D parameter can only be removed after it has been replaced by a NIDD parameter.

Owner: Pierre Jacolot

---

### 3.6.5.0-30 R&amp;D Parameters rdDisable256QamPowerBackoffRescaling (ID: 11120224)

**3.6.5.0-30.0-1**  (ID: `11120228`)

R&D Parameters
Short description: Disable the 256QAM power backoff rescaling based on number of allocated PRBs

Value range: 0: keep rescaling enabled, 1: disable rescaling for FR1, 2: disable for FR2, 3: disable for both FR1 & FR2  
Default value: 0  
Step size: -  
Unit: -  
Online modifiable: No  
Type: Control  
Performance Impact: None  
Used in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2560\_replaced([11118403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  
Trigger for deletion: Never  
Owner: Simon Goedecke/ André Gille

### 3.6.5.0-35 R&amp;D Parameters rdEirpEpicOlcDlPerCent (ID: 12533649)

**3.6.5.0-35.0-1**  (ID: `12533650`)

R&D Parameters
Short description: The R&D parameter defines the load thresholds for activation of L2 countermeasures when the L2 pool level signaling overload increases and for deactivation of L2 countermeasures when the load decreases. While the countermeasure is active, the gNB-DU for a TDD cell shall suspend FD-POLITE EPIC algorithm and when the countermeasure is deactivated the gNB-DU shall resume EPIC algoritm.

The 3 least significant decimal digits define the deactivation threshold, and the next 3 more significant decimal digits define the activation threshold. The threshold values are percentages of the L2 Celle level severity metric l2PsRtCellLevelSeverityMetric (See [11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_h-Ph0vvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). When the parameter is set to 0, the countermeasure is never activated due to high load.

Value range: 0…100 in every 3 digits tuple

Default value: 080060

Unit: %

Online modifiable: Yes

Performance impact: Reduces CPU load.

Step Size: 1 within every 3 digits tuple.

Used in: [12533550](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_cjQ8QRxREfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

Trigger for deletion: Never

Owner: Pierre Jacolot

---
